### [29] [The Stellar IMF and Dark Matter Halo of ESO0286: Constraints from Strong Lensing and Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26894)
*Han Wang,Jens Thomas,Mathias Lipka,Sherry H. Suyu,Aymeric Galan,Stefano de Nicola,Tian Li*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文聚焦于强引力透镜系统ESO0286-G022，通过结合强透镜和动力学建模研究暗物质晕和恒星初始质量函数，与用户Zotero画像中的核心主题（强引力透镜、暗物质、透镜）高度吻合。论文方法（Schwarzschild轨道叠加模型）和科学问题（区分恒星质量与暗物质）与用户兴趣直接相关。虽然作者不在核心作者列表中，但论文主题和方法匹配度极高，且用户明确要求优先考虑强透镜研究。

TL;DR: 该研究通过结合引力透镜和动力学建模，分析了ESO0286-G022椭圆星系的质量分布和恒星初始质量函数，发现其具有内在三轴性，排除了比Kroupa更重的IMF，展示了透镜与动力学结合在星系结构研究中的强大能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 椭圆星系内部质量结构对理解星系形成至关重要，但区分恒星质量与暗物质、确定恒星初始质量函数(IMF)仍然具有挑战性。本研究旨在通过结合引力透镜和动力学建模来解决这些问题。

Method: 使用哈勃太空望远镜高分辨率成像和VLT/MUSE积分场恒星运动学数据，构建轴对称和三轴Schwarzschild轨道叠加模型来重建ESO0286-G022星系的固有形状和质量分布。利用强引力透镜的爱因斯坦半径内的质量作为补充约束。

Result: 尽管是快速旋转体，ESO0286显示出明确的内在三轴性特征（沿主轴和副轴旋转），这是第二个被确认的此类案例。强透镜约束显著减少了外质量剖面的不确定性，表明只有具有强径向各向异性的模型与数据兼容。在内部区域，排除了比Kroupa更重的IMF，但允许向中心略微加重的IMF梯度。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了结合透镜和动力学建模在解析大质量星系详细内部结构方面的强大能力，结果与本地大质量早型星系的动力学研究一致，但与z>0.1透镜星系报告的较重IMF形成对比。

Abstract: The internal mass structure of elliptical galaxies offers critical insights into galaxy formation, yet disentangling stellar mass from dark matter and determining the stellar initial mass function (IMF) remains challenging. We present a detailed analysis of ESO0286-G022 ($z=0.0312$), a rare nearby strong-lens system with a fast-rotating elliptical galaxy, combining high-resolution Hubble Space Telescope (HST) imaging with VLT/MUSE integral-field stellar kinematics. We construct axisymmetric and triaxial Schwarzschild orbit-superposition models to reconstruct its intrinsic shape and mass distribution. Despite being a fast rotator, ESO0286 exhibits clear kinematic signatures of intrinsic triaxiality, characterized by rotation along both the major and minor axes, making it only the second such confirmed case. By incorporating the mass enclosed within the Einstein radius from strong lensing as a complementary constraint, we tightly anchor the total mass at large radii. This significantly reduces the uncertainty on the outer mass profile and orbital structure, demonstrating that only models with strong radial anisotropy beyond the IFU field of view are compatible with the data. In the inner regions, we robustly constrain an upper limit for the stellar mass around $r \sim 0.7$ kpc, ruling out an IMF more bottom-heavy than Kroupa, though a gentle gradient toward a slightly heavier central IMF is permitted. This aligns with recent dynamical studies of local massive early-type galaxies but contrasts with heavier IMFs reported for lenses at $z>0.1$. Our work demonstrates the power of combining lensing and dynamical modeling to resolve the detailed inner structure of massive galaxies.

Abstract Translation:
椭圆星系的内部质量结构为星系形成提供了关键见解，然而将恒星质量与暗物质分离并确定恒星初始质量函数（IMF）仍然具有挑战性。我们对ESO0286-G022（红移z=0.0312）进行了详细分析，这是一个罕见的近邻强透镜系统，包含一个快速旋转的椭圆星系。我们结合了哈勃空间望远镜的高分辨率成像与VLT/MUSE积分场恒星运动学数据。我们构建了轴对称和三轴Schwarzschild轨道叠加模型，以重建其固有形状和质量分布。尽管ESO0286是一个快速旋转体，但它表现出明显的固有三轴性运动学特征，即沿长轴和短轴均有旋转，这使其成为第二个被确认的此类案例。通过将强透镜约束的爱因斯坦半径内质量作为补充约束，我们严格锚定了大半径处的总质量。这显著减小了外部质量轮廓和轨道结构的不确定性，表明只有IFU视场外具有强径向各向异性的模型才与数据兼容。在内部区域，我们稳健地约束了约0.7千秒差距处恒星质量的上限，排除了比Kroupa IMF更底重的IMF，但允许向中心略重的IMF存在平缓梯度。这与近期对本地大质量早型星系的动力学研究一致，但与红移大于0.1的透镜星系中报告的更重IMF形成对比。我们的工作展示了结合透镜和动力学建模来解析大质量星系详细内部结构的能力。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，该研究展示了结合透镜和动力学建模在解析大质量星系详细内部结构方面的强大能力，结果与本地大质量早型星系的动力学研究一致，但与z>0.1透镜星系报告的较重IMF形成对比。

<small>Figure 1 : Photometric and kinematic constraints for the lens ESO0286. Left: HST/F814W image of the lens overlaid with the MUSE WFM FoV (white rectangle). The coordinate system ( \(x,y\) ) aligns with the galaxy’s photometric major and minor axes, respectively. The upper inset provides a zoom-in of the central region to highlight the dust structure, while dashed circles mark lensed images A and B (shown in the bottom insets). Right: Predicted \(M_{Ein}\) in units of \(10^{10}\penalty 10000\ M_{\odot}\) , derived from lensing and dynamical modeling. The more transparent green and orange regions show the probability density distribution of \(M_{Ein}^{lens}\) constrained only by image positions and flux ratios, while the less transparent regions correspond to models constrained by the extended images in the F814W and F336W bands. The vertical black line and gray shaded region indicate the inferred value, \(\overline{M_{Ein}^{lens}}=(8.85\pm 0.38)\times 10^{10}\penalty 10000\ M_{\odot}\) , based on the best-fit EPL-ESR and PIEMD-ESR models. The gray dashed line marks the lens mass derived by C18 .</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.26894v1/M_to_light_ratio.png)

图2：动力学建模中质量分布的设置，说明了恒星质光比梯度的实现。内半径 \(r_{i}\) 固定为0.1千秒差距。质光比 \(\Upsilon_{\ast,i}\) 和 \(\Upsilon_{\ast,f}\) 以及外半径 \(r_{f}\) 在动力学建模过程中允许变化。如阴影区域和虚线所示， \(r_{f}\) 的变化范围限制在 \(r_{f,min}=0.45\) 千秒差距和 \(r_{f,max}=1.2\) 千秒差距之间。

<small>Figure 2 : Setup for the mass distribution in the dynamical modeling, illustrating the implementation of the stellar mass-to-light ratio gradient. The inner radius \(r_{i}\) is fixed at 0.1 kpc. The mass-to-light ratios \(\Upsilon_{\ast,i}\) and \(\Upsilon_{\ast,f}\) , as well as the outer radius \(r_{f}\) , are allowed to vary during the dynamical modeling. As indicated by the shaded region and dotted lines, the variation range for \(r_{f}\) is restricted to between \(r_{f,min}=0.45\) kpc and \(r_{f,max}=1.2\) kpc.</small>

The color of each Model ID corresponds to the individual AIC envelopes plotted in Figs. 5 and 15 .</small>

### [30] [The velocity dispersion function of red galaxies in four Hubble Frontier Fields galaxy clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26869)
*G. Granata,L. Tortorelli,C. Grillo,P. Rosati,M. D'Addona,A. Mercurio,G. Angora,P. Bergamini,G. B. Caminha*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文聚焦于四个强引力透镜星系团（Hubble Frontier Fields）中红色成员星系的恒星运动学，核心是测量速度弥散度并校准基本平面关系。这与用户Zotero画像中的'velocity dispersion'、'lensing'、'strong lensing'高度匹配，且属于强引力透镜领域。论文使用MUSE积分场光谱和pPXF代码进行动力学分析，方法上与用户关注的星系动力学和运动学研究一致。虽然核心作者未出现在用户画像中，但主题和方法契合度极高，因此给予高分。

TL;DR: 该研究对哈勃前沿场计划中四个中红移强引力透镜星系团的红色成员星系进行了详细的恒星运动学分析，测量了213个星系的视线速度弥散度，校准了早型星系的基本平面关系，并研究了速度弥散度函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究中红移星系团中星系恒星运动学性质，特别是扩展到低速度弥散度区域，以更好地理解星系团中星系的动力学演化。

Method: 使用MORPHOFIT测量723个红色成员星系的结构参数，利用MUSE积分场光谱仪数据，基于pPXF代码系统测量视线速度弥散度，校准基本平面关系，并分析速度弥散度函数。

Result: 获得了213个速度弥散度测量值，校准了早型星系的基本平面关系，发现不同星系团间参数兼容，并检测到零点随红移演化的迹象。速度弥散度函数的Schechter函数拟合显示α斜率在0.55-1.60之间，σ*在2.18-2.47之间。

Conclusion: 该研究将星系团星系中心速度弥散度的系统研究扩展到低σ区域，为理解星系团中星系的动力学演化提供了重要数据。

Abstract: We present a detailed study of the stellar kinematic properties of red member galaxies in the cores of four strong lensing galaxy clusters at intermediate redshift included in the the Hubble Frontier Fields programme: Abell 2744 ($z=0.307$), Abell S1063 ($z=0.346$), MACS J0416.1$-$2403 ($z=0.397$), and MACS J1149.6$+$2223 ($z=0.542$). We focussed on a sample of 723 red cluster members in the four clusters and we measured their structural parameters using MORPHOFIT for all Hubble Frontier Fields bands. Taking advantage of deep (3.1h to 17h of exposure) integral-field spectroscopy from MUSE on the Very Large Telescope, we tested a pipeline based on the public spectral fitting code pPXF to systematically measure the line-of-sight stellar velocity dispersion $σ$ of cluster members with a spectral $S/N\geq 10$, with a statistical uncertainty consistently below 5%. The resulting catalogue contains 213 measured $σ$ values across the four clusters. We calibrated the Fundamental Plane relation in the rest-frame $r$ band for the early-type cluster members, selected from their colour and morphology, finding compatible parameters both across the clusters, and noting hints of zero-point evolution with redshift. Finally, we used the calibrated Fundamental Plane relations to assign a velocity dispersion value to all 723 red cluster members and studied the velocity dispersion function for each cluster, down to $\log σ\, \mathrm{[km \, s^{-1}] = 1.5}$. A Schechter-function fit of the velocity functions suggests compatible parameters: a positive $α$ slope with values in the range $0.55-1.60$, and $\logσ^*\, [\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}}]$ between $2.18$ and $2.47$. Compared to previous works, we extend the systematic study of the central velocity dispersion of cluster galaxies to lower-$σ$ regimes.

Abstract Translation:
我们详细研究了哈勃前沿场计划中四个中等红移强引力透镜星系团核心区域红色成员星系的恒星运动学性质：Abell 2744（z=0.307）、Abell S1063（z=0.346）、MACS J0416.1−2403（z=0.397）和MACS J1149.6+2223（z=0.542）。我们聚焦于四个星系团中723个红色成员星系的样本，并使用MORPHOFIT测量了它们在所有哈勃前沿场波段中的结构参数。利用甚大望远镜MUSE的深场（曝光时间3.1小时至17小时）积分场光谱，我们测试了一个基于公共光谱拟合代码pPXF的流程，以系统测量成员星系的视线方向恒星速度弥散度σ，要求光谱信噪比S/N≥10，统计不确定性始终低于5%。最终目录包含四个星系团中213个测量的σ值。我们校准了早型成员星系（根据颜色和形态选取）在静止系r波段的基本平面关系，发现各星系团参数兼容，并注意到零点随红移演化的迹象。最后，我们利用校准后的基本平面关系为所有723个红色成员星系分配速度弥散度值，并研究了每个星系团的速度弥散度函数，下限至logσ [km s^{-1}] = 1.5。速度函数的Schechter函数拟合表明参数兼容：α斜率正值，范围在0.55–1.60之间，logσ* [km s^{-1}]介于2.18和2.47之间。与先前工作相比，我们将星系团星系中心速度弥散度的系统研究扩展到了更低σ区域。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，该研究将星系团星系中心速度弥散度的系统研究扩展到低σ区域，为理解星系团中星系的动力学演化提供了重要数据。

The regions masked as potentially affected by issues with the subtraction of sky features and emission lines are shaded in grey. We note that the mask in the spectral region around \(4200\,{\AA }\) is intended to avoid the effects of the adaptive-optics laser emission used for some MUSE exposures of M0416, and as such was not adopted for the other three clusters. ### [31] [Spectroscopical Confirmation and Lens Modeling of a Complex Strong Lensing System Produced by a Close Galaxy Pair at $z_d=0.79$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12790)
*Zizhao He,Limeng Deng,Qihang Chen,Yiping Shu,Nan Li,Di Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文直接涉及强引力透镜系统的光谱确认和透镜建模，核心主题与用户的主要研究领域（强引力透镜，特别是星系-星系强透镜）高度吻合。论文研究了一对红移0.79的透镜星系和一个红移2.16的背景源，涉及暗物质分布、质量建模等用户兴趣点。虽然作者不在核心作者列表中，但主题和方法匹配度极高，且用户明确要求优先考虑强透镜论文。

TL;DR: 该论文确认了J0233-0205复杂强引力透镜系统，包含一对红移0.790的透镜星系和一个红移2.160的背景源，通过建模分析得到了透镜和源的结构参数、质量分布及暗物质比例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究J0233-0205复杂强引力透镜系统，旨在通过精确建模分析近距离星系对的质量分布和暗物质含量，同时利用源平面中的两个盘星系和点状源研究星系合并过程。

Method: 采用光谱学确认和引力透镜建模方法，结合恒星种群分析，对透镜系统进行联合建模，确定透镜和源的结构参数、质量分布及暗物质比例。

Result: 确认了透镜系统参数：透镜红移0.790，源红移2.160，爱因斯坦半径1.680角秒。透镜由两个椭圆星系组成，源包含两个盘星系和一个点状源。测得透镜对总恒星质量1.956×10^11太阳质量，总质量1.107×10^12太阳质量，暗物质比例82%。两个透镜星系的暗物质比例分别为57%和70%。

Conclusion: J0233-0205系统因其透镜对的小间距和较高红移，成为研究近距离星系对质量分布和暗物质含量的理想实验室，同时源平面的结构也为研究星系合并过程提供了宝贵机会。

Abstract: We report the spectroscopic confirmation and lens modeling of the complex strong-lens system J0233-0205, in which the deflector consists of a pair of galaxies at zd = 0.790 +/- 0.022, the background source lies at zs = 2.160 +/- 0.002, and the circularized Einstein radius is thetaE = 1.680 arcsec +/- 0.003 arcsec. Our lens modeling requires two lens components, namely two elliptical galaxies with Einstein radii of 0.669 arcsec +/- 0.002 arcsec and 0.735 arcsec +/- 0.002 arcsec, respectively, and a projected separation of 0.513 arcsec (about 3.832 kpc), as well as three source components: two disk galaxies separated by 0.4965 arcsec (about 3.712 kpc), plus a point-like component closely aligned with one of the disks. From a joint lensing and stellar-population analysis, we infer a total stellar mass within the critical curve of the lens pair of (1.956 +/- 0.418) x 10^11 solar masses and a total enclosed mass of (1.107 +/- 0.008) x 10^12 solar masses, corresponding to a projected dark-matter fraction of 82 +/- 4%. The stellar masses of the two lens galaxies are (8.548 +/- 2.128) x 10^10 solar masses and (1.525 +/- 0.295) x 10^11 solar masses, implying dark-matter fractions within the z-band effective radius of 57 +/- 11% and 70 +/- 6%, respectively. The small separation of the lens pair, together with its relatively high deflector redshift, makes J0233-0205 a potentially ideal laboratory for probing the mass distribution and dark-matter content of close galaxy pairs. In addition, the two disk galaxies and the associated point-like source make this system valuable for investigating the merger process in the source plane.

Abstract Translation:
我们报告了复杂强透镜系统J0233-0205的光谱确认和透镜建模，其中偏转体由一对红移为zd = 0.790 ± 0.022的星系组成，背景源位于zs = 2.160 ± 0.002，圆化爱因斯坦半径为θE = 1.680角秒 ± 0.003角秒。我们的透镜建模需要两个透镜分量，即两个椭圆星系，其爱因斯坦半径分别为0.669角秒 ± 0.002角秒和0.735角秒 ± 0.002角秒，投影间距为0.513角秒（约3.832千秒差距），以及三个源分量：两个盘状星系相距0.4965角秒（约3.712千秒差距），加上一个与其中一个盘紧密对齐的点状分量。通过联合透镜和星族分析，我们推断出透镜对临界曲线内的总恒星质量为(1.956 ± 0.418) × 10^11太阳质量，总包围质量为(1.107 ± 0.008) × 10^12太阳质量，对应的投影暗物质比例为82 ± 4%。两个透镜星系的恒星质量分别为(8.548 ± 2.128) × 10^10太阳质量和(1.525 ± 0.295) × 10^11太阳质量，意味着在z波段有效半径内的暗物质比例分别为57 ± 11%和70 ± 6%。透镜对的小间距及其相对较高的偏转体红移，使得J0233-0205成为研究近距离星系对质量分布和暗物质含量的潜在理想实验室。此外，两个盘状星系及相关联的点状源使该系统对于研究源平面中的合并过程具有重要价值。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，J0233-0205系统因其透镜对的小间距和较高红移，成为研究近距离星系对质量分布和暗物质含量的理想实验室，同时源平面的结构也为研究星系合并过程提供了宝贵机会。

### [32] [Varstrometry for Off-nucleus and Dual Subkiloparsec AGN (VODKA): Three Quadruply Lensed Quasars at Cosmic Noon in HST and JWST](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.16995)
*Mingrui Liu,Yu-Ching Chen,Nadia L. Zakamska,Xin Liu,Yue Shen,Xuheng Ding,Arran Gross,Hsiang-Chih Hwang,Yuzo Ishikawa,Kedar A. Phadke*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文直接研究强引力透镜系统（四重透镜类星体），使用HST和JWST进行高分辨率成像，聚焦于宇宙正午（z~1.5-3）的透镜星系，与用户画像中的核心主题（强引力透镜、JWST、宇宙正午、透镜星系）高度吻合。论文方法（SIE+Sersic建模）和科学问题（亚角秒分离透镜系统）与用户兴趣完全一致。虽然作者不在核心作者列表中，但主题和方法匹配度极高。

TL;DR: 利用哈勃和韦伯望远镜观测三个四重引力透镜类星体，测量了爱因斯坦半径，约束了透镜星系红移范围，发现这些透镜星系为早型星系，代表了亚角秒分离透镜中尚未充分探索的有趣象限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究亚角秒分离的四重引力透镜系统，这类系统在单星系强引力透镜群体中尚未得到充分探索，对于理解透镜星系的特性和未来高分辨率透镜巡天具有重要意义。

Method: 使用哈勃太空望远镜和詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜对三个四重透镜类星体进行成像观测，采用奇异等温椭球质量剖面和椭圆Sérsic剖面建模透镜星系，重建每个系统的几何构型并测量爱因斯坦半径。

Result: 测量得到三个系统的爱因斯坦半径分别为0.44"、0.58"和0.49"，约束透镜红移范围分别为0.5<z<1.2、1.0<z<1.5和0.4<z<0.9。最佳拟合光模型显示典型的de Vaucouleurs剖面（n_Sérsic~4），有效半径约1.5-3.5 kpc，分类为早型星系。

Conclusion: 这些透镜星系代表了单星系强引力透镜群体中尚未充分探索的亚角秒分离透镜的有趣象限，位于爱因斯坦半径分布的低端和透镜红移分布的高端，将成为未来高分辨率透镜巡天的重要目标。

Abstract: We present results from imaging observations of three quadruply lensed quasars by Hubble Space Telescope (HST) and James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) at redshifts $z = 2.550$, 2.975, and 1.500. We model our targets assuming a singular isothermal ellipsoid mass profile and an elliptical SÃ\c{opyright}rsic profile for the lensing galaxies, and reconstruct the geometric configuration of each system with measured Einstein radii of 0.44$'$, 0.58$'$, and 0.49$'$. While no spectroscopic measurements are available for the lenses, we constrain the redshift of each lens to $0.5 < z < 1.2$, $1.0 < z < 1.5$, and $0.4 < z < 0.9$. For all three lenses, the best-fit light model yield a typical de Vaucouleurs $n_{\rm S\acute{e}rsic} \sim 4$ profile and an effective radius $R_e$ around $\sim 1.5 - 3.5$ kpc. We accordingly classify the three lenses as early-type galaxies at an intermediate to high redshift, a common type for strong lensing galaxies. Compared to other known quadruple lenses, the lensing galaxies in this work are at the lower end of the distribution of Einstein radii and upper end of the distribution of the lens redshifts. They represent an interesting quadrant of subarcsecond-separation lenses in the population of single-galaxy strong lensing which have been largely unexplored yet and will be great targets of interest in upcoming high-resolution lensing surveys.

Abstract Translation:
我们展示了哈勃空间望远镜（HST）和詹姆斯·韦伯空间望远镜（JWST）对三个四重透镜类星体在红移 $z = 2.550$、2.975 和 1.500 处的成像观测结果。我们假设透镜星系具有奇异等温椭球质量分布和椭圆 Sérsic 轮廓，对目标进行建模，并重建了每个系统的几何构型，测得的爱因斯坦半径分别为 0.44$'$、0.58$'$ 和 0.49$'$。虽然无法获得透镜的光谱测量，但我们将其红移分别约束在 $0.5 < z < 1.2$、$1.0 < z < 1.5$ 和 $0.4 < z < 0.9$ 范围内。对于所有三个透镜，最佳拟合光模型均呈现出典型的 de Vaucouleurs $n_{\rm S\acute{e}rsic} \sim 4$ 轮廓，有效半径 $R_e$ 约为 $\sim 1.5 - 3.5$ kpc。据此，我们将这三个透镜归类为中等至高红移的早型星系，这是强透镜星系的常见类型。与其他已知的四重透镜相比，本工作中的透镜星系位于爱因斯坦半径分布的低端和透镜红移分布的高端。它们代表了单星系强透镜群体中一个有趣的亚角秒分离透镜象限，此前尚未得到充分探索，将成为未来高分辨率透镜巡天的重要目标。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，这些透镜星系代表了单星系强引力透镜群体中尚未充分探索的亚角秒分离透镜的有趣象限，位于爱因斯坦半径分布的低端和透镜红移分布的高端，将成为未来高分辨率透镜巡天的重要目标。

#### Figure 5
表 1：使用 Lenstronomy 对每个四重透镜类星体系统的透镜质量和光模型参数的最佳拟合值及其不确定性。从上到下：爱因斯坦半径 \(\theta_{E}\)、有效半径 \(R_{e}\)、Sérsic 指数 \(n_{S\acute{e}rsic}\)、光模型短轴与长轴比 \(q_{L}\) 和位置角 \(\phi_{L}\)、质量模型轴比 \(q_{M}\) 和位置角 \(\phi_{M}\)、透镜及每个透镜像的质心位置 \(\Delta x\) 和 \(\Delta y\)（定义为相对于图像中心的位移）。不确定性包括拟合不确定性（MCMC 后验分布的第 16 和第 84 百分位数）以及第 III.5 节中提到的运行间变异性。Lenstronomy 能够实现亚两位小数的拟合精度，参见例如 Shajib 等人 (2019)；Li 等人 (2023)；Schmidt 等人 (2023)；Adnan 等人 (2025)。

<small>Table 1: Best-fit values of parameters with uncertainties for the lens mass and light models of each quadruply lensed quasar system from Lenstronomy . From top to bottom: Einstein radius \(\theta_{E}\) , effective radius \(R_{e}\) , Sérsic index \(n_{S\acute{e}rsic}\) , light model minor-to-major axis ratio \(q_{L}\) and position angle \(\phi_{L}\) , mass model axis ratio \(q_{M}\) and position angle \(\phi_{M}\) , centroid positions of lens and each lensed image \(\Delta x\) and \(\Delta y\) (defined as displacements from image center). Uncertainties include both the fitting uncertainties (the 16th and 84th percentiles of the MCMC posterior distributions) and the run-to-run variability noted in Sec. III.5 . Lenstronomy is capable of achieving sub-two-decimal precision for its fits, see e.g. Shajib et al. ( 2019 ); Li et al. ( 2023 ); Schmidt et al. ( 2023 ); Adnan et al. ( 2025 ) .</small>

#### Figure 5

### [33] [New Dynamical Measurements from a Lensed Quasar Sample: Joint Analysis Constrains the Mass Profile Evolution of Lens Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.13578)
*Ziyu Guo,Yun Chen,Yiping Shu,Jiaze Gao,Hui Li,Zizhao He,Jun Wang*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文聚焦于强引力透镜系统（特别是透镜类星体）联合透镜几何与恒星运动学分析，研究早型星系质量密度剖面斜率随红移和表面质量密度的演化，与用户Zotero画像中'lens'、'lensing'、'strong gravitational lensing'等核心主题高度吻合。论文方法（联合透镜-动力学分析）和科学问题（星系结构演化）均属于用户主要兴趣领域。虽无核心作者匹配，但主题和方法匹配度极高，且属于用户明确优先的强引力透镜研究。

TL;DR: 该研究通过106个强引力透镜系统，结合透镜几何和恒星运动学分析，发现早型星系的质量密度剖面斜率随表面质量密度增加而变陡，随红移增加而变平缓。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究早型星系内部质量结构的演化趋势，验证先前在星系-星系透镜系统中观察到的结构趋势，并确立透镜类星体作为探测星系结构的有效工具。

Method: 使用106个具有背景类星体的星系尺度强引力透镜系统，从中选择24个高质量系统进行联合分析。采用迭代光谱拟合程序获得11个透镜星系的新单孔径恒星速度弥散度数据，通过蒙特卡洛嵌套采样在平坦ΛCDM框架下约束质量密度剖面斜率参数。

Result: 质量密度剖面斜率γ随表面质量密度增加而增加（γ_s > 0），随红移增加而减小（γ_z < 0）。具体参数约束为：γ_0 = 1.62^{+0.11}_{-0.12}，γ_z = -0.35^{+0.08}_{-0.09}，γ_s = 0.37^{+0.08}_{-0.07}（68%置信区间）。

Conclusion: 研究验证了早型星系结构演化趋势：在相同红移下，恒星核心更密集的星系具有更陡的质量剖面；在相同密度下，高红移星系的剖面更平缓。这确立了透镜类星体作为研究大质量早型星系结构的强大探针。

Abstract: We present a systematic study of the internal mass structure of early-type galaxies (ETGs) based on 106 galaxy-scale strong gravitational lenses with background quasars, all having spectroscopic redshifts. From this parent sample, we select 24 systems with high-quality ancillary data for joint analysis of strong lensing geometry and stellar kinematics. A key contribution is the derivation of new single-aperture stellar velocity dispersions for 11 lens galaxies via an iterative spectroscopic fitting procedure that mitigates quasar contamination, providing previously unavailable data. We model the total mass-density profile as a power law, $ρ\propto r^{-γ}$, and parameterise its logarithmic slope as $γ= γ_0 + γ_z \cdot z_l + γ_s \cdot \log \tildeΣ$, where $z_l$ is the lens redshift and $\tildeΣ$ the surface mass density. Within a flat $Λ$CDM framework and using DESI BAO measurements as a prior, we constrain the parameters via Monte Carlo nested sampling to $γ_0 = 1.62^{+0.11}_{-0.12}$, $γ_z = -0.35^{+0.08}_{-0.09}$, and $γ_s = 0.37^{+0.08}_{-0.07}$ ($68\%$ confidence intervals). Our results robustly demonstrate that $γ$ increases with surface mass density ($γ_s > 0$) and decreases with redshift ($γ_z < 0$). This implies that, at fixed redshift, galaxies with denser stellar cores have steeper mass profiles, while at fixed density, profiles become shallower at higher redshifts. By successfully applying the joint lensing--dynamics method to a substantial, independently acquired sample of lensed quasars, this work provides crucial validation of structural trends previously observed in galaxy--galaxy lensing systems, reinforcing the established evolutionary picture for massive ETGs and establishing lensed quasars as a potent probe of galaxy structure.

Abstract Translation:
我们基于106个具有背景类星体的星系尺度强引力透镜系统（所有系统均有光谱红移），对早型星系（ETGs）的内部质量结构进行了系统研究。从该母样本中，我们选取了24个具有高质量辅助数据的系统，用于强透镜几何与恒星运动学的联合分析。一项关键贡献是通过迭代光谱拟合程序（该程序可减轻类星体污染）推导出11个透镜星系的新单孔径恒星速度弥散，提供了此前无法获取的数据。我们将总质量密度轮廓建模为幂律形式 $\rho\propto r^{-\gamma}$，并将其对数斜率参数化为 $\gamma= \gamma_0 + \gamma_z \cdot z_l + \gamma_s \cdot \log \tilde\Sigma$，其中 $z_l$ 是透镜红移，$\tilde\Sigma$ 是表面质量密度。在平坦 $\Lambda$CDM 框架内，并以 DESI BAO 测量作为先验，我们通过蒙特卡洛嵌套采样将参数约束为 $\gamma_0 = 1.62^{+0.11}_{-0.12}$，$\gamma_z = -0.35^{+0.08}_{-0.09}$，$\gamma_s = 0.37^{+0.08}_{-0.07}$（$68\%$ 置信区间）。我们的结果有力地表明，$\gamma$ 随表面质量密度增加而增大（$\gamma_s > 0$），随红移增加而减小（$\gamma_z < 0$）。这意味着，在固定红移下，恒星核心更密集的星系具有更陡的质量轮廓；而在固定密度下，高红移星系的轮廓变得更平缓。通过成功地将透镜-动力学联合方法应用于一个规模可观、独立获取的透镜类星体样本，本研究为先前在星系-星系透镜系统中观测到的结构趋势提供了关键验证，强化了已建立的大质量早型星系演化图景，并将透镜类星体确立为研究星系结构的有效探针。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，研究验证了早型星系结构演化趋势：在相同红移下，恒星核心更密集的星系具有更陡的质量剖面；在相同密度下，高红移星系的剖面更平缓。这确立了透镜类星体作为研究大质量早型星系结构的强大探针。

### [34] [MeerKAT discovery of a high-redshift strongly-lensed hydroxyl gigamaser](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.13396)
*Thato E. Manamela,Roger P. Deane,Tariq Blecher,Ian Heywood,Athol J. Kemball,Danail Obreschkow*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文直接涉及强引力透镜系统中的羟基巨脉泽（OHM）探测，红移z=1.027，属于高红移星系气体研究，与用户对强引力透镜、高红移星系气体、分子气体等核心兴趣高度吻合。论文主题聚焦于引力透镜放大效应下的分子气体发射线，方法上利用MeerKAT射电观测，结果揭示了透镜星系中的复杂气体动力学和HI吸收线，完全符合用户对高红移星系动力学和多相气体的优先关注。虽然作者不在核心作者列表中，但论文的科学问题和数据直接对应用户兴趣，且无任何负向关键词。

TL;DR: 在红移z=1.027的引力透镜系统HATLAS J142935.3-002836中首次探测到最遥远的羟基巨脉泽(OHM)，其表观光度创历史新高，同时在同一数据集中发现了新的HI吸收线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 羟基巨脉泽(OHMs)在低红移下已被证明能追踪星系合并、遮蔽星暴、高分子气体密度和候选双超大质量黑洞系统。为探索这些天体在更大宇宙回溯时间的特性，需要利用新型高灵敏度射电设施如MeerKAT来扩展OHM探测的前沿。

Method: 利用MeerKAT射电望远镜对引力透镜系统HATLAS J142935.3-002836进行4.7小时宽频带观测，在红移z=1.027处探测羟基巨脉泽发射线，并分析其光谱特征和光度特性。

Result: 成功探测到迄今为止最遥远的OHM源，其混合1667和1665 MHz发射线呈现复杂光谱轮廓，谱线宽度从<8 km/s到~300 km/s不等。未校正放大率的积分光度log(L_OH/L_⊙)=5.51±0.67，成为目前已知表观光度最高的OHM。在同一数据集中还发现了新的HI吸收线，信噪比超过150。

Conclusion: 这项发现证明了MeerKAT和未来平方公里阵列中频阵列在探索高红移羟基巨脉泽宇宙方面的巨大潜力，为研究早期宇宙中的星系合并、星暴活动和超大质量黑洞系统提供了新的观测手段。

Abstract: At low redshifts, hydroxyl megamasers (OHMs) have been shown to trace galaxy mergers, obscured starbursts, high molecular gas densities, and candidate dual supermassive black hole systems. Given this astrophysical utility, exploring these sources at larger cosmological look-back times is therefore of key interest. While previous OHM surveys have been limited to redshifts of $z \lesssim 0.25$, the ability to expand the OHM frontier is significantly enhanced with new high-sensitivity radio facilities such as MeerKAT. In this Letter, we report the discovery of an OHM in the gravitational lens system HATLAS J142935.3-002836 at $z = 1.027$, the most distant OHM source yet detected. The spectrum has blended 1667 and 1665 MHz emission and exhibits a highly complex profile, with spectral components ranging in widths of $<8$ km s$^{-1}$ to $\sim300$ km s$^{-1}$. The integrated (magnification uncorrected) luminosity of log($L_{\rm OH} / L_{\odot}$) = 5.51 $\pm$ 0.67 makes this the most apparently luminous OHM known to date. In the same wide-band dataset, we have also detected a previously unknown ${\rm H I}$ absorption line. The signal-to-noise ratio of over 150 with just a 4.7 h observation highlights the potential that MeerKAT and the future Square Kilometre Array mid-frequency array offer to explore the high-redshift OHM universe.

Abstract Translation:
在低红移处，羟基巨脉泽已被证明可以示踪星系合并、遮蔽星暴、高分子气体密度以及候选双超大质量黑洞系统。鉴于这种天体物理学效用，探索这些源在更大宇宙学回溯时间下的情况因此具有关键意义。虽然之前的羟基巨脉泽巡天仅限于红移 $z \lesssim 0.25$，但利用诸如MeerKAT等新型高灵敏度射电设施，拓展羟基巨脉泽前沿的能力得到了显著增强。在本快报中，我们报告在引力透镜系统HATLAS J142935.3-002836中于 $z = 1.027$ 处发现了一个羟基巨脉泽，这是迄今探测到的最遥远的羟基巨脉泽源。其光谱具有混合的1667和1665 MHz发射，并展现出高度复杂的轮廓，光谱成分的宽度范围从 $<8$ km s$^{-1}$ 到 $\sim300$ km s$^{-1}$。积分（未修正放大效应）光度为 log($L_{\rm OH} / L_{\odot}$) = 5.51 $\pm$ 0.67，使其成为迄今已知的表观最亮的羟基巨脉泽。在同一宽频数据集中，我们还探测到一条先前未知的 ${\rm H I}$ 吸收线。仅用4.7小时观测就获得了超过150的信噪比，突显了MeerKAT以及未来的平方公里阵列中频阵列在探索高红移羟基巨脉泽宇宙方面的潜力。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，这项发现证明了MeerKAT和未来平方公里阵列中频阵列在探索高红移羟基巨脉泽宇宙方面的巨大潜力，为研究早期宇宙中的星系合并、星暴活动和超大质量黑洞系统提供了新的观测手段。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/figs/fig_datamodelresid.png)

图2：透镜系统HATLAS1429-0028的观测羟基巨脉泽发射光谱。16.6 kHz分辨率光谱显示出一个复杂的发射轮廓，具有非常高的积分信噪比。贝叶斯模型选择倾向于5-高斯成分模型（蓝色曲线）。残差（数据 - 模型）显示在底部面板中。

<small>Figure 2: Observed OHM emission spectrum of the lensed system, HATLAS1429-0028. The 16.6 kHz resolution spectrum shows a complex emission profile with remarkably high integrated SNR. #### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/x1.png)

图3：以Calanog等人（2014）使用凯克K s自适应光学成像数据进行的透镜建模中识别的三个近红外成分为中心的假设羟基巨脉泽成分的放大率与半径之间的关系。我们将圆对称高斯成分置于这三个位置，并计算每个成分的放大率。虚线水平线显示了源自Calanog等人（2014）的总近红外放大率，该值与Messias等人（2014）推导的值一致。完整讨论见正文。

<small>Figure 3: The relationship between magnification and radius for hypothetical OH maser components centred on the three NIR components identified in the Calanog et al. ( 2014 ) lens modelling with Keck K s Adaptive-Optics imaging data. We centre circularly symmetric Gaussian components on these three locations and compute the magnifications for each. The dashed horizontal line shows the total NIR magnification derived from Calanog et al. ( 2014 ) , which is consistent with the value derived in Messias et al. ( 2014 ) . See the main text for the full discussion.</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/figs/fig2_loh-lfir.png)

图4：远红外与羟基光度相关性（数据点来自Glowacki等人，2022；Jarvis等人，2024；Zhang等人，2024）。三个由MeerKAT发现的羟基巨脉泽（蓝色、绿色、红色）分别将此前保持了近二十年的羟基巨脉泽红移记录翻倍、增至三倍和四倍。本工作中报告的MIGHTEE（绿色）和最高红移源（红色）均受到强引力透镜效应，这表明非定向羟基巨脉泽搜索可作为识别透镜系统的一种方法（参见Button和Deane，2024）。

<small>Figure 4: Far-infrared and OH luminosity correlation (data points from Glowacki et al. , 2022 ; Jarvis et al. , 2024 ; Zhang et al. , 2024 ) . The three MeerKAT-discovered OHMs (blue, green, red) have doubled, tripled, and quadrupled the previous OHM redshift record held for almost two decades, respectively. The MIGHTEE (green) and highest redshift source (red) reported in this work are both strongly lensed, suggesting untargeted OHM searches as a way of identifying lensed systems (see, Button and Deane, 2024 ) .</small>

#### Figure 5
表1：五成分高斯羟基谱线模型的中值后验参数，其中每个成分的平均值、半高全宽、积分流量、积分表观光度以及1667与1665线比率分别由 \(\nu_{\text{obs}}\) 、 \(\Delta v_{\text{rest}}\) 、 \(F_{\text{line}}\) 、 log \((\mu L_{\text{OH}})\) 和 \(R^{1667}_{1665}\) 表示。

<small>Table 1: Median posterior parameters of the five-component Gaussian OH spectral line model, where each component’s mean, FWHM, integrated flux, integrated apparent luminosity, and 1667-to-1665 line ratio is denoted by \(\nu_{\text{obs}}\) , \(\Delta v_{\text{rest}}\) , \(F_{\text{line}}\) , log \((\mu L_{\text{OH}})\) , and \(R^{1667}_{1665}\) , respectively.</small>

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/figs/HIabs_spectrum.png)

图5：中性氢吸收光谱（浅蓝色），其中心位于系统红移（ \(V=0\) km s -1 ）处，该红移由光学和低J CO谱线推导得出。羟基发射光谱（深蓝色），为比较而缩放0.04倍，显示为蓝移，可能指示一个分子外流。

<small>Figure 5: The H i absorption spectrum (light blue), which is centred on the systemic redshift ( \(V=0\) km s -1 ), as derived from optical and low-J CO lines. The OH emission spectrum (dark blue), scaled by 0.04 for comparison, appears blue-shifted, potentially indicating a molecular outflow.</small>

### [35] [Multi-band Reconstruction of Sixteen Gravitational Lens Systems using PISCO data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.15585)
*Huimin Qu,Daniel J. Ballard,Geraint F. Lewis,Karl Glazebrook,Antony Stark,Sarah M. Sweet,Colin Jacobs,Kim-Vy Tran,Brian Stalder,Tania M. Barone,Tucker Jones,Keerthi Vasan G. C.,Thomas E. Collett,Glenn G. Kacprzak,Dorota Bayer*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文直接聚焦于星系-星系尺度强引力透镜的多波段建模，与用户的核心研究领域高度吻合。论文开发了可扩展的贝叶斯建模流程，并应用于16个透镜候选体，成功恢复15个，包括首个双曲脐点强透镜候选体。方法上采用同步多波段建模，利用颜色信息联合约束透镜质量，与用户对透镜建模、高红移星系动力学等兴趣高度一致。虽然作者列表中无用户核心作者，但主题和方法匹配度极高，且论文涉及地面数据（PISCO）与下一代巡天（Euclid、LSST）的衔接，对用户未来研究有重要参考价值。

TL;DR: 开发了可扩展的多波段贝叶斯透镜建模流程，应用于16个PISCO透镜候选体，成功恢复15个，包括首个双曲脐点星系尺度强透镜候选体，证明地面数据多波段建模能有效约束质量和源形态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代巡天（如Euclid、LSST、CSST）预计将发现约10^5个星系-星系尺度强引力透镜，需要开发可扩展且稳健的透镜建模方法，以便在获得高分辨率后续观测前，能有效可靠地从广域巡天数据中学习。

Method: 设计了基于Lenstronomy的可扩展贝叶斯建模流程，应用于16个PISCO透镜候选体。采用同步多波段建模方法：在四个波段（z、i、r、g）中使用共同的质量分布，但每个波段独立的光度分布，利用颜色信息联合约束透镜质量。

Result: 16个PISCO透镜候选体中成功恢复15个，包括首个报告的双曲脐点星系尺度强透镜候选体DESJ0533-2536。多波段分析相比单波段分析减少了不确定性，评估了PISCO类数据的分辨率和视宁度下可可靠约束的模型复杂度。

Conclusion: 可扩展的地面数据多波段透镜建模能够提取质量和源形态的有意义约束，为最大化即将到来的巡天中大量样本的科学回报提供了实用途径。

Abstract: Next-generation surveys such as the Euclid survey, the Legacy Survey of Space and Time (LSST), and the China Space Station Telescope (CSST) survey are expected to discover ~10^5 galaxy-galaxy scale strong gravitational lenses. This motivates the development of scalable and robust lens modeling approaches that can efficiently and reliably learn from wide-field survey datasets before high-resolution follow-up. We design a scalable, Bayesian, Lenstronomy-based pipeline and apply it to a sample of sixteen lens candidates observed with the Parallel Imager for Southern Cosmology Observations (PISCO) on the Magellan telescope. PISCO provides four-band imaging (z, i, r, g) with colours, depth and seeing conditions comparable to LSST. To fully exploit the constraining power of this dataset, our pipeline performs simultaneous multi-band modeling, using a common mass profile across all four bands while allowing independent light profiles in each. This approach leverages color information to provide joint constraints on the lens mass and yields reduced uncertainties compared to single-band analyses. Fifteen out of sixteen PISCO lens candidates are successfully recovered with interpretable lensing configurations, including DESJ0533-2536, the first reported hyperbolic-umbilic galaxy-galaxy scale strong lensing candidate. We further assess how much model complexity can be reliably constrained given the resolution and seeing of PISCO-like data. Overall, our results demonstrate that scalable, multi-band lens modeling of ground-based data can extract meaningful constraints on mass and source morphology, providing a practical pathway to maximize the scientific return from large samples in upcoming surveys.

Abstract Translation:
下一代巡天项目，如欧几里得巡天、时空遗产巡天（LSST）和中国空间站望远镜（CSST）巡天，预计将发现约10^5个星系-星系尺度强引力透镜。这促使开发可扩展且稳健的透镜建模方法，以便在高分辨率后续观测之前，能够高效可靠地从广域巡天数据集中学习。我们设计了一个可扩展的、基于贝叶斯和Lenstronomy的流水线，并将其应用于一个由16个透镜候选体组成的样本，这些候选体是用麦哲伦望远镜上的南天天体观测并行成像仪（PISCO）观测的。PISCO提供四个波段（z、i、r、g）的成像，其颜色、深度和视宁度条件与LSST相当。为了充分利用该数据集的约束能力，我们的流水线执行同步多波段建模，在所有四个波段中使用共同的质量分布，同时允许每个波段有独立的光分布。这种方法利用颜色信息对透镜质量提供联合约束，与单波段分析相比，减少了不确定性。16个PISCO透镜候选体中有15个成功恢复，并具有可解释的透镜构型，包括DESJ0533-2536，这是首个报道的双曲脐点星系-星系尺度强透镜候选体。我们进一步评估了在PISCO类数据的分辨率和视宁度下，能够可靠约束的模型复杂度。总体而言，我们的结果表明，对地面数据进行可扩展的多波段透镜建模能够提取质量和源形态的有意义约束，为最大化即将到来的巡天中大量样本的科学回报提供了实用途径。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，可扩展的地面数据多波段透镜建模能够提取质量和源形态的有意义约束，为最大化即将到来的巡天中大量样本的科学回报提供了实用途径。

<small>Figure 1 : Dark Energy Survey (DES) data of the 16 lens candidates identified using a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) (Jacobs et al. , 2019 , 2019 ) . In most cases, the central lens galaxies appear red or orange, consistent with their quenched nature, while the lensed background sources are blue, reflecting ongoing star formation.</small>

表1：每个系统采用的模型配置总结。质量分布在所有波段中一致，而偏转体和源的光分布可以在各波段共享相同模型，或采用不同组件，每个波段有独立参数。如果存在卫星组件，则按表中所述进行建模。

If present, satellite components are modeled as stated in the table.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/x2.png)

图2：所有16个透镜系统的三面板概览。每个面板显示按候选体ID排列的2×8张图像。从上到下依次为：（1）观测数据，（2）最佳拟合透镜模型重建，以及（3）源平面重建。每张图像通过将\(z\)、\(i\)、\(r\)和\(g\)波段配准到\(r\)波段帧后叠加而成，左上角有标签。重建结果代表MCMC链中最高似然度的透镜构型，基于表现最佳的透镜模型（表2中灰色高亮行），红色临界曲线叠加在透镜平面，白色焦散曲线显示在源平面。内临界曲线（对应源平面的外焦散）的存在（或缺失）反映了质量密度分布的斜率，仅当对数斜率比等温（\(\gamma\)）更浅时出现。

<small>Figure 2 : Three-panel overview of all 16 lens systems. Each panel shows 2×8 images arranged by candidate ID. From top to bottom: (1) observed data, (2) best-fit lens model reconstructions, and (3) source-plane reconstructions. Each image is created by stacking the \(z\) , \(i\) , \(r\) , and \(g\) bands after registering them to the \(r\) -band frame, with a label in the top-left corner. The reconstructions represent the highest likelihood lens configurations in the MCMC chain, under the best-performing lens models (grey-highlighted row in Table 2 ), with red critical curves overlaid in the lens plane and white caustic curves shown in the source plane. The presence (or absence) of an inner critical curve (corresponding to the outer caustic in the source plane) reflects the slope of the mass density profile, appearing only when the logarithmic slope is shallower than isothermal ( \(\gamma</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/x50.png)

图3：系统DESJ2032-5658的多波段引力透镜重建示例。每一行对应不同的滤光片——从上到下依次为\(z\)、\(i\)、\(r\)和\(g\)——最后一行是基于波段归一化数据的合成彩色图像。各列显示：（i）观测数据；（ii）带有红色临界曲线的重建模型图像；（iii）归一化残差，定义为\(({model}-{data})/\sigma\)；（iv）带有白色焦散曲线的源平面重建；以及（v）图像平面中的透镜化源光，也带有红色临界曲线。在每个波段内，数据、模型和透镜化源图像使用一致的颜色标尺，揭示了透镜化源在更蓝波段中日益突出的现象。临界曲线由共享质量模型计算，并利用相对于\(r\)波段推断的相对偏移和旋转，变换到每个波段的帧中。对于合成行，所有图像都配准到\(r\)波段帧，残差在各波段间取平均。

<small>Figure 3 : Example of multi–band gravitational lens reconstruction for the system DESJ2032-5658. Each row corresponds to a different filter— \(z\) , \(i\) , \(r\) , and \(g\) from top to bottom—followed by a composite color image based on band-normalized data in the final row. The columns display: (i) observed data; (ii) reconstructed model image with red critical curves; (iii) normalized residuals, defined as \(({model}-{data})/\sigma\) ; (iv) source-plane reconstruction with white caustics; and (v) lensed source light in the image plane, also with red critical curves. Within each band, a consistent color scale is used for the data, model, and lensed source image, revealing the increasing prominence of the lensed source in bluer bands. Critical curves, computed from a shared mass model, are transformed into each band’s frame using the inferred relative shifts and rotations with respect to the r-band. For the composite row, all images are aligned to the r-band frame, and the residuals are averaged across bands.</small>

Values with uncertainties are either directly obtained or derived from the posterior distributions, with 68% credible intervals. Spectroscopic redshifts are drawn from the ASTRO 3D Galaxy Evolution with Lenses (AGEL) survey ( tranAGELSurveyStrong2023 ; baroneAGELSurveyData2025 ) . The row highlighted in grey corresponds to the lens model shown in Figure 2 .</small>

The number of decimal places for each parameter is chosen to reflect the precision suggested by the 68% credible interval of its posterior distribution. For model with satellite mass (constrianed position), the SIS component’s Einstein radius \(\theta_{E}^{\text{\tiny SIS}}\) has a posterior distribution that peaks near zero, and we report the 84% upper limit, derived from an exponential fit to the posterior.</small>

<small>Table 4 : Same as Table 3 , but for the DESJ2125 system. The inclusion of a SIS component significantly improves the fit, with BIC differences of approximately 52 and 76 for Model 2 and Model 3, respectively, relative to Model 1. The inferred external shear correspondingly decreases when the satellite is included, indicating that part of the perturbation previously absorbed by the shear is now attributed to the satellite mass.</small>

### [36] [Detailed lens modeling and kinematics of the submillimeter galaxy G09v1.97. An analysis of CO, H2O, H2O+, and dust continuum emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.14685)
*K. Kade,C. Yang,M. Yttergren,K. K. Knudsen,S. König,A. Amvrosiadis,S. Dye,J. Nightingale,L. Zhang,Z. Zhang,A. Cooray,P. Cox,R. Gavazzi,E. Ibar,M. J. Michałowski,P. van der Werf,R. Xue*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文直接聚焦于强引力透镜星系G09v1.97的详细透镜建模和运动学分析，核心主题与用户的主要研究领域（星系-星系强引力透镜）高度吻合。论文使用PyAutoLens进行源平面重建，并利用3DBarolo进行动力学建模，方法上完全匹配用户兴趣。作者列表中包含K. Kade、S. König、K. K. Knudsen等用户Zotero库中的核心作者，作者匹配度极高。论文研究高红移星暴星系的星际介质、尘埃连续谱和分子气体，与用户对高红移星系动力学、多相气体等优先主题高度一致。无负面关键词。

TL;DR: 对高红移引力透镜星系G09v1.97的多波段观测和运动学建模表明，该星系呈现旋转盘结构而非多源系统，具有高速恒星形成率和短气体耗尽时间，暗示其近期经历了相互作用触发的星暴活动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高红移强烈星暴星系的形成机制，特别是通过引力透镜效应详细观测极端星暴星系的星际介质和环境，以探索相互作用和合并是否是其触发机制。

Method: 使用高角分辨率观测尘埃连续谱、CO(6-5)、H2O(211-202)和H2O+(202-111)发射线；利用PyAutoLens创建去放大源平面CO(6-5)发射线立方体；使用3DBarolo进行运动学建模；分析源平面连续谱和分子线发射特性。

Result: CO(6-5)和H2O(211-202)发射区域在源平面匹配良好，但尘埃连续谱发射更紧凑；透镜建模表明仅需单个源而非多源系统；G09v1.97呈现旋转盘结构(Vmax/σ=2.8±0.4)，存在非圆周运动迹象（可能与双锥外流、潮汐尾或背景星系相关）；计算得到高恒星形成率和短气体耗尽时间。

Conclusion: G09v1.97近期经历了相互作用触发了强烈恒星形成，目前正在向盘状结构演化，其高恒星形成率和短气体耗尽时间支持这一演化阶段。

Abstract: The formation mechanisms of intensely starbursting galaxies at high redshift remain unknown. One possible mechanism for triggering these starbursts is mergers and interactions, but detecting these at high redshift remains a challenge. Observations of high-redshift gravitationally lensed galaxies enable studies of the interstellar medium and environment of these extreme starbursts in detail. We used high angular resolution observations of dust continuum, CO(6-5), H2O(211-202), and H2O+(202-111) emission to constrain the ongoing processes in the z = 3.63 gravitationally lensed submillimeter galaxy H-ATLAS J083051.0+013224 (G09v1.97). We used PyAutoLens to create a de-magnified source plane CO(6-5) emission line cube and performed kinematic modeling using 3DBarolo. Additionally, we investigated the properties of the continuum and molecular line emission in the source plane. We find that the regions of CO(6-5) and H2O(211-202) emission match closely in the source plane but that the dust continuum emission is more compact. We find that our lens modeling results do not require more than one source, contrary to what has been found in previous studies. Instead, we find that G09v1.97 resembles a rotating disk with Vmax/sigma = 2.8 +/- 0.4 with evidence for residual emission indicative of non-circular motions such as outflows, tidal tails, or an additional background galaxy. We suggest that the origin of the non-circular motions may be associated with a bi-conical outflow, a tidal tail from an interaction, or indicate the possible presence of an additional galaxy. We calculate the dynamical mass, gas mass, star-formation rate, and depletion time for G09v1.97 and find a high star-formation rate and low gas depletion time. In combination, this suggests that G09v1.97 has recently undergone an interaction, triggering intense star formation, and is in the process of settling into a disk.

Abstract Translation:
高红移剧烈星暴星系的形成机制仍然未知。触发这些星暴的一种可能机制是合并与相互作用，但在高红移处探测这些过程仍具挑战。对高红移引力透镜星系的观测能够详细研究这些极端星暴的星际介质和环境。我们利用尘埃连续谱、CO(6-5)、H2O(211-202)和H2O+(202-111)发射的高角分辨率观测，来约束红移z = 3.63的引力透镜亚毫米星系H-ATLAS J083051.0+013224 (G09v1.97)中的持续过程。我们使用PyAutoLens创建了去放大源平面的CO(6-5)发射线数据立方体，并利用3DBarolo进行了运动学建模。此外，我们研究了源平面中连续谱和分子线发射的性质。我们发现CO(6-5)和H2O(211-202)发射区域在源平面中紧密匹配，但尘埃连续谱发射更为致密。我们发现透镜建模结果不需要多于一个源，这与先前研究的结果相反。相反，我们发现G09v1.97类似于一个旋转盘，其Vmax/sigma = 2.8 +/- 0.4，并存在指示非圆周运动（如外流、潮汐尾或额外背景星系）的残余发射证据。我们认为非圆周运动的起源可能与双锥外流、相互作用产生的潮汐尾有关，或表明可能存在另一个星系。我们计算了G09v1.97的动力学质量、气体质量、恒星形成率和耗尽时间，发现其恒星形成率高而气体耗尽时间短。综合来看，这表明G09v1.97近期经历了一次相互作用，触发了强烈的恒星形成，并正在向盘状结构演化。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有总结：G09v1.97近期经历了相互作用触发了强烈恒星形成，目前正在向盘状结构演化，其高恒星形成率和短气体耗尽时间支持这一演化阶段。

Key Figures:



</details>


### [37] [Mirror images of lensed star clusters with mismatched spectral energy distributions: A possible signature of top-heavy stellar initial mass functions and extreme stars in high-redshift star clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.14385)
*Erik Zackrisson,Jose M. Diego,Jose M. Palencia,Francesco Gabrielli,Armin Nabizadeh,Angela Adamo,Guglielmo Costa*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文直接聚焦于强引力透镜效应下的星团镜像图像，并利用JWST观测研究高红移星团中的极端恒星群体（如超大质量恒星和top-heavy IMF），这与用户的核心兴趣——强引力透镜、高红移星系动力学及JWST观测高度吻合。论文主题、方法（微引力透镜建模）及科学目标（探测早期宇宙恒星形成）均与用户画像中的关键词（lens、lensed、jwst、initial mass function）及核心作者群（如Tommaso Treu等）的研究方向紧密相关。尽管涉及恒星物理，但作为强透镜研究的直接延伸，且服务于高红移天体物理这一优先领域，因此给予高分。

TL;DR: 通过JWST观测发现，强引力透镜下的星团镜像图像可能因微引力透镜效应而呈现不同的光谱能量分布，这为探测早期宇宙中的超大质量恒星提供了新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上认为强引力透镜产生的星团镜像图像应具有相同的光谱能量分布，但微引力透镜效应可能破坏这一假设，这为研究早期宇宙恒星形成提供了新视角。

Method: 分析微引力透镜对星团镜像图像光谱能量分布的影响条件，确定JWST可观测到SED差异的星团质量和年龄范围，并探讨不同恒星初始质量函数的影响。

Result: JWST观测中可检测到SED差异的星团质量需小于10^5太阳质量且年龄小于500万年；若恒星初始质量函数偏向大质量恒星（如第三星族），镜像图像SED差异会更显著。

Conclusion: 强引力透镜星团镜像图像的光谱能量分布差异可作为探测早期宇宙中超大质量恒星和极端恒星群体的有效工具，为理解早期宇宙恒星形成提供新途径。

Abstract: Strongly lensed star clusters have recently been detected up to redshift $z\approx 10$ in galaxy cluster fields using the James Webb Space Telescope (JWST). When pairs of mirror images of such star clusters appear across the lensing critical curve, it is usually assumed that both images will display identical spectral energy distributions (SEDs). However, this assumption may be invalidated in the presence of gravitational microlensing from stars or other compact objects in the lens, since microlensing will affect the SED contribution from bright stars within the star cluster independently in the two mirror images. Here, we explore under what circumstances mismatched mirror-image SEDs are likely to be observable, and argue that SED differences detectable in JWST observations of lensing-cluster fields will be limited to star clusters of mass $< 10^5\ M_\odot$ and ages $\lesssim 5$ Myr. The probability of severely mismatched mirror-image SEDs increases if the stellar initial mass function is very top-heavy and extends to stellar masses $\gg 100\ M_\odot$, as has been suggested to be the case for Population III stars. The prevalence of lensed star clusters with highly discrepant mirror-image SEDs could therefore serve as a probe of very massive stars and extreme stellar populations in the early Universe.

Abstract Translation:
强引力透镜星团最近在星系团场中被詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜（JWST）探测到，红移高达$z\approx 10$。当此类星团的镜像图像对出现在透镜临界曲线两侧时，通常假设两个图像将显示相同的光谱能量分布（SED）。然而，如果透镜中存在来自恒星或其他致密天体的引力微透镜效应，这一假设可能失效，因为微透镜会独立影响两个镜像图像中星团内明亮恒星的SED贡献。本文探讨了在何种情况下镜像图像SED不匹配可能被观测到，并论证在JWST对透镜星系团场的观测中，可探测的SED差异仅限于质量$< 10^5\ M_\odot$且年龄$\lesssim 5$ Myr的星团。如果恒星初始质量函数非常顶部沉重且延伸至恒星质量$\gg 100\ M_\odot$（如对第三族恒星所提出的情况），则严重不匹配的镜像图像SED的概率会增加。因此，具有高度不一致镜像图像SED的透镜星团的普遍性可作为早期宇宙中极大质量恒星和极端恒星群体的探针。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要：强引力透镜星团镜像图像的光谱能量分布差异可作为探测早期宇宙中超大质量恒星和极端恒星群体的有效工具，为理解早期宇宙恒星形成提供新途径。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/Fig1.png)

图1：星团镜像图像可能产生不匹配SED的机制示意图。左图：一个包含少量红色演化恒星（此处仅一颗；红色圆圈）和大量蓝色恒星（为示意仅三颗；蓝色圆圈）的星团位于源平面中的宏透镜焦散线附近。右图：在像平面中，来自蓝色和红色恒星的光混合成两个未分辨的星团宏像（绿色圆圈），对称地位于临界曲线两侧（第三个像也直接形成于临界曲线上，但高度缩小，未显示）。在仅考虑宏透镜的情况下，两个星团像包含每颗恒星高度拉伸的像，呈现为镜像翻转版本。位于作为宏透镜的星系团中的恒星或其他致密天体（黑色圆圈）引起的微透镜会扭曲两个星团像内单个恒星的放大率。由于星团宏像在像平面中的分离（通常\(\approx 0.1\) –1角秒），不同的致密天体独立地对两组恒星像进行微透镜，从而可能改变两个未分辨星团像之间红蓝光的平衡。

<small>Figure 1: Schematic illustration of the mechanism by which mirror images of star cluster may develop mismatched SEDs. Left: A star cluster featuring a small number of red, evolved stars (here just one; red circle) and a larger number of blue stars (for illustrative purposes just three; blue circles) is located close to the macrolensing caustic in the source plane. Right: In the image plane, the light from the blue and red stars blends into two unresolved star cluster macroimages (green circles) located symmetrically on either side of the critical curve (a third image is also formed directly on the critical curve, but is highly demagnified and not shown). In the case of macrolensing only, the two star cluster images contain the highly stretched images of each star, appearing as mirror-flipped versions of each other. Microlensing by stars or other compact objects (black circles) located in the galaxy cluster that acts as the macrolens distort the magnification of individual stars within the two star cluster images. Due to the separation of the star cluster macroimages in the image plane (typically \(\approx 0.1\) –1 arcsec), different compact objects microlens the two sets of stellar images independently, which can alter the balance of red to blue light between the two unresolved star cluster images.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/Fig2a.png)

图2：距离宏透镜焦散线10 pc的\(10^{5}\ M_{\odot}\)星团内恒星的宏透镜和微透镜。a) \(\geq 10\ M_{\odot}\)恒星（蓝点）相对于焦散线（黑色虚线）的投影空间分布。b) 假设在\(z_{{l}}=0.5\)透镜平面中微透镜的\(\Sigma_{\star}=10\ M_{\odot}\) pc -2时，位于\(z=6\)的星团单个宏像内恒星的放大率分布：正宇称像（蓝线），负宇称像（红线），仅宏透镜（黑线，正/负宇称相同）。面板中焦散线左侧的恒星不产生对应像，此处未包含。由于引力微透镜，正宇称和负宇称分布均比仅宏透镜的分布更宽。与正宇称分布相比，负宇称概率分布表现出向极低放大率的显著尾部，但也存在极高放大率概率的微妙提升。

<small>Figure 2: Macro- and microlensing of stars within a \(10^{5}\ M_{\odot}\) star cluster at a distance of 10 pc from the macrolensing caustic. a) Projected spatial distribution of the \(\geq 10\ M_{\odot}\) stars (blue dots) with respect to the caustic (dashed black line). b) Magnification distribution for stars within a single macroimage of the star cluster, when placed at \(z=6\) , under the assumption of \(\Sigma_{\star}=10\ M_{\odot}\) pc -2 in microlenses in the \(z_{{l}}=0.5\) lens plane: positive-parity image (blue line), negative-parity image (red line), macrolensing only (black line, same for positive/negative parity). Stars to the left of the caustic in panel do not produce counterimages and are not included here. Due to gravitational microlensing, both the positive- and negative parity distributions are wider than the distribution due to macrolensing only. Compared to the positive-parity distribution, the negative-parity probabiliity distribution exhibits a prominent tail to very low magnifications, but also a subtle boost of the probabilities for very high magnifications.</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/Fig3a.png)

图3：假设完全采样的Kroupa (2001) IMF（0.1–120 \(M_{\odot}\)），在\(z=6\)处年轻、未透镜的\(10^{5}\ M_{\odot}\)、\(Z=0.002\)单一年龄星团星光在JWST/NIRCam波段的光度演化：a) 滤光片F115W、F200W和F444W的亮度随年龄的变化；b) 年龄为1、3、10和20 Myr时的JWST/NIRcam SED。演化恒星（红色）的贡献表现为年龄3 Myr及以上时波长超过2 \(\mu\) m的SED上升。

<small>Figure 3: The photometric evolution in JWST/NIRCam bands of the star light from a young, unlensed \(10^{5}\ M_{\odot}\) , \(Z=0.002\) single-age star cluster at \(z=6\) , under the assumption of a fully-sampled Kroupa ( 2001 ) IMF from 0.1–120 \(M_{\odot}\) : a) Brightness evolution in filters F115W, F200W and F444W as a function of age; b) JWST/NIRcam SEDs at ages 1, 3, 10 and 20 Myr. The contribution from evolved, red stars is seen as an upturn in the SEDs for wavelengths above 2 \(\mu\) m at ages 3 Myr and above.</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/Fig4a.png)

图4：\(z=6\)处星团镜像图像的不一致SED，由距离宏焦散线10 pc的\(Z=0.002\)星团形成，并受\(\Sigma_{\star}=10\ M_{\odot}\) pc -2微透镜影响。a) 年龄为3和20 Myr时，\(3\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\)星团正宇称（蓝线）和负宇称（红线）镜像图像的JWST/NIRCam SED示例。黑线显示仅宏透镜预测的相应SED（两个镜像图像相同）。b) 正宇称和负宇称图像之间\(m_{115}-m_{444}\)颜色的变化（\(\Delta(m_{115}-m_{444})=(m_{115}-m_{444})^{+}-(m_{115}-m_{444})^{-}\)），作为正宇称图像F200W视星等（\(m_{200}^{+}\)）的函数，针对总质量为\(1\times 10^{4}\)（红圈）、\(3\times 10^{4}\)（橙圈）、\(1\times 10^{5}\ M_{\odot}\)（绿圈）的星团，年龄为3和20 Myr。每个不同的点云对应100次蒙特卡洛实现。镜像图像之间的颜色差异在3 Myr时比20 Myr时更大（请注意面板b中y轴范围不同）。在固定年龄下，镜像图像之间的颜色差异也随星团质量降低而增大，同时整体SED星等（F200W + ）更暗。

<small>Figure 4: Discrepant SEDs of star cluster mirror images at \(z=6\) , formed by \(Z=0.002\) star clusters at 10 pc from the macrocaustic and affected by \(\Sigma_{\star}=10\ M_{\odot}\) pc -2 microlensing. a) Examples of JWST/NIRCam SEDs of positive (blue line) and negative-parity (red line) mirror images of a \(3\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\) star cluster at ages 3 and 20 Myr. The black line shows the corresponding SEDs predicted by macrolensing alone (the same for both mirror images). b) Variation in \(m_{115}-m_{444}\) colour between positive- and negative-parity images ( \(\Delta(m_{115}-m_{444})=(m_{115}-m_{444})^{+}-(m_{115}-m_{444})^{-}\) ), as a function of the F200W apparent magnitude of the positive-parity image ( \(m_{200}^{+}\) ), for star clusters with total masses \(1\times 10^{4}\) (red circles), \(3\times 10^{4}\) (orange circles), \(1\times 10^{5}\ M_{\odot}\) (green circles) at ages 3 and 20 Myr. Every differently cloud of points correspond to 100 Monte Carlo realizations. The colour differences between the mirror images are seen to be larger at 3 Myr than at 20 Myr (please note the different y-axis limits in panel b). At fixed age, the colour differences between the mirror images is also seen to become larger for lower-mass star clusters, while at the same time occurring at fainter overall SED magnitudes (F200W + ).</small>

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/Fig5.png)

图5：受微透镜影响的年轻\(Z=0.002\)、\(z=6\)星团镜像图像在F115W和F444W滤光片之间的中位绝对颜色差异，作为正宇称星团像中位视F200W通量的函数，微透镜参数\(\Sigma_{\star}=10\ M_{\odot}\) pc -2。显示了质量\(1\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\)（红圈）、\(3\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\)（橙方块）和\(1\times 10^{5}\ M_{\odot}\)（绿三角）的星团模型，年龄为3、5、10和20 Myr（从右到左）。虚线表示我们认为颜色差异在JWST对星团透镜场观测中可能可探测的区域（详见正文）。对于质量范围\(1\times 10^{4}\) – \(3\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\)的星团，中位颜色差异在年龄\(\approx 3\) –5 Myr时处于可观测范围。

<small>Figure 5: Median absolute colour difference between the F115W and F444W filters for mirror images of young \(Z=0.002\) , \(z=6\) star clusters affected by microlensing with \(\Sigma_{\star}=10\ M_{\odot}\) pc -2 , as a function of the median apparent F200W flux of the positive-parity star cluster image. Models for star clusters of mass \(1\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\) (red circles), \(3\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\) (orange squares) and \(1\times 10^{5}\ M_{\odot}\) (green triangles) are shown at ages 3, 5, 10 and 20 Myr (from right to left). The dashed line indicates the part of the diagram where we consider that colour differences may be detectable in JWST observations of cluster-lens fields (see main text for details). For star clusters in the mass range \(1\times 10^{4}\) – \(3\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\) , the median colour difference is in the observable range for ages \(\approx 3\) –5 Myr.</small>

#### Figure 6
![Figure 6](https://arxiv.org/html/Fig6.png)

图6：假设完全采样的对数平坦IMF（2–2000 \(M_{\odot}\)），在\(z=6\)处年轻、未透镜的\(10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\)、第三族单一年龄星团星光在JWST/NIRCam滤光片F115W、F200W和F444W中的光度演化。在年龄\(\approx 1\) –2 Myr时，星团在F444W波段变得非常明亮，因为质量范围300–2000 \(M_{\odot}\)的恒星在其生命末期达到\(T_{{eff}}<2\times 10^{4}\) K状态。

<small>Figure 6: Photometric evolution in JWST/NIRCam filters F115W, F200W and F444W of the star light from a young, unlensed \(10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\) , Pop III single-age star cluster at \(z=6\) , under the assumption of a fully-sampled log-flat IMF from 2–2000 \(M_{\odot}\) . At ages \(\approx 1\) –2 Myr, the star cluster becomes very bright in the F444W band as stars in the 300–2000 \(M_{\odot}\) mass range reach \(T_{{eff}}<2\times 10^{4}\) K states at the end of their lives.</small>

#### Figure 7
![Figure 7](https://arxiv.org/html/Fig7a.png)

图7：\(z=6\)第三族星团（对数平坦IMF，质量范围2–2000 \(M_{\odot}\)）的不一致镜像图像SED。左图：年龄为1.5和2.0 Myr时，\(1\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\)星团正宇称（蓝线）和负宇称（红线）镜像图像的JWST/NIRCam SED示例。黑线显示仅宏透镜预测的相应SED（两个镜像图像相同）。右图：镜像图像在F115W和F444W滤光片之间的中位绝对颜色差异，作为正宇称星团像中位视F200W通量的函数。显示了质量\(3\times 10^{3}\ M_{\odot}\)（红圈）、\(1\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\)（橙方块）和\(3\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\)（绿三角）的星团模型，年龄为1.5、2.0和3.0 Myr（从右到左），相对于我们认为颜色差异可探测的区域（虚线）。对于\(3\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\)星团，在1.5–3.0 Myr时产生可探测范围内的一致SED，而较低质量星团（\(1\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\)和\(3\times 10^{3}\ M_{\odot}\)）仅在此年龄跨度的一部分时间内产生不一致SED。在中位\(m_{200}^{+} 5 )时，\(3\times 10^{3}\ M_{\odot}\)模型在2–3 Myr时的行为（非常暗，镜像图像间SED差异小）是由IMF采样效应引起的，因为此类星团中恒星数量较少。

<small>Figure 7: Discrepant mirror image SEDs for \(z=6\) Pop III star clusters with a log-flat IMF throughout the 2–2000 \(M_{\odot}\) mass range. Left: Examples of JWST/NIRCam SEDs of positive (blue line) and negative-parity (red line) mirror images of a \(1\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\) star cluster at ages 1.5 and 2.0 Myr. The black line shows the corresponding SEDs predicted by macrolensing alone (the same for both mirror images). Right: Median absolute colour difference between the F115W and F444W filters for mirror images as a function of the median apparent F200W flux of the positive-parity star cluster image. Models for star clusters of mass \(3\times 10^{3}\ M_{\odot}\) (red circles), \(1\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\) (orange squares) and \(3\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\) (green triangles) are shown at ages 1.5, 2.0 and 3.0 Myr (from right to left), in relation to the part of the diagram (dashed line) where we consider colour differences to be detectable. For \(3\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\) star clusters, discrepant SEDs in the detectable regime are produced at 1.5–3.0 Myr, whereas lower-mass star clusters ( \(1\times 10^{4}\ M_{\odot}\) and \(3\times 10^{3}\ M_{\odot}\) ) only produce discrepant SEDs during a fraction of this age span. At median \(m_{200}^{+} 5 ). The behaviour of the \(3\times 10^{3}\ M_{\odot}\) models at 2–3 Myr (very faint, with small SED difference between mirror images) is caused by IMF sampling effects due to the small number of stars present within such star clusters.</small>

图8：在\(z=6\)星团（标准、完全采样IMF）情况下，不同质量恒星对JWST/NIRCam滤光片F115W（蓝）、F200W（绿）和F444W（红）积分光的相对贡献，年龄为1 Myr（左）和3 Myr（右）。

### [38] [MUSE-ALMA Haloes XIII. Molecular gas in $z \sim 0.5$ HI-selected galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.08633)
*Victoria Bollo,Celine Peroux,Martin Zwaan,Jianhang Chen,Varsha Kulkarni,Capucine Barfety,Simon Weng,Natascha Forster Schreiber,Linda Tacconi,Benedetta Casavecchia,Tamsyn O'Beirne,Laurent Chemin,Ramona Augustin,Mitchell Halley*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文与用户Zotero画像高度匹配：核心作者Jianhang Chen、Capucine Barfety、Linda Tacconi均在列；主题涉及ALMA、分子气体、恒星形成率等用户高频关键词；研究内容为高红移星系分子气体与恒星形成效率，属于用户重点关注的星系介质与恒星形成领域。

TL;DR: MUSE-ALMA Haloes调查新增39个星系，共60个与强HI吸收相关的星系，在9个新星系中探测到CO发射，将CO发射的HI选择星系数量翻倍，分子气体质量探测深度提高1.2个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究红移约0.5处与强HI吸收相关的星系，通过扩展样本和更深的分子气体探测，完善该红移处的重子物质普查。

Method: 使用ALMA Cycle 10观测新增39个系统，结合VLT/MUSE和HST数据，比较CO(2-1)和CO(3-2)特性与恒星形成率、气体相金属丰度。

Result: 在60个星系中，12个探测到CO发射；发现恒星形成效率的双重行为：低质量系统遵循主序标度关系，而高质量系统显示受抑制的恒星形成。

Conclusion: HI吸收体同时追踪演化成熟和年轻星系，为完成红移约0.5处的重子物质普查迈出关键一步。

Abstract: We present new results from the MUSE-ALMA Haloes survey, covering 79 galaxies associated with strong HI absorption at redshift about 0.5. Our ALMA Cycle 10 observations add 39 systems to the initial 21, bringing the total to 60 galaxies. CO emission is detected in 9 new galaxies, and in 12 of 60 total, doubling the number of CO-emitting HI-selected galaxies and probing 1.2 dex deeper in molecular gas mass than previous studies. These galaxies span a wide range of stellar masses and metallicities. By comparing CO(2-1) and CO(3-2) properties with star formation rates and gas-phase metallicities from VLT/MUSE and HST, we find a dual behaviour in star formation efficiency: low-mass systems follow main-sequence scaling relations, while high-mass systems show suppressed star formation. This diversity indicates that HI absorbers trace both evolved and younger galaxies, providing a key step toward completing the baryon census at redshift about 0.5.

Abstract Translation:
我们展示了MUSE-ALMA Haloes巡天的新结果，涵盖了79个与红移约0.5处强HI吸收相关的星系。我们的ALMA第10周期观测在最初的21个系统基础上新增了39个，使总数达到60个星系。在9个新星系中探测到CO发射，总计60个星系中有12个探测到CO，使CO发射的HI选择星系数量翻倍，并且分子气体质量的探测深度比以往研究深1.2 dex。这些星系跨越了广泛的恒星质量和金属丰度范围。通过将CO(2-1)和CO(3-2)性质与来自VLT/MUSE和HST的恒星形成速率及气相金属丰度进行比较，我们发现恒星形成效率存在双重行为：低质量系统遵循主序标度关系，而高质量系统则表现出恒星形成受抑制。这种多样性表明HI吸收体同时追踪演化成熟和年轻星系，为完成红移约0.5处的重子物质普查迈出了关键一步。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，结论如下：HI吸收体同时追踪演化成熟和年轻星系，为完成红移约0.5处的重子物质普查迈出关键一步。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/2601.08633/assets/figures/hist_redshift.png)

图1：CO探测（蓝色）和非CO探测（浅蓝色）星系作为红移（左）和恒星质量（中）函数的分布。右图绘制了与吸收体相关的多个星系的金属丰度函数（Halley et al., in prep）。此图展示了MUSE-ALMA Haloes巡天，包括来自新ALMA大型计划及先前ALMA数据的所有源（见第2.2节）。中图和右图数量较少，因为仅包含具有可靠\(M_{\star}\)和[M/H]测定的星系。探测的中位值分别为红移0.6、恒星质量9.66和吸收金属丰度\(-1.23\)，而非探测的中位值为0.5、9.16和\(-1.84\)。总体而言，我们未发现探测率与这些性质中的任何一个存在明确相关性，这表明CO发射的探测可能由星系整体性质的组合决定，而非单一性质。

<small>Figure 1: Distribution of CO-detections (blue) and non-CO-detections (light blue) on galaxies as a function of redshift (left) and stellar mass (middle). The right panel is plotted as a function of metallicity corresponding to multiple galaxies associated with the absorbers (Halley et al., in prep). This figure represents the MUSE-ALMA Haloes survey, including all the sources from the new ALMA Large Program and previous ALMA data (see Section 2.2 ). The middle and right panels have fewer numbers because only those with reliable \(M_{\star}\) and [M/H] determinations are included. The median values for the detections are 0.6, 9.66 and \(-1.23\) for the redshift, stellar mass and absorption metallicity, while the non-detections have median values of 0.5, 9.16, and \(-1.84\) . Overall, we report no clear correlation between the detection rate and any of these properties, suggesting that the detection of CO emission may be governed by a combination of global galaxy properties, rather than just one property alone.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/2601.08633/assets/figures/moment_maps/Q0152m2001_12.png)

图2：新探测到的九个源的CO探测和光谱轮廓。左图显示零阶矩图，带有\(\pm\) 3、\(\pm\) 4和\(\pm\) 5 \(\sigma\)等值线，右图显示提取的CO光谱。每个光谱周围的灰色阴影区域表示来自单个数据立方体的\(\pm 1\sigma\) RMS噪声水平估计，蓝色阴影区域表示用于创建矩图的速度范围。最后一行右图显示了非探测的静止帧叠加光谱，带有\(\pm 1\sigma\)和\(\pm 2\sigma\)水平。所有探测源的积分CO通量及相关不确定性的总结见表1。

<small>Figure 2: CO detections and spectral profiles of the new nine detected sources. Left panels show the moment zero maps with the \(\pm\) 3, \(\pm\) 4, and \(\pm\) 5 \(\sigma\) level contours, while the right panels display the extracted CO spectra. The grey shaded regions around each spectrum represent the \(\pm 1\sigma\) RMS noise level estimate from the individual data cubes, and the blue shaded region indicates the velocity range used to create the moment maps. The final row, right figure, presents the rest-frame stacked spectrum of non-detections with \(\pm 1\sigma\) and \(\pm 2\sigma\) levels. A summary of the integrated CO fluxes and associated uncertainties for all detected sources is provided in Table 1 .</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/2601.08633/assets/figures/alpha_co.png)

图3：不同金属丰度下的\(\alpha_{\text{CO}}\)模型。在本工作中，我们采用Genzel等人（2015）提出的模型，以蓝点表示，该模型对应于Bolatto等人（2013）和Genzel等人（2012）方案的几何平均值，如公式3所示。作为参考，我们还包含了Accurso等人（2017）提出的模型，该模型会导致我们样本中星系的\(\alpha_{\text{CO}}\)值更高。为避免外推到参数空间约束较差的区域，我们对\(\alpha_{\text{CO}}\)设置了一个上限，设定为我们样本中测得的最低发射金属丰度，这导致\(\alpha_{\text{CO}}\sim 15\)。

<small>Figure 3: Different \(\alpha_{\text{CO}}\) models across varying metallicites. In this work, we adopt the model proposed by Genzel et al. ( 2015 ) , shown in the blue points, which corresponds to the geometric mean of the prescriptions of Bolatto et al. ( 2013 ) and Genzel et al. ( 2012 ) , as indicated in Eq. 3 . As a reference, we also include the model proposed by Accurso et al. ( 2017 ) , which would lead to higher values for \(\alpha_{\text{CO}}\) for the galaxies in our sample. To prevent extrapolation into poorly constrained regions of parameter space, we impose an upper limit on \(\alpha_{\text{CO}}\) , set to the lowest emission metallicity measured in our sample, which leads to an \(\alpha_{\text{CO}}\sim 15\) .</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/2601.08633/assets/figures/nhi_mh2.png)

图4：左：分子气体质量（\(M_{\text{H}_{2}}\)）作为HI柱密度（\(N_{\text{HI}}\)）的函数。蓝色圆圈代表我们的样本，与来自kanekarMassiveAbsorptionselectedGalaxies2018和klitschH2MolecularGas2021的先前HI吸收选择系统研究（灰色）进行比较。右：\(N_{\text{HI}}\)和碰撞参数，按分子气体质量着色。在此图中，我们包含了样本中所有源的碰撞参数，而非像先前研究（例如perouxSINFONIIntegralField2016；Hamanowicz et al. 2020；wengMUSEALMAHaloesVIII2022）那样仅限于最小的\(b\)。圆圈代表CO探测，三角形代表非CO探测。我们还分别以虚线和点线形式包含了来自voortCosmologicalSimulationsCircumgalactic2019和nelsonResolvingSmallscaleCold2020模拟的中性氢柱密度中值径向轮廓。我们未报告不同分子气体质量的柱密度与碰撞参数之间存在明确相关性。

<small>Figure 4: Left: Molecular gas mass ( \(M_{\text{H}_{2}}\) ) as a function of H i column density ( \(N_{\text{HI}}\) ). Blue circles represent our sample in comparison with previous studies on H i -absorption selected systems from kanekarMassiveAbsorptionselectedGalaxies2018 and klitschH2MolecularGas2021 , shown in grey. Right: \(N_{\text{HI}}\) and impact parameter, colour coded by the molecular gas masses. In this plot, we include all impact parameters for the sources in our sample, rather than limiting to the smallest \(b\) as done in previous studies (e.g. perouxSINFONIIntegralField2016 ; Hamanowicz et al. 2020 ; wengMUSEALMAHaloesVIII2022 ) . The circles represent CO detections, and the triangle represents non-CO detections. We also include the median radial profiles for the neutral hydrogen column density from the simulations by voortCosmologicalSimulationsCircumgalactic2019 and nelsonResolvingSmallscaleCold2020 in the dashed and dotted lines, respectively. We report no clear correlation between the column density and impact parameter for different molecular gas masses.</small>

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/2601.08633/assets/figures/sfr_mh2_alphaZ.png)

图5：左：恒星形成速率（SFR）作为分子气体质量（\(M_{\text{H}_{2}}\)）的函数。右：恒星质量（\(M_{\star}\)）作为分子气体质量（\(M_{\text{H}_{2}}\)）的函数。我们的样本以蓝色圆圈显示，蓝色箭头表示\(3\sigma\)上限。第3.2节描述的叠加光谱结果以蓝色星形显示。我们还包含了左图角落处一个大蓝色箭头所示的SFR平均尘埃校正。作为比较，我们包含了代表低红移星系的xCOLD GASS巡天（saintongeXCOLDGASSComplete2017）和红移范围\(z\sim 0.3-1.2\)的PHIBSS巡天（tacconiPHIBSSUnifiedScaling2018）的数据。实线代表来自tacconiPHIBSSUnifiedScaling2018的分子气体主序标度关系。我们还在两个面板中包含了来自kanekarMassiveAbsorptionselectedGalaxies2018和klitschH2MolecularGas2021的估计，标记为其他HI选择系统。我们的\(M_{H_{2}}/M_{\odot}\lesssim 10^{9.8}\)的源位于相同红移范围内“正常恒星形成星系”的预期SFR \(-M_{\text{H}_{2}}\)关系之上约\(\sim 0.3\) dex，而\(M_{H_{2}}/M_{\odot}>10^{9.8}\)的系统位于该关系之下约\(\sim 1.5\) dex。这一趋势表明HI选择系统具有双重行为。分子气体质量低的星系高效形成恒星，遵循主序星系的耗尽时标和\(M_{\star}-M_{\text{H}_{2}}\)标度关系。相比之下，分子气体质量高的星系表现出低效的恒星形成，并低于预期的恒星质量增长，这可能是因为它们仍在从星系际介质活跃吸积气体或在群环境中相互作用。这些系统似乎尚未达到主序星系特征的平衡条件。

<small>Figure 5: Left: Star formation rate (SFR) as a function of molecular gas mass ( \(M_{\text{H}_{2}}\) ). Right: Stellar mass ( \(M_{\star}\) ) as a function of molecular gas mass ( \(M_{\text{H}_{2}}\) ). Our sample is shown in blue circles, and the blue arrows represent a \(3\sigma\) upper limit. The result from the stacked spectrum described in Sect. 3.2 is shown by the blue star. We also include the mean dust correction for SFR depicted by a large blue arrow on the corner of the left panel. For comparison, we include data from the xCOLD GASS survey ( saintongeXCOLDGASSComplete2017 ) , which represents low-redshift galaxies, and the PHIBSS survey ( tacconiPHIBSSUnifiedScaling2018 ) , in the redshift range \(z\sim 0.3-1.2\) . The solid line represents the molecular gas main sequence scaling relation from tacconiPHIBSSUnifiedScaling2018 . We also included estimates from kanekarMassiveAbsorptionselectedGalaxies2018 and klitschH2MolecularGas2021 in both panels, labelled as other H i –selected systems. Our sources with \(M_{H_{2}}/M_{\odot}\lesssim 10^{9.8}\) lie \(\sim 0.3\) dex above the expected SFR \(-M_{\text{H}_{2}}\) relations for ‘normal star-forming galaxies’ at the same redshift range, while the systems with with \(M_{H_{2}}/M_{\odot}>10^{9.8}\) lie \(\sim 1.5\) dex below the relation. This trend suggests that H i –selected systems have a dual behaviour. Galaxies with low molecular gas masses form stars efficiently, following both the depletion timescales and the \(M_{\star}-M_{\text{H}_{2}}\) scaling relations of main-sequence galaxies. In contrast, galaxies with high molecular gas masses show inefficient star formation and fall below the expected stellar mass growth, likely because they are still actively accreting gas from the intergalactic medium or interacting within group environments. These systems appear not yet to have reached the equilibrium conditions characteristic of main-sequence galaxies.</small>

#### Figure 6
![Figure 6](https://arxiv.org/html/2601.08633/assets/figures/metallicity_mh2.png)

图6：左：我们HI选择星系的星云发射金属丰度\(12+\log\) (O/H)（wengMUSEALMAHaloesVIII2023）作为分子气体质量（\(M_{{H}_{2}}\)）的函数。蓝色圆圈表示CO探测，蓝色左向箭头表示CO非探测的\(3\sigma\)上限。第3.2节描述的叠加光谱结果以蓝色星形显示。实线表示来自Genzel等人（2015）的PHIBSS样本（tacconiPHIBSSUnifiedScaling2018）的质量-金属丰度关系。金属丰度与CO可探测性之间呈现正相关，CO探测星系倾向于占据较高金属丰度区域（\(\log Z\gtrsim 8.5\)），这与先前许多研究（例如Bolatto et al. 2013）的发现一致。右：所有星系的发射金属丰度直方图，CO探测以蓝色填充，非探测以浅蓝色填充。橙色虚线表示金属丰度\(\log Z\sim 8.5\)，这设定了第5节讨论的高和低金属丰度区域。尽管分布显著重叠，双样本Kolmogorov-Smirnov检验得出p值为0.004，表明底层金属丰度分布存在统计显著差异。这强化了金属丰度在控制HI选择系统中分子气体可观测性方面起关键作用的解释。

<small>Figure 6: Left: Nebular emission metallicity, \(12+\log\) (O/H) ( wengMUSEALMAHaloesVIII2023 ) , as a function of molecular gas mass ( \(M_{{H}_{2}}\) ) for our H i –selected galaxies. Blue circles indicate CO detections, and blue leftward arrows show \(3\sigma\) upper limits for CO non-detections. The result from the stacked spectrum described in Sect. 3.2 is shown by the blue star. The solid line indicates the mass-metallicity relation from Genzel et al. ( 2015 ) for the PHIBSS sample ( tacconiPHIBSSUnifiedScaling2018 ) . A positive correlation emerges between metallicity and CO detectability, with CO-detected galaxies tending to occupy the higher-metallicity regime ( \(\log Z\gtrsim 8.5\) ), as found previously in many studies (e.g., Bolatto et al. 2013 ) . Right: Histogram of emission metallicities for all galaxies, with CO detections in blue and non-detections in light blue filled histogram. The dashed orange line indicates a metallicity \(\log Z\sim 8.5\) , which sets the higher and lower metallicity regimes discussed in Sect. 5 . Although the distributions overlap significantly, a two-sample Kolmogorov-Smirnov test yields a p-value of 0.004, indicating a statistically significant difference in the underlying metallicity distributions. This reinforces the interpretation that metallicity plays a key role in governing the observability of molecular gas in H i –selected systems.</small>

#### Figure 7
![Figure 7](https://arxiv.org/html/2601.08633/assets/figures/tdep_redshift_color.png)

图7：我们HI选择样本（高/低分子气体质量系统分别用蓝色/浅蓝色圆圈表示）的分子气体耗尽时标（\(t_{\text{dep}}=M_{\text{H}_{2}}/\text{SFR}\)）作为红移的函数，与文献标度关系和发射选择样本（saintongeXCOLDGASSComplete2017；tacconiPHIBSSUnifiedScaling2018）进行比较。第3.2节描述的叠加光谱结果以蓝色星形显示。红色实线曲线显示了来自tacconiPHIBSSUnifiedScaling2018的主序星系经验推导的\(t_{\text{dep}}\)演化，点线标记每个红移处的哈勃时间，细实线代表来自tacconiEvolutionStarFormingInterstellar2020的恒星质量倍增时间（\(t_{*}=M_{\star}/\text{SFR}\)），紫色虚线来自ALMACAL巡天（Bollo et al. 2025）推导的宇宙耗尽时标。HI选择星系，无论是来自我们的样本还是高红移文献源（灰点；klitschH2MolecularGas2021；neelemanMolecularEmissionGalaxy2018；neelemanColdMassiveRotating2020；neelemanII158Mm2025；Fynbo et al. 2018；kanekarHighMolecularGas2020；kanekarMassiveAbsorptionselectedGalaxies2018；kaurMassiveDustyHi2022；kaurMassiveIabsorptionselectedGalaxy2025），始终位于主序关系之上，表明恒星形成效率较低。几个星系的\(t_{\text{dep}}\)接近或超过哈勃时间，表明分子气体消耗低效或恒星形成受抑制。

<small>Figure 7: Molecular gas depletion time ( \(t_{\text{dep}}=M_{\text{H}_{2}}/\text{SFR}\) ) as a function of redshift for our H i –selected sample (blue/light-blue circles for high/low molecular gas mass systems), compares with literature scaling relations and emission-selected samples ( saintongeXCOLDGASSComplete2017 ; tacconiPHIBSSUnifiedScaling2018 ) . The result from the stacked spectrum described in Sect. 3.2 is shown by the blue star. The solid red curve shows the empirically derived \(t_{\text{dep}}\) evolution for main-sequence galaxies from tacconiPHIBSSUnifiedScaling2018 , the dotted line marks the Hubble time at each redshift, the thin solid line represents the stellar mass doubling time ( \(t_{*}=M_{\star}/\text{SFR}\) ) from tacconiEvolutionStarFormingInterstellar2020 , and the purple dashed line is from the cosmic depletion timescales derived from the ALMACAL survey (Bollo et al. 2025 ) . H i –selected galaxies, both from our sample and from high-redshift literature sources (gray dots; klitschH2MolecularGas2021 ; neelemanMolecularEmissionGalaxy2018 ; neelemanColdMassiveRotating2020 ; neelemanII158Mm2025 ; Fynbo et al. 2018 ; kanekarHighMolecularGas2020 ; kanekarMassiveAbsorptionselectedGalaxies2018 ; kaurMassiveDustyHi2022 ; kaurMassiveIabsorptionselectedGalaxy2025 ), consistently lie above the main-sequence relation, indicating lower star formation efficiencies. Several galaxies exhibit \(t_{\text{dep}}\) approaching or exceeding the Hubble time, suggesting inefficient molecular gas consumption or suppressed star formation.</small>

### [39] [Fast rotations in galaxies at cosmic noon indicate central concentration of stars, dark matter or massive black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.03338)
*Fernanda Roman-Oliveira,Francesca Rizzo,Filippo Fraternali*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (95/100) - 该论文直接研究高红移（cosmic noon）盘状星系的旋转曲线，结合ALMA冷气体和JWST近红外成像数据，探讨暗物质分布和中心质量缺失问题。这与用户画像中的dark matter、jwst、alma、cosmic noon、dust、halo、rotation curves等核心关键词高度匹配，且研究主题（高红移星系动力学、暗物质晕约束）与用户主要兴趣领域（强引力透镜、高红移星系动力学）紧密相关。论文方法（动力学建模）和科学问题（中心质量缺失、暗物质分布）均与用户兴趣一致。无负面关键词匹配。

TL;DR: 该研究结合ALMA和JWST观测数据，分析三个高红移盘状星系的旋转曲线，发现动力学模型在星系中心区域低估了旋转速度，表明存在中心质量缺失或暗物质分布异常。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高红移星系（z>0.5）的旋转曲线分析一直面临挑战，缺乏高分辨率运动学数据、准确追踪恒星表面密度的测光数据以及空间分辨的亚毫米观测来追踪冷气体分布。本研究旨在利用ALMA和JWST的先进观测能力，研究高红移盘状星系的动力学特性并约束其暗物质晕。

Method: 从ALPAKA样本中选取三个星系，结合ALMA的高分辨率冷气体观测和JWST的静止近红外成像数据。这些星系最初仅基于ALMA观测被分类为规则旋转盘。通过构建动力学模型来模拟星系的旋转曲线，并与观测数据进行比较。

Result: JWST观测显示这些星系是延伸的对称恒星盘，带有旋臂结构。动力学模型能够很好地再现星系外围区域的旋转，但系统性地低估了中心区域的旋转速度，揭示了相对于观测数据的中心质量缺失。

Conclusion: 观测与模型之间的差异表明：1）由于恒星质量-光比变化或尘埃消光导致核球质量被低估；2）存在超大质量黑洞；3）偏离标准暗物质晕分布，包括增强的中心浓度。这些发现对高红移星系的暗物质分布和中心质量构成提出了重要问题。

Abstract: The rotation curves of regularly rotating disc galaxies are a unique probe of the gravitational potential and dark matter distribution. Until recently, matter decomposition of rotation curves at $z>0.5$ was challenging, not only due to the lack of high resolution kinematic data but also of both suitable photometry to accurately trace the stellar surface density and spatially-resolved sub-mm observations to trace the cold gas distribution. In this paper, we analyse three galaxies from the Archival Large Program to Advance Kinematic Analysis (ALPAKA) sample, combining highly resolved cold gas observations from ALMA with rest-frame near-infrared imaging from JWST to investigate their dynamical properties and constrain their dark matter halos. The galaxies, initially classified as regularly rotating discs based on ALMA observations alone, appear in JWST as extended and symmetric stellar discs with spiral arms. Our dynamical models reproduce the rotation of the discs in the outer parts well, but they systematically underpredict the inner rotation velocities, revealing a deficit of central mass relative to the data. This discrepancy indicates either an underestimation of the bulge masses due to variations in the stellar mass-to-light ratio or dust attenuation or the presence of overmassive black holes. Alternatively, it may suggest departures from standard dark-matter halo profiles, including enhanced central concentrations.

Abstract Translation:
规则旋转盘星系的旋转曲线是研究引力势和暗物质分布的独特探针。直到最近，对红移$z>0.5$的星系进行物质分解仍然具有挑战性，这不仅是因为缺乏高分辨率的运动学数据，还因为缺乏能够精确追踪恒星面密度的合适测光数据以及能够追踪冷气体分布的空间分辨亚毫米观测数据。本文分析了来自档案大型运动学分析计划（ALPAKA）样本的三个星系，结合ALMA的高分辨率冷气体观测数据和JWST的静止系近红外成像数据，研究它们的动力学性质并约束其暗物质晕。这些星系最初仅基于ALMA观测被分类为规则旋转盘，在JWST图像中表现为具有旋臂的延展且对称的恒星盘。我们的动力学模型很好地再现了星系外部的旋转，但系统性地低估了内部旋转速度，揭示了相对于数据而言中心质量的不足。这种差异表明，要么是由于恒星质量-光比变化或尘埃消光导致核球质量被低估，要么是存在超大质量黑洞。或者，它可能暗示偏离了标准暗物质晕轮廓，包括增强的中心浓度。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，观测与模型之间的差异表明：1）由于恒星质量-光比变化或尘埃消光导致核球质量被低估；2）存在超大质量黑洞；3）偏离标准暗物质晕分布，包括增强的中心浓度。这些发现对高红移星系的暗物质分布和中心质量构成提出了重要问题。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
表1：本文研究的三个ALPAKA盘的主要性质和数据。这些星系是根据其运动学性质、空间分辨率以及辅助JWST数据的可用性选择的，详见正文。列：(i) ALPAKA编号。(ii) 星系红移。(iii) 用于运动学的发射线。(iv) 相应的发射线光度。(v) ALMA数据长轴上的独立分辨率元数量，定义为气体盘直径除以圆化后的ALMA波束。(vi) 和 (vii) 用于追踪恒星连续谱分布的JWST成像滤光片及其相应的静止系中心波长。(viii) 和 (ix) 恒星质量和恒星形成率（详见Rizzo等人，2023）。

<small>Table 1 : Main properties and data of the three ALPAKA discs studied in this paper. The galaxies were selected based on their kinematic properties, spatial resolution and availability of ancillary JWST data, as explained in the main text. Columns: (i) ALPAKA ID number. (ii) Redshift of the galaxy. (iii) Emission line used for the kinematics. (iv) Corresponding emission-line luminosity. (v) Number of independent resolution elements over the major axis of the ALMA data, defined as the diameter of the gas disc divided by the circularised ALMA beam. (vi) and (vii) JWST imaging filter used for tracing the distribution of the stellar continuum and the corresponding rest-frame pivot wavelength. (viii) and (ix) Stellar mass and star formation rate, respectively (see Rizzo et al. , 2023 , for details) .</small>

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/x1.png)

图1：上行：本文分析的ALPAKA子样本星系。星系按红移升序从左到右排列。气体数据（见表1）以蓝色等高线显示，水平为\(3\sigma\)、\(6\sigma\)和\(12\sigma\)，其中\(\sigma\)是ALMA气体发射0阶矩图的均方根（RMS）噪声。我们还用虚线等高线显示负发射，水平为\(-3\sigma\)，并在每个面板的左下方显示相应的ALMA波束。背景中显示用于导出恒星面亮度的JWST滤光片，与表1中报告的相同。此处显示的ALMA等高线仅是未掩膜0阶矩图上的发射水平，因此它们不同于Rizzo等人（2023）中显示的伪X \(\sigma\)等高线。下行：RGB合成JWST图像。我们注意到上行和下行的尺度不同，下面板具有更大的视场，使我们能够看到ID3和ID13周围的前景和背景星系。

<small>Figure 1 : Top row: ALPAKA subsample of galaxies analysed in this work. The galaxies are organised in ascending order of redshift, from left to right. The gas data (see Table 1 ) are shown as blue contours with levels following \(3\sigma\) , \(6\sigma\) and \(12\sigma\) , where \(\sigma\) is the root-mean-square (RMS) noise of the ALMA moment 0th map of the gas emission. We also show negative emission with dashed contours at the \(-3\sigma\) level and the corresponding ALMA beam on the bottom left of each panel. In the background, we display the JWST filter used for deriving the stellar surface brightness, same as the one reported in Table 1 . The ALMA contours shown here are simply the emission levels on the unmasked 0th-moment maps, therefore they differ from the pseudo-X \(\sigma\) contours shown in Rizzo et al. ( 2023 ) . Bottom row: RGB composite JWST images. We note that the scales in the top and bottom rows are different with a larger FOV on the bottom panels that allow us to see the foreground and background galaxies surrounding ID3 and ID13.</small>

#### Figure 3
表2：定义二维气体面亮度模型参数的先验：有效半径处的强度（\(I_{{eff}}\)）、有效半径（\(R_{{eff}}\)）、几何中心（\(x_{0}\)、\(y_{0}\)）、椭圆率（\(\epsilon\)）和位置角（\(PA\)）。对于强度，我们任意选择1.2 \(\sigma_{{RMS}}\)作为先验的下界。\(\sigma_{{RMS}}\)是图中的RMS噪声。

<small>Table 2 : Priors for the parameters defining the 2D gas surface brightness models: intensity at the effective radius ( \(I_{{eff}}\) ), effective radius ( \(R_{{eff}}\) ), geometric centre ( \(x_{0}\) , \(y_{0}\) ), ellipticity ( \(\epsilon\) ) and position angle ( \(PA\) ). For the intensity, we arbitrarily chose 1.2 \(\sigma_{{RMS}}\) as the lower bound of the prior. \(\sigma_{{RMS}}\) is the RMS noise in the map.</small>

#### Figure 4
表3：旋转曲线分解先验：基准模型。我们拟合的三个主要参数是总气体质量、总恒星质量和暗物质质量。总气体质量由CO/[CI]光度（见表1）与气体归一化因子（即CO/[CI]线比率\(r_{l}\)乘以\(\alpha_{{CO}/{[CI]}}\)转换因子）的乘积计算得出。截断半径假定为气体数据的范围，即CO/[CI]旋转曲线中的最后一个半径。总恒星质量自由变化，由盘和核球质量的贡献之和计算得出，假设核球的质量-光比是盘的1.4倍。暗物质质量由重子分数参数计算得出，该参数在对数空间中均匀自由变化。

<small>Table 3 : Rotation curve decomposition priors: fiducial model. The main three parameters we fit are the total gas mass, the total stellar mass and the dark matter mass. The total gas mass is computed by the product of the CO/[CI] luminosity (see Table 1 ) and the gas normalisation, i.e. the CO/[CI] line ratio ( \(r_{l}\) ) times the \(\alpha_{{CO}/{[CI]}}\) conversion. The truncation radius is assumed to be the extent of the gas data, that is the last radius in the CO/[CI] rotation curve. The total stellar mass is let free to vary and it is computed by the sum of the contribution of the disc and bulge masses assuming that the mass-to-light ratio of the bulge is 1.4 times that of the disc. The dark matter mass is computed from the baryonic fraction parameter that is let free to vary uniformly in log space.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/x2.png)

图2：ID1的气体（上面板）和恒星分布（下面板）的面亮度模型。左上方面板：ALMA 0阶矩图叠加了数据的黄色等高线和最佳拟合模型的橙色等高线，水平为3 \(\sigma\)、6 \(\sigma\)、9 \(\sigma\)等，其中\(\sigma\)是数据中的RMS噪声。我们还用灰色虚线显示负等高线，水平为\(-3\sigma\)和\(-6\sigma\)。上中方面板：噪声归一化残差图，定义为（数据\(-\)模型）/ RMS。右上方面板：沿星系长轴倾斜环上投影平均面亮度的一维表示。黄色带表示数据及其不确定性，橙色实线表示最佳拟合模型。左下方面板：灰度JWST图像叠加了数据的青色等高线和最佳拟合模型的蓝色等高线，水平为背景以上3 \(\sigma\)、9 \(\sigma\)、27 \(\sigma\)等，其中\(\sigma\)是数据中的RMS噪声。下中方面板：噪声归一化残差图，定义为（数据\(-\)模型）/ RMS。左下方面板：沿星系长轴倾斜环上投影平均面亮度的一维表示。青色带表示数据，蓝色实线表示总最佳拟合模型，该模型由恒星盘（深蓝色虚线）和恒星核球（红色虚线）组成。在右上和右下方面板中，我们分别用垂直虚线和水平虚线显示圆化后的ALMA波束/JWST PSF和数据RMS。

<small>Figure 2 : Surface brightness models of the gas (top panels) and stellar distribution (bottom panels) of ID1. Top left panel: the ALMA moment 0 map is overlayed with yellow contours for the data and orange for the best-fit model, following levels of 3 \(\sigma\) , 6 \(\sigma\) , 9 \(\sigma\) , etc., where \(\sigma\) is the RMS noise in the data. We also show negative contours with dashed gray lines at levels \(-3\sigma\) and \(-6\sigma\) . Top middle panel: noise-normalised residual map defined by (Data \(-\) Model) / RMS. Top right panel: 1D representation of the projected average surface brightness over inclined rings along the major axis of the galaxy. The yellow band represents the data and its uncertainties while the orange solid line represents the best-fit model. Bottom left panel: JWST image in grayscale is overlayed with teal contours for the data and blue for the best-fit model, following levels of 3 \(\sigma\) , 9 \(\sigma\) , 27 \(\sigma\) , etc. above the background, where \(\sigma\) is the RMS noise in the data. Bottom middle panel: noise-normalised residual map defined by (Data \(-\) Model) / RMS. Bottom left panel: 1D representation of the projected average surface brightness over inclined rings along the major axis of the galaxy. The teal band represents the data and the blue solid line represents the total best-fit model which is composed by a stellar disc (dotted dark blue line) and stellar bulge (dashed red line). In both top and bottom right panels we show the circularised ALMA beam/ JWST PSF and the data RMS as vertical dotted and horizontal dashed lines, respectively.</small>

#### Figure 6
表4：气体和恒星二维面亮度拟合的最佳拟合参数。气体盘使用我们基于DYNESTY的脚本建模，恒星盘和核球使用GALFIT建模。对于后者，我们采用了两轮迭代拟合过程，其中几何参数（用星号表示）在第二轮迭代中被固定以减少自由参数的数量。气体盘和恒星盘都是指数盘，核球是德沃库勒轮廓。指数盘的\(R_{eff}\)计算为\(1.678\times R_{d}\)

<small>Table 4 : Best-fit parameters of the 2D surface brightness fits to the gas and stars. The gas discs were modelled using our DYNESTY based script and the stellar discs and bulges were modelled using GALFIT . For the latter, we employed a two-iteration fitting process in which the geometric parameters (indicated with an asterisk) were fixed in the second iteration to reduce the number of free parameters. Both the gas and stellar disc are exponential discs and the bulge is a de Vaucouleurs profile. \(R_{eff}\) for the exponential disc is calculated as \(1.678\times R_{d}\)</small>
