### [54] [The ionised interstellar medium of DSFGs revealed by JWST/NIRSpec and ALMA: Super-solar metallicity, low ionisation parameters and, typical electron densities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.18558)
*Steven Gillman,Kei Ito,Francesco Valentino,Gabe Brammer,Pablo Araya Araya,Georgios Magdis,Ugnė Dudzevičiūtė,Aswin P. Vijayan,Minju Lee,Bitten Gullberg,Daniel Ceverino,Andreas L. Faisst,Seiji Fujimoto,Thomas R. Greve,Rashmi Gottumukkala,Chandana Hegde,Michaela Hirschmann,Shuowen Jin,Christian Kragh Jespersen,Takumi Kakimoto,Mariko Kubo,Peter Laursen,Masato Onodera,Antonio Pensabene,Francesca Rizzo,John R. Weaver,Po-Feng Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (92/100) - 该论文利用JWST/NIRSpec和ALMA研究高红移尘埃遮蔽恒星形成星系(DSFGs)的星际介质，包括金属丰度、电子密度和电离参数，与用户对高红移星系动力学、多相气体和强引力透镜的兴趣高度吻合。论文作者中包含用户核心作者列表中的Seiji Fujimoto、Andreas L. Faisst、Michaela Hirschmann和Aswin P. Vijayan，且主题涉及JWST、ALMA、星际介质和尘埃，与用户Zotero库中的高频关键词匹配。

TL;DR: JWST/NIRSpec观测48个高红移ALMA星系，发现这些远红外明亮星系是质量大、化学演化成熟的系统，偏离了标准尘埃-金属平衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高红移、尘埃遮蔽的恒星形成星系的性质，特别是它们的金属丰度、电子密度和电离参数，以了解这些系统的星际介质特征和演化状态。

Method: 使用JWST/NIRSpec获取近红外光谱(2-4μm)，结合ALMA探测，对48个高红移(z=2.53)星系进行多波段SED分析，测量金属丰度([NII]/Hα)、电子密度([SII]双线比)和电离参数([OII]/Hβ)。

Result: 样本中位恒星质量log(M*/M⊙)=10.8±0.1，尘埃质量log(Md/M⊙)=8.7±0.1；金属丰度12+log(O/H)=8.71±0.02，最明亮的FIR星系偏离基本金属丰度关系0.15±0.03dex；电子密度log(ne/cm³)=2.53±0.07；电离参数log(U)=-2.84±0.06；40%星系显示AGN活动迹象。

Conclusion: 远红外明亮星系是质量大、化学演化成熟的系统，偏离了在较少尘埃遮蔽星系中观察到的标准尘埃和金属产生平衡，突显了JWST和ALMA协同研究的重要性。

Abstract: We present a detailed study of near-infrared (2-4$\rm μ$m) JWST/NIRSpec spectra of 48 high-redshift ($z=2.53^{+1.32}_{-0.70}$) galaxies detected with ALMA at $>3σ$. From a multi-wavelength SED analysis we establish the sample has a a median stellar mass of $\rm\log_{10}(M_\ast/M_\odot)=10.8\pm0.1$ and dust mass of $\rm\log_{10}(M_{\rm d}/M_\odot)=8.7\pm0.1$, covering a broad range of far-infrared luminosity $\rm (\log_{10}(L_{FIR}/L_\odot)=10.9-12.7)$. The majority of sources show no signs of AGN activity, with 40% having either X-ray counterparts $(\rm L_{Xc}>10^{42}erg/s)$, elevated optical line ratios, or broad (FWHM>800 km/s) H$α$ profiles, although we note this is a lower limit due to the stochastic placement of NIRSpec slits. We establish the sample has a median gas-phase metallicity of $12+\log({\rm O/H})=8.71\pm0.02$, as derived from the [NII]/H$α$ ratio, with the most FIR-luminous galaxies ($\rm\log_{10}(L_{\rm FIR}/L_\odot)>12$) falling $0.15\pm0.03$dex above the fundamental metallicity relation. From the [SII] emission-line doublet ratio, we measure a median electron density of $\log_{10}(n_{\rm e}/{\rm cm}^{-3})=2.53\pm0.07$ consistent with less-massive, star-forming, galaxies at the same epoch. For nine galaxies with [OII] and H$β$ detections (median $\rm\log_{10}(L_{\rm FIR}/L_\odot)=11.81\pm0.15$), we derive a median observed (dust-uncorrected) ionisation parameter of $\rm\log_{10}(U)=-2.84\pm0.06$. Our results indicate that luminous far-infrared galaxies are massive, chemically evolved systems that appear to deviate from the standard dust and metal production equilibrium observed in less obscured galaxies. This study demonstrates the synergy of JWST and ALMA in unveiling the nature of DSFGs, and highlights the need for a NIRSpec survey of uniformly selected, massive, dust-obscured, galaxies to fully characterise their interstellar medium.

Abstract Translation:
我们详细研究了48个高红移（$z=2.53^{+1.32}_{-0.70}$）且被ALMA以$>3σ$探测到的星系的近红外（2-4$\rm μ$m）JWST/NIRSpec光谱。通过多波段SED分析，我们确定该样本的中值恒星质量为$\rm\log_{10}(M_\ast/M_\odot)=10.8\pm0.1$，尘埃质量为$\rm\log_{10}(M_{\rm d}/M_\odot)=8.7\pm0.1$，覆盖了广泛的远红外光度范围$\rm (\log_{10}(L_{FIR}/L_\odot)=10.9-12.7)$。大多数源没有显示出活动星系核（AGN）活动的迹象，40%的源具有X射线对应体$(\rm L_{Xc}>10^{42}erg/s)$、增强的光学谱线比或宽的（FWHM>800 km/s）H$α$轮廓，尽管我们注意到由于NIRSpec狭缝的随机放置，这是一个下限。我们确定样本的中值气体相位金属丰度为$12+\log({\rm O/H})=8.71\pm0.02$，这是根据[NII]/H$α$比值推导出的，其中远红外光度最高的星系（$\rm\log_{10}(L_{\rm FIR}/L_\odot)>12$）比基本金属丰度关系高出$0.15\pm0.03$dex。根据[SII]发射线双线比值，我们测量到中值电子密度为$\log_{10}(n_{\rm e}/{\rm cm}^{-3})=2.53\pm0.07$，与同一时期质量较小的恒星形成星系一致。对于九个探测到[OII]和H$β$的星系（中值$\rm\log_{10}(L_{\rm FIR}/L_\odot)=11.81\pm0.15$），我们推导出中值观测（未经尘埃校正）电离参数为$\rm\log_{10}(U)=-2.84\pm0.06$。我们的结果表明，明亮的远红外星系是质量大、化学演化成熟的系统，似乎偏离了在较少尘埃遮蔽星系中观察到的标准尘埃和金属产生平衡。这项研究展示了JWST和ALMA在揭示DSFGs性质方面的协同作用，并强调需要对均匀选择的、大质量的、尘埃遮蔽的星系进行NIRSpec巡天，以全面表征其星际介质。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，远红外明亮星系是质量大、化学演化成熟的系统，偏离了在较少尘埃遮蔽星系中观察到的标准尘埃和金属产生平衡，突显了JWST和ALMA协同研究的重要性。

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/x8.png)

图5：观测到的（未经尘埃校正）[O iii ]/H \(\beta\) 作为[N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) （左）和[S ii ]/H \(\alpha\) （右）的函数。信噪比 \( ii ]/H \(\alpha\) 和[S ii ]/H \(\alpha\) 的分布由灰色直方图显示。我们展示了来自斯隆数字巡天（SDSS；Brinchmann et al., 2004）的典型恒星形成星系在\(z\) \(\sim\) 0（红色密度）的比较样本，以及来自CEERS（Shapley et al., 2023）和AURORA巡天（Shapley et al., 2025）的红移匹配的恒星形成星系样本。黑色实线显示了\(z\) = 0时恒星形成活动与AGN之间的划分（Kauffmann et al., 2003），而来自（Kewley et al., 2013）在\(z\) = 2和\(z\) = 3的理论分界线分别由蓝色和红色虚线给出。黑色箭头表示使用Calzetti et al.（2000）尘埃定律进行A V = 5尘埃校正的影响。大多数ALMA – NIRSpec星系与同一时期的典型SFG一致，趋向于更低的[O iii ]/H \(\beta\) 谱线比，只有三个星系显示出类似AGN的光学谱线诊断特征。

<small>Figure 5 : Observed (dust-uncorrected) [O iii ]/H \(\beta\) as function of [N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) (left) and [S ii ]/H \(\alpha\) (right). Sources with S/N \( ii ]/H \(\alpha\) and [S ii ]/H \(\alpha\) for the full sample is shown by the grey histograms. We show comparison samples of typical star-forming galaxies at \(z\) \(\sim\) 0 (red density) from the Sloan Digital Sky Survey (SDSS; Brinchmann et al., 2004 ) , as well as a redshift matched sample of star-forming galaxies from the CEERS (Shapley et al., 2023 ) and AURORA Surveys Shapley et al. ( 2025 ) . The black solid curve shows the division between star-formation acticity and AGN (Kauffmann et al., 2003 ) at \(z\) = 0 whilst the theoretical demarcation at \(z\) = 2 and \(z\) = 3 from (Kewley et al., 2013 ) is given by the blue- and red-dashed lines respectively. The black arrow indicates the impact of A V = 5 dust correction using a Calzetti et al. ( 2000 ) dust law. The majority of ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies are consistent with typical SFGs at the same epoch, pushing to lower [O iii ]/H \(\beta\) line ratios, with only three galaxies showing AGN-like optical line diagnostics.</small>

#### Figure 6
![Figure 6](https://arxiv.org/html/x9.png)

图6：使用Bian et al.（2018）强线校准从[N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) 指数推导出的气体相位金属丰度，作为ALMA – NIRSpec星系恒星质量的函数。信噪比 \( ii ] 6584 \(\lambda\) 发射线的源显示为上限。水平虚线表示太阳金属丰度（Asplund, 2005，12+log(O/H)= 8.66）。我们展示了来自SDSS（Curti et al., 2020）在\(z\) \(\sim\) 0（灰线）、MOSDEF巡天（Sanders et al., 2021）在\(z\) \(\sim\) 2.3（绿实线）和\(z\) \(\sim\) 3.3（红实线）的典型恒星形成星系比较样本，以及来自CEERS（Shapley et al., 2023）和AURORA巡天（Shapley et al., 2025）的红移匹配星系样本。我们进一步比较了来自KAOSS在\(z\) \(\sim\) 1 – 3（Birkin, 2022；Birkin et al., 2024b）的DSFGs高红移观测、来自Hogan et al.（2021）在\(z\) \(\sim\) 2.25的赫歇尔选择源，以及来自L-Galaxies模拟（Araya-Araya et al., 2025a）的远红外明亮（\(S_{870\mu m}\) \(>\) 1mJy）在\(z\) = 1 – 5的星系（蓝色密度）。ALMA – NIRSpec星系的气体相位金属丰度高于同一时期的观测比较样本，但与L-Galaxies的预测相当。

<small>Figure 6 : Gas-phase metallicity, as derived from the [N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) index using the Bian et al. ( 2018 ) strong-line calibrations, as a function of stellar mass for the ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies. Sources with S/N \( ii ] 6584 \(\lambda\) emission-line are shown as limits. The horizontal dashed line indicates solar metallicity (Asplund, 2005 , 12+log(O/H)= 8.66) . We show comparison samples of typical star-forming galaxies at \(z\) \(\sim\) 0 from SDSS (Curti et al., 2020 ) (grey line), the MOSDEF Survey (Sanders et al., 2021 ) at \(z\) \(\sim\) 2.3 (green solid line) and \(z\) \(\sim\) 3.3 (red solid line), and a redshift matched sample of galaxies from the CEERS (Shapley et al., 2023 ) and AURORA Surveys Shapley et al. ( 2025 ) . We further compare to high-redshift observations of DSFGs from KAOSS at \(z\) \(\sim\) 1 – 3 (Birkin, 2022 ; Birkin et al., 2024b ) and Herschel selected sources from Hogan et al. ( 2021 ) at \(z\) \(\sim\) 2.25, as well as far-infrared bright ( \(S_{870\mu m}\) \(>\) 1mJy) at \(z\) = 1 – 5 galaxies (blue density) from the L-Galaxies simulation (Araya-Araya et al., 2025a ) . The ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies have higher gas-phase metallicity than the observational comparison samples at the same epoch, but comparable to predications from L-Galaxies.</small>

#### Figure 8
![Figure 8](https://arxiv.org/html/x12.png)

图8：左图：ALMA – NIRSpec样本的[S ii ]双线发射线比值作为光谱红移的函数，按比恒星形成率（sSFR）着色。信噪比 \( ii ] 发射线的源显示为上限。我们展示了来自CEERS巡天（Shapley et al., 2023）（圆圈）和AURORA巡天（Shapley et al., 2025）（三角形）的典型恒星形成星系比较样本。我们还标明了[S ii ]谱线比对电子密度的敏感区域（黑色虚线）（Kewley et al., 2019b）。ALMA – NIRSpec样本的[S ii ]双线发射线比值略低于来自CEERS和AURORA的质量较低的SFG样本，且与sSFR没有明显依赖关系。右图：使用mappings v5.1光电离代码（Kewley et al., 2019b）推导的[S ii ]电子密度作为光谱红移的函数，ALMA – NIRSpec星系按尘埃质量着色。灰色实线表示来自Abdurro’uf et al.（2024）的恒星形成星系典型演化（\(n_{e}\) \(\propto\) (1+z) 1.2）。ALMA – NIRSpec星系的电子密度与典型恒星形成星系一致，与比恒星形成率或远红外光度没有强相关性。

<small>Figure 8 : Left: [S ii ] doublet emission-line ratio as function of spectroscopic redshift for the ALMA – NIRSpec sample coloured by specific star-formation rate (sSFR). Sources with S/N \( ii ] emission-lines are shown as limits. We show comparison samples of typical star-forming galaxies from the CEERS Survey Shapley et al. ( 2023 ) (circles) and AURORA survey Shapley et al. ( 2025 ) (triangles). We further indicate the sensitivity region (black dashed lines) of the [S ii ] line ratio to the electron density (Kewley et al., 2019b ) . The ALMA – NIRSpec sample exhibits slightly lower [S ii ] doublet emission-line ratios to the lower mass SFGs samples from CEERS and AURORA, with no clear dependence on sSFR. Right: The [S ii ] derived electron density, using the mappings v5.1 photoionisation code (Kewley et al., 2019b ) , as a function of spectroscopic redshift, with the ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies coloured by dust mass. The grey solid line indicates the typical evolution of star-forming galaxies ( \(n_{e}\) \(\propto\) (1+z) 1.2 ) from Abdurro’uf et al. ( 2024 ) . The electron density of the ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies are consistent with typical star-forming galaxies, with no strong correlations with specific star-formation rate or far-infrared luminosity.</small>

#### Figure 9
![Figure 9](https://arxiv.org/html/x13.png)

图9：从O 32强线比推导出的电离参数（\(U\)）作为H \(\alpha\) 恒星形成率面密度的函数。对于ALMA – NIRSpec星系，这代表观测值（未经尘埃校正），而对于CEERS样本，我们显示的是本征值（经尘埃校正）。我们按[S ii ]推导的电子密度对星系着色，并显示来自Reddy et al.（2023）对CEERS巡天的参数拟合，形式为log \({}_{10}(U)\) = (0.378 \(\pm\) 0.021) \(\times\) log 10 (sSFR) \(-\) (2.655 \(\pm\) 0.011)。黑色箭头表示A V = 1的尘埃消光影响。ALMA – NIRSpec星系的观测值（未经尘埃校正）与经尘埃校正的CEERS星系一致，尽管统计数量较少。

<small>Figure 9 : Ionisation parameter ( \(U\) ), as derived from the O 32 strong-line ratio, as a function of H \(\alpha\) star-formation rate surface density. For the ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies this represents the observed (dust-uncorrected) values whilst for the CEERS sample we show the intrsinc (dust-corrected) values. We colour the galaxies by [S ii ] derived electron density and show the parametric fit from Reddy et al. ( 2023 ) for the CEERS survey of the form log \({}_{10}(U)\) = (0.378 \(\pm\) 0.021) \(\times\) log 10 (sSFR) \(-\) (2.655 \(\pm\) 0.011). The black arrow indicates the impact of dust attenuation with A V = 1. The observed (dust-uncorrected) values of the ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies are consistent with dust-corrected CEERS galaxies, although with low number statistics.</small>

#### Figure 1
表1：48个远红外探测到的NIRSpec源的源属性，按红外光度降序排列，如图1所示。对于每个源，我们列出NIRSpec ID（第1列，C1）、ALMA ID（AS2UDS (A2-) 或 A3COSMOS (A3-) 或 ECOGAL (EG-)）（C3）、J2000 赤经（C5）、J2000 赤纬（C6）、NIRSpec光谱红移（C7）、ALMA主波束校正流量（C8）、ALMA波段、ALMA – NIRSpec间距（C10）。NIRSpec ID以JWST项目缩写（DD = DeepDive, RB = Rubies, JD = JADES, GR = George Rieke, GT = GTO, BA = BlueJay）后跟DJA目标ID（objid）给出。DJA光谱文件名包含在表格的在线版本中。没有ALMA ID的源来自相应ALMA档案程序的盲探测星表。被识别为AGN（见第4.2节）的源被高亮显示，其中\(\dagger\)表示宽发射线，\(\ddagger\)表示X射线对应体，\(*\)表示增强的光学谱线比。

<small>Table 1 : The source properties for the 48 far-infrared detected NIRSpec sources, ranked in descending infrared luminosity, as per Figure 1 . For each source we list the NIRSpec ID (Column 1, C1), ALMA ID, either AS2UDS (A2-) or A3COSMOS (A3-) or ECOGAL (EG-) (C3), J2000 R.A (C5), J2000 DEC. (C6), NIRSpec spectroscopic redshift (C7), ALMA primary beam corrected flux (C8), ALMA Band, ALMA – NIRSpec separation (C10). The NIRSpec ID is given as JWST program acronym (DD = DeepDive, RB = Rubies, JD = JADES, GR = George Rieke, GT = GTO, BA = BlueJay) followed by the DJA object-id ( objid ). DJA spectra file names are included in the online version of the table. Sources with no ALMA ID originate from the blind detection catalogue of the respective ALMA archival program. Sources identified as AGN (see Sec. 4.2 ) are highlighted, where \(\dagger\) indicates broad emission lines, \(\ddagger\) indicates an X-ray counterpart and \(*\) highlights elevated optical-line ratios.</small>

### [55] [Searching for Galaxy Cluster-Scale Strong lenses from the DESI Legacy Imaging Surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.11054)
*Zhejian Zhang,Nan Li,Shude Mao,Hu Zou,Zizhao He,Mingxiang Fu,Shenzhe Cui*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (92/100) - 该论文聚焦于星系团尺度强引力透镜搜索，与用户的核心兴趣领域（强引力透镜、暗物质）高度吻合。虽然用户更关注星系-星系强透镜，但星系团透镜是强透镜的重要分支，且论文使用了深度学习方法和DESI巡天数据，与用户兴趣中的‘lens’、‘dark matter’、‘gravitational lensing: strong’等关键词匹配。论文不涉及用户明确要求降权的领域（如恒星物理、纯宇宙学等）。

TL;DR: 使用深度学习从DESI巡天数据中识别星系团引力透镜，通过迭代训练和人工筛选发现了485个高置信度候选体，其中247个是新发现的


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 星系团尺度强引力透镜系统稀少但价值重大，可用于研究暗物质、暗能量及遥远宇宙。大规模巡天提供了扩展透镜样本的机会

Method: 采用基于ResNet-18的深度学习模型，使用模拟透镜图像作为正样本，观测非透镜图像作为负样本进行训练。通过迭代操作增加完整性，将发现的真阳性样本加入训练集多次训练。最后进行人工检查，按强透镜弧的显著性分为A、B、C等级

Result: 从540,432个星系团候选体中发现了485个高置信度引力透镜候选体，质量范围10^13.67-14.97 M⊙，红移范围0.04-0.89。排除先前研究已发现的，得到247个新发现候选体（16个A级、90个B级、141个C级）

Conclusion: 成功建立了星系团引力透镜候选体目录并公开，鼓励后续观测确认并深入研究这些系统

Abstract: Galaxy cluster-scale strong gravitational lensing systems are rare yet valuable tools for investigating the properties of dark matter and dark energy, as well as providing the opportunity to study the distant universe at flux levels and spatial resolutions that would otherwise be unavailable. Large-scale imaging surveys present unprecedented opportunities to expand the sample of cluster lenses. In this study, we adopt a deep learning-based approach to identify cluster lenses from the DESI Legacy Imaging Surveys, utilizing the catalog of galaxy cluster candidates identified by Zou et al. (2021). Our lens-finder employs a ResNet-18 architecture, trained with mock images of cluster lenses as positives and observational images of cluster scale non-lenses as negatives. We do an iterative operation to increase the completeness of our work, namely adding the found true positive samples back to the training set and training again for several times. Human inspection is conducted to further refine the candidates, categorizing them into grades (A, B, C) according to the significance of the strongly lensed arcs. Reviewing all 540,432 objects in Zou's catalog, we discover 485 high-confidence cluster lens candidates with a cluster $M_{500}$ range of $10^{13.67\sim14.97}M_{\odot}$ and a Brightest Central Galaxy (BCG) redshift range of $0.04\sim0.89$. After excluding the lens candidates listed in previous studies, we identify 247 newly discovered cluster lens candidates, including 16 grade A, 90 grade B, and 141 grade C. This catalog of cluster lens candidates is publicly available online, and follow-up observations are encouraged to confirm and conduct thorough investigations of these systems.

Abstract Translation:
星系团尺度的强引力透镜系统是稀有但宝贵的工具，可用于研究暗物质和暗能量的性质，并提供以其他方式无法获得的通量水平和空间分辨率来研究遥远宇宙的机会。大规模成像巡天为扩大星系团透镜样本提供了前所未有的机遇。在本研究中，我们采用基于深度学习的方法，利用Zou等人（2021）识别的星系团候选体目录，从DESI传统成像巡天中识别星系团透镜。我们的透镜查找器采用ResNet-18架构，以星系团透镜的模拟图像为正样本，以星系团尺度非透镜的观测图像为负样本进行训练。我们进行迭代操作以提高工作的完整性，即将找到的真阳性样本添加回训练集并再次训练多次。通过人工检查进一步筛选候选体，根据强透镜弧的显著性将其分为A、B、C三个等级。在审查Zou目录中的所有540,432个天体后，我们发现了485个高置信度的星系团透镜候选体，其星系团$M_{500}$范围为$10^{13.67\sim14.97}M_{\odot}$，最亮中心星系（BCG）红移范围为$0.04\sim0.89$。在排除先前研究中列出的透镜候选体后，我们识别出247个新发现的星系团透镜候选体，包括16个A级、90个B级和141个C级。该星系团透镜候选体目录已在线公开，鼓励进行后续观测以确认并深入研究这些系统。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，成功建立了星系团引力透镜候选体目录并公开，鼓励后续观测确认并深入研究这些系统。

![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/x4.png)

图4：左图：在训练的最后一次迭代中，两种情况下训练集和验证集在200个训练周期上的交叉熵损失。在情况1中，我们采用Adam优化器，批大小为32，学习率为\(3\times 10^{-6}\)，权重衰减为\(1\times 10^{-1}\)。此外，在情况2中，我们使用初始学习率\(1\times 10^{-4}\)，最终学习率\(1\times 10^{-5}\)，权重衰减\(1\times 10^{-2}\)，并采用余弦退火。在周期20和90处的垂直虚线表示我们在两种情况下选择的早停点，即AUC的最高点（情况2），或训练损失变得异常之前的最高AUC（情况1）。中图：同一训练过程中ROC曲线下面积随周期的变化。右图：同一训练过程中AUC的导数随周期的变化。

<small>Figure 4: Left: The cross-entropy loss on the training and validation sets over 200 training epochs with two cases in the final iteration of our training. In Case 1, we adopt Adam optimizer, configured with a batch size of 32, a learning rate of \(3\times 10^{-6}\) , and a weight decay of \(1\times 10^{-1}\) . Moreover, in Case 2, We use a initial learning rate of \(1\times 10^{-4}\) , a final learning rate of \(1\times 10^{-5}\) , a weight decay of \(1\times 10^{-2}\) , with Cosine Annealing. The vertical dashed line at epoch 20 and 90 indicates the early stopping points we selected in the two cases, which is the highest point of the AUC (Case 2), or the highest AUC before the training loss become abnormal (Case 1). Middle: The Area Under the ROC curve as a function of epoch in the same training session. Right: The derivative of AUC as a function of epoch in the same training session.</small>

The middle and right panels shows the Purity and completeness when applying our classifier to the testing set containing the lens candidates from the COOL-LAMPS project.</small>

### [56] [An extreme ram-pressure stripping event in a protocluster at redshift 4.3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18229)
*Dazhi Zhou,Scott C. Chapman,Manuel Aravena,Roger Deane,Anthony H. Gonzalez,Ryley Hill,Nicholas LeVar,Matthew A. Malkan,Adam Muzzin,Nan Zhang,Kedar A. Phadke,Vismaya R. Pillai,Manuel Solimano,Justin S. Spilker,Nikolaus Sulzenauer,Joaquin D. Vieira,David Vizgan,George C. P. Wang,Axel Weiss*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (91/100) - 该论文研究红移4.3原星系团中的冲压剥离事件，直接涉及高红移星系冷气体、环境淬灭和ALMA/JWST观测，与用户对高红移星系动力学、多相气体和强引力透镜的兴趣高度吻合。作者Manuel Aravena是用户核心作者之一，且论文主题与用户Zotero中的'cold gas'、'ALMA'、'JWST'等关键词强匹配。

TL;DR: 利用ALMA和JWST观测，在红移4.30的SPT2349-56原星系团中，发现一个大质量星系C26正经历极端的冲压剥离事件，超过一半的冷气体被剥离，表明在宇宙早期（z>4）环境淬灭已可通过流体动力学机制发生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往认为在早期宇宙（z>2）原星系团中，热气体晕尚未充分发展，环境效应以引力相互作用为主，流体动力学剥离（如冲压剥离）不足以淬灭大质量星系。但近期观测开始显示冲压剥离可能在星系团形成之前就已发生，其是否能在更高红移（z>4）有效淬灭大质量星系仍不清楚。

Method: 对SPT2349-56原星系团中的星系C26进行ALMA和JWST联合观测，分析其冷气体分布与恒星体之间的空间偏移，定量测量被剥离的冷气体比例。

Result: C26星系中超过一半的观测冷气体已被剥离，气体发射峰值与恒星体之间存在约6千秒差距的大尺度偏移，表明该星系正处于剧烈的主动剥离阶段。

Conclusion: 冲压剥离在红移4.3的致密原星系团核心中即可移除大质量星系的大部分冷气体，提供了在z>4时期通过流体动力学途径实现环境淬灭的直接证据，将冲压剥离的有效时间推前至宇宙更早期。

Abstract: In the nearby Universe, the environment plays a crucial role in suppressing star formation in dense regions. In particular, ram-pressure stripping (RPS) is a major mechanism for removing gas from galaxies in clusters, occurring when galaxies travel through a dense hot atmosphere and leave trailing gaseous wakes. By depleting the cold gas reservoir, RPS can drive outside-in quenching and is therefore thought to be an important route for transforming cluster galaxies. At earlier times, however, protoclusters are dynamically young and their hot atmospheres are expected to be immature, so environmental effects are commonly assumed to be dominated by gravitational interactions rather than hydrodynamic stripping. Recent observations have begun to show that RPS can already operate before mature cluster assembly, including extended gas tails in a forming cluster at $z=2.51$ and in a galaxy group at $z=3.06$. These studies demonstrate that hydrodynamic stripping is possible at earlier times, but whether RPS can become sufficient enough to quench massive galaxies at $z>2$ remains unclear. Here we report ALMA and JWST observations of SPT2349$-$56-C26, a massive galaxy experiencing an extreme RPS event in the SPT2349$-$56 protocluster at $z=4.30$. C26 appears to exhibit a particularly severe active-stripping phase: the displaced gas contains more than half of the observed cold-gas reservoir, with the gas-emission peak showing a large 6-kpc offset from the stellar body. These observations show that RPS can remove most of the cold gas from massive galaxies in dense protocluster cores as early as $z=4.3$, providing a direct hydrodynamic pathway for environmental quenching at $z>4$.

Abstract Translation:
在近邻宇宙中，环境在抑制致密区域恒星形成方面起着关键作用。特别是，冲压剥离（RPS）是星系在星系团中运动时穿过致密热大气并留下尾随气体尾迹的主要气体移除机制。通过消耗冷气体储库，RPS可以驱动由外向内淬灭，因此被认为是转变星系团星系的重要途径。然而，在更早的时期，原星系团在动力学上尚不成熟，其热大气预计也不发达，因此环境效应通常被认为以引力相互作用为主，而非流体动力学剥离。最近的观测开始表明，RPS在成熟的星系团形成之前就可以运作，包括在红移2.51的一个形成中星系团和红移3.06的一个星系群中观测到的延伸气体尾迹。这些研究证明流体动力学剥离在更早时期是可能的，但RPS是否足以在红移大于2时淬灭大质量星系仍不清楚。在此，我们报告ALMA和JWST对SPT2349−56原星系团中红移4.30处经历极端RPS事件的大质量星系SPT2349−56-C26的观测。C26似乎表现出一个特别严重的主动剥离阶段：被置换的气体包含超过一半的观测到的冷气体储库，气体发射峰值与恒星主体存在6千秒差距的大偏移。这些观测表明，RPS最早可以在红移4.3时从致密原星系团核心的大质量星系中移除大部分冷气体，为红移大于4时的环境淬灭提供了直接的流体动力学途径。

Conclusion Translation:
冲压剥离在红移4.3的致密原星系团核心中即可移除大质量星系的大部分冷气体，提供了在z>4时期通过流体动力学途径实现环境淬灭的直接证据，将冲压剥离的有效时间推前至宇宙更早期。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/2606.18229v1/x1.png)

图1：SPT2349–56中RPS星系C26的JWST成像。(a) SPT2349–56原星系团核心的红绿蓝图像（蓝色：NIRCam/F200W；绿色：NIRCam/F444W；红色：MIRI/F1000W）。RPS星系C26用红色矩形标出。十字标记原星系团的运动学中心。(b–d) 分别为C26在F200W、F444W和F1000W波段的放大图像。比例尺表示红移z=4.3时的10千秒差距。

<small>Figure 1: JWST imaging of the RPS galaxy C26 in SPT2349 \(–\) 56. (a) Red-green-blue image of the SPT2349 \(–\) 56 protocluster core (blue: NIRCam/F200W; green: NIRCam/F444W; red: MIRI/F1000W). The RPS galaxy C26 is marked by the red rectangle. The cross labels the kinematic center of the protocluster. (b–d) Zoomed images of C26 in F200W, F444W, and F1000W, respectively. Scale bars show 10 kpc at \(z\,{=}\,4.3\) .</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/2606.18229v1/x2.png)

图2：C26中多相星际介质的ALMA成像。(a) NIRCam F200W图像叠加ALMA [C II] 零阶矩等值线，等值线水平为均方根水平的[3, 4.5, 6, 7.5, 9, 10.5, 12, 13.5]倍。(b) ALMA [C II] 一阶矩图，等值线为[-200, -150, -100, -50, 0, 50, 100, 150, 200] km/s。噪声像素根据其对应的通道显著性进行掩蔽（方法）。(c) ALMA 850微米尘埃连续谱等值线叠加在ALMA [C II] 零阶矩图上。棕色等值线为ALMA尘埃连续谱图均方根水平的[2,3,4]倍。(d) ALMA [N II] 205微米零阶矩等值线叠加在ALMA [C II] 零阶矩图上。青色等值线为ALMA [N II] 零阶矩图均方根水平的[2,3,4]倍。

<small>Figure 2: ALMA imaging of the multiphase ISM in C26. (a) NIRCam F200W image with ALMA [C II ] moment-0 contours at [3, 4.5, 6, 7.5, 9, 10.5, 12, 13.5] times the rms level. (b) ALMA [C II ] moment-1 map with contours at [-200, -150, -100, -50, 0, 50, 100, 150, 200] km s -1 . The noisy pixels are masked based on their corresponding channel significance (Methods). (c) ALMA 850- \(\mu\) m dust continuum contours overlaid on the ALMA [C II ] moment-0 map. The brown contours are [2,3,4] times the rms level of the ALMA dust continuum map. (d) ALMA [N II ] 205 \(\mu\) m moment-0 contours overlaid on the ALMA [C II ] moment-0 map. The cyan contours are [2,3,4] times the rms level of the ALMA [N II ] moment-0 map.</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/2606.18229v1/x3.png)

图3：冲压剥离驱动C26走向贫气体状态。C26在M_gas−M_star平面上的位置，与红移z~4.5的主序星系（蓝色）和红移z>2的宁静星系（红色）进行比较[参考文献bethermin2020, Faisst2020, Wang2025, Umehata2025, Scholtz2026, Adscheid2025, DEugenio2026]。蓝色星表示推断的C26剥离前状态，使用整个系统的冷气体质量和头部的恒星质量。橙色星标记RPS期间恒星头部及其剩余冷气体的当前状态。文献关系以蓝色显示星暴星系，红色显示宁静星系[参考文献Dessauges-Zavadsky2020, Tacconi2018, Magdis2021]。虚线表示气体分数为50%。箭头表示推断的C26剥离驱动演化：RPS移除冷气体，同时大部分恒星质量保持不变，将星系从富气体状态转变为贫气体、宁静的系统。

<small>Figure 3: Ram-pressure stripping drives C26 toward a gas-poor state C26 in the \(M_{gas}-M_{\star}\) plane, compared with main-sequence galaxies at \(z\sim 4.5\) (blue) and quiescent galaxies at \(z>2\) (red) [ bethermin2020 , Faisst2020 , Wang2025 , Umehata2025 , Scholtz2026 , Adscheid2025 , DEugenio2026 ] . The blue star represents the inferred pre-stripping state of C26, using the cold-gas mass of the full system and the stellar mass of the head. The orange star marks the current state of the stellar head with its remaining cold gas during RPS. Literature relations are shown in blue for star-forming galaxies and in red for quiescent galaxies [ Dessauges-Zavadsky2020 , Tacconi2018 , Magdis2021 ] . The dotted line shows a gas fraction of 50%. The arrow illustrates the stripping-driven evolution inferred for C26: RPS removes cold gas while leaving most of the stellar mass unchanged, moving the galaxy from a gas-rich state toward a gas-poor, quiescent system.</small>

White ellipses show apertures for the component photometry of the head, tail, and knot. Blue contours indicate the segmentation map used to separate the head and tail.</small>

<small>Extended Data Fig. 3: [C II ] spectra of C26 and its components. ALMA [C II ] spectra extracted for the full C26 system (grey), the stellar head (red), and the tail (blue). The dashed lines are the best-fit Gaussian profiles for determining the velocity ranges for velocity-integrated intensity calculations, which are indicated as the shaded regions. The head and tail spectra are extracted using the same component apertures adopted in the photometry analysis. The [C II ] emission is detected in both the head and tail apertures, suggesting that the cold gas extends across the stellar head and the tail.</small>

#### Fig. 4
![Fig. 4](https://arxiv.org/html/2606.18229v1/x7.png)

扩展数据图4：C26中[C II]尾部的位置-速度图。沿主轴提取的C26中ALMA [C II]发射的位置-速度图。颜色尺度显示经主波束校正的强度，黑色等值线表示局部均方根水平的[3, 5, 7, 9, 11, 13]倍。[C II]发射在运动学上从恒星头部连接到下游结，支持头部、尾部和结属于同一气体结构的解释。该图还显示了下游多个气体组分的证据。

<small>Extended Data Fig. 4: Position–velocity diagram of the [C II ] tail in C26 Position–velocity diagram of the ALMA [C II ] emission in C26, extracted along the major axis. The color scale shows the primary-beam-corrected intensity, and black contours indicate [3, 5, 7, 9, 11, 13] times the local rms. The [C II ] emission remains kinematically connected from the stellar head to the downstream knot, supporting the interpretation that the head, tail, and knot belong to the same gaseous structure. The diagram also shows evidence for multiple downstream gaseous components.</small>

![Fig. 5](https://arxiv.org/html/2606.18229v1/x8.png)

<small>Extended Data Fig. 5: [N II ] spectra of the northern and southern tail components. The dashed lines are the best-fit Gaussian profiles for determining the velocity ranges for velocity-integrated intensity calculations, which are indicated as the shaded regions.</small>

### [57] [The Early Maturity of High-Redshift Galaxies: Insights from sSFR, M/L and SFHs at z~7-14](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09139)
*P. Santini,M. Castellano,A. Calabrò,A. Fontana,E. Merlin,D. Bevacqua,P. Bergamini,S. Cantarella,L. Ciesla,A. Ferrara,S. L. Finkelstein,F. Fortuni,G. Gandolfi,T. Gasparetto,E. Giallongo,N. A. Grogin,S. T. Guida,A. M. Koekemoer,N. Menci,L. Napolitano,D. Paris,L. Pentericci,B. Perez-Diaz,B. Stoyanova,T. Treu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (90/100) - 论文聚焦JWST高红移星系（z~7-14）的恒星形成历史与sSFR演化，与用户Zotero库中JWST、高红移星系、恒星形成率等核心主题高度吻合；作者列表包含用户核心作者T. Treu、A. M. Koekemoer、A. Ferrara、S. L. Finkelstein，匹配度极高；方法上使用非参数SFH模型分析星系性质，与用户关注的恒星形成、尘埃、暗物质等方向紧密相关。

TL;DR: JWST观测发现z>10处存在意外多的UV亮星系，通过分析2420个z~7-14的星系样本，发现特定恒星形成率(sSFR)和质量-光度比(M/L)在红移范围内基本恒定，与多数理论模型存在矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST观测到z>10处存在超出预期的UV亮星系，理解这些高红移系统的物理特性和恒星形成历史对于区分不同理论模型至关重要。

Method: 从ASTRODEEP-JWST数据集中选取2420个z~7-14的可靠候选星系，使用非参数恒星形成历史模型分析其特定恒星形成率(sSFR)和恒星种群特性。

Result: 发现sSFR和M/L中值在探测的红移范围内基本恒定；样本显示广泛的物理条件和星系类型，包括z~10处已演化的星系；最高M/L星系在观测前至少500Myr形成大部分恒星；z>11星系通过随机恒星形成历史形成，早期保持UV暗，近期经历主要增长。

Conclusion: 观测到的sSFR演化与多数理论模型存在矛盾，成为区分竞争模型的关键参数；缺乏观测到的高sSFR系统表明任何无尘埃星暴阶段必须是短暂的；星系形成历史呈现多样性，包括早期演化和近期增长两种模式。

Abstract: The James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) has revealed an unexpected excess of UV-bright galaxies at z>10, unaccounted for by extrapolations from pre-JWST observations and theoretical models. Understanding the physical properties and star formation histories (SFH) of high redshift systems is key to distinguish between the different proposed scenarios. We identify and analyse a sample of 2420 robust candidates at z~7-14 drawn from the ASTRODEEP-JWST dataset over ~0.2 deg^2 and model their properties with non-parametric SFHs to derive their specific star formation rate (sSFR) and stellar population properties. We find that the median sSFR and M/L remain roughly constant across the probed redshift range. We show that this result is robust against potential systematics unless a hidden population of dust-enshrouded starbursts, undetectable in current data, exists at these redshifts. In any case, the absence of observed high-sSFR systems at the highest redshifts suggests that any dust-free starburst phase must be short-lived. The observed sSFR evolution is in tension with most (though not all) theoretical models, making it a key quantity for discriminating among competing scenarios. The sample shows a wide range of physical conditions and galaxy classes, including systems with low sSFR and high mass-to-light ratios (M/L) up to z~10, indicative of already evolved galaxies only a few hundred Myr after the Big Bang, and different degrees of dust attenuation. We finally attempt to reconstruct the assembly histories of two sub-samples: a) the highest-M/L galaxies at z~7-8, which appear to have formed the bulk of their stars at least 500 Myr before observation, implying progenitors observable as UV-bright sources at z>20, and b) z>11 galaxies, which formed through stochastic SFH, remaining UV-faint for most of their early evolution, before undergoing recent (~50 Myr old) episodes of major growth.

Abstract Translation:
詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜（JWST）在红移z>10处发现了出乎意料的大量紫外明亮星系，这是基于JWST之前的观测外推和理论模型所未能预见的。理解高红移系统的物理性质和恒星形成历史（SFH）是区分不同提出方案的关键。我们从ASTRODEEP-JWST数据集中识别并分析了约0.2平方度范围内z~7-14的2420个稳健候选体，并使用非参数化SFH对其性质进行建模，以推导其比恒星形成率（sSFR）和星族性质。我们发现，中位sSFR和质光比（M/L）在探测的红移范围内大致保持恒定。我们表明，除非在这些红移处存在当前数据无法探测的隐藏尘埃包裹星暴群，否则这一结果对潜在系统误差是稳健的。无论如何，在最高红移处缺乏观测到的高sSFR系统表明，任何无尘埃星暴阶段都必须是短暂的。观测到的sSFR演化与大多数（尽管并非全部）理论模型存在矛盾，使其成为区分竞争方案的关键量。该样本展示了广泛的物理条件和星系类别，包括在z~10处具有低sSFR和高质光比（M/L）的系统，表明这些星系在大爆炸后仅几亿年就已演化，以及不同程度的尘埃消光。我们最终尝试重建两个子样本的组装历史：a) z~7-8处最高M/L的星系，它们似乎在观测前至少5亿年就形成了大部分恒星，这意味着其前体在z>20处可作为紫外明亮源被观测到；b) z>11的星系，它们通过随机SFH形成，在大部分早期演化中保持紫外暗淡，直到经历近期（约5千万年历史）的主要增长阶段。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要的结论：观测到的sSFR演化与多数理论模型存在矛盾，成为区分竞争模型的关键参数；缺乏观测到的高sSFR系统表明任何无尘埃星暴阶段必须是短暂的；星系形成历史呈现多样性，包括早期演化和近期增长两种模式。

### [58] [Probing Infrared eXcess to Investigate Early-Universe Dust (PIXIEDust)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.07964)
*Tom J. L. C. Bakx,Hiddo S. B. Algera,Jean-Baptiste Jolly,Clarke Esmerian,Kirsten Knudsen,Laura Sommovigo,Joris Witstok,Stefano Carniani,Jianhang Chen,Stephen Eales,Andrea Ferrara,Yoshinobu Fudamoto,Masato Hagimoto,Takuya Hashimoto,Hanae Inami,Akio K. Inoue,Theo Khouri,Ikki Mitsuhashi,Gunnar Nyman,Gustav Olander,Stephen Serjeant,Renske Smit,Ilsang Yoon,Jorge Zavala,Susanne Aalto,Caitlin M. Casey,Yoichi Tamura,Wouter Vlemmings*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (90/100) - 论文主题与用户Zotero库高度吻合，聚焦高红移星系尘埃、ALMA观测、早期宇宙尘埃形成等核心兴趣；多位作者（如A. Ferrara, Y. Fudamoto, S. Carniani, J. Chen, S. Serjeant）直接出现在用户核心作者列表中；方法（ALMA/NOEMA深度观测）与用户常用手段一致；结果对尘埃质量上限的约束与用户关注的尘埃、星际介质、恒星形成等主题紧密相关。

TL;DR: 对10个z>8高红移星系进行ALMA和NOEMA观测，未探测到显著尘埃发射，约束了尘埃质量和尘埃-恒星质量比的上限，表明早期宇宙尘埃积累效率低下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管高红移星系中通过红化的紫外发射暗示存在尘埃，但在z>8.3以上的（亚）毫米波段从未探测到尘埃发射。本研究旨在通过深度观测探索早期宇宙中尘埃的存在和性质。

Method: 结合约200小时的ALMA和NOEMA观测数据，对10个z>8星系进行分析。观测深度达到1σ灵敏度：158μm和88μm处2.0μJy，所有数据综合1.5μJy。按红移(8<z<9.5和9.5<z<15)、紫外连续谱斜率(βUV≶-2)和恒星质量(log10M*/M⊙≶9)进行分箱分析。

Result: 未探测到显著尘埃发射，约束平均尘埃质量在3σ置信度下低于10^5 M⊙，尘埃-恒星质量比低于3.7×10^-4（假设Tdust=50K，βdust=2.0）。分箱分析得到类似严格约束。

Conclusion: 结合其他研究，结果表明z>8宇宙中尘埃积累效率低下，可能原因包括超新星产生效率低、星际尘埃生长受限和/或外流导致的尘埃抛射。研究提供了在线数据和工具以促进高红移尘埃搜索。

Abstract: Despite the implied presence of dust through reddened UV emission in high-redshift galaxies, no dust emission has been detected in the (sub)millimetre regime beyond $z > 8.3$. This study combines around two hundred hours of Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array (ALMA) and Northern Extended Millimeter Array (NOEMA) observations on ten $z > 8$ galaxies, revealing no significant dust emission down to a $1 σ$ depth of $2.0$, $2.0$, and $1.5 \,μ$Jy at rest-frame 158, 88 $μ$m, and across all the data, respectively. This constrains average dust masses to be below $< 10^{5}$ M$_{\odot}$ at $3 σ$ and dust-to-stellar mass ratios to be below $3.7 \times{} 10^{-4}$ (assuming $T_{\rm dust} = 50$ K and $β_{\rm dust} = 2.0$). Binning by redshift ($8 < z < 9.5$ and $9.5 < z < 15$), UV-continuum slope ($β_{\rm UV} \lessgtr -2$) and stellar mass ($\log_{10} M_{\ast}/{\rm M_{\odot}} \lessgtr 9$) yields similarly stringent constraints. Combined with other studies, these results are consistent with inefficient dust build-up in the $z > 8$ Universe, likely due to inefficient supernova production, limited interstellar grain growth and/or ejection by outflows. We provide data and tools online to facilitate community-wide high-redshift dust searches.

Abstract Translation:
尽管高红移星系中紫外发射的变红暗示了尘埃的存在，但在红移z > 8.3以上的（亚）毫米波段尚未探测到尘埃发射。本研究结合了阿塔卡马大型毫米/亚毫米阵列（ALMA）和北方扩展毫米阵列（NOEMA）对十个z > 8星系的约两百小时观测，在静止框架158微米、88微米以及所有数据中，分别未探测到显著的尘埃发射，1σ深度分别为2.0、2.0和1.5微央斯基。这限制了平均尘埃质量在3σ水平上低于10^5太阳质量，尘埃与恒星质量比低于3.7×10^{-4}（假设尘埃温度T_dust = 50 K，尘埃发射率指数β_dust = 2.0）。按红移（8 < z < 9.5和9.5 < z < 15）、紫外连续谱斜率（β_UV ≶ -2）和恒星质量（log10 M_*/M_⊙ ≶ 9）进行分箱分析，也得出了同样严格的限制。结合其他研究，这些结果与z > 8宇宙中尘埃积累效率低下的情况一致，可能原因包括超新星产生效率低、星际尘埃生长受限和/或外流导致的尘埃抛射。我们在线提供数据和工具，以促进社区范围内的高红移尘埃搜索。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要的总结：结合其他研究，结果表明z>8宇宙中尘埃积累效率低下，可能原因包括超新星产生效率低、星际尘埃生长受限和/或外流导致的尘埃抛射。研究提供了在线数据和工具以促进高红移尘埃搜索。

### [59] [Spatially Resolved Physical Properties of Young Star Clusters and Star-forming Clumps in the Brightest z>6 Galaxy, the Strongly Lensed Cosmic Spear at z=6.2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08054)
*Abdurro'uf,Dan Coe,Tom Resseguier,Calla Murphy,Xinfeng Xu,Angela Adamo,Namrata Roy,Alaina Henry,Vasily Kokorev,Gabriel Brammer,Seiji Fujimoto,Henry C. Ferguson,Amanda Pagul,Rogier A. Windhorst,Timothy Heckman,Jose M. Diego,Hollis B. Akins,Joseph Allingham,Ricardo O. Amorín,Danielle A. Berg,Maruša Bradač,Larry D. Bradley,Wenlei Chen,John Chisholm,Christopher J. Conselice,Pratika Dayal,Miroslava Dessauges-Zavadsky,Andreas L. Faisst,Steven L. Finkelstein,Yoshinobu Fudamoto,Lukas J. Furtak,Yuichi Harikane,Tiger Yu-Yang Hsiao,Yolanda Jimenez-Teja,Anton M. Koekemoer,Rebecca L. Larson,Ray A. Lucas,Matteo Messa,Lamiya Mowla,Minami Nakane,Gaël Noirot,Richard Pan,Massimo Pascale,Johan Richard,Massimo Ricotti,Luke Robbins,Daniel Schaerer,Fengwu Sun,Eros Vanzella,Brian Welch,Chris Willott,Adi Zitrin*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (89/100) - 论文聚焦于强引力透镜星系中极端致密星团的空间分辨研究，与用户Zotero库中强引力透镜、JWST、高红移星团、恒星形成等核心主题高度吻合。多位核心作者（Seiji Fujimoto, Yoshinobu Fudamoto, Christopher J. Conselice, Gabriel Brammer, Miroslava Dessauges-Zavadsky, Anton M. Koekemoer）直接参与，方法（JWST NIRCam/NIRSpec IFU空间分辨分析）和科学问题（早期宇宙恒星形成、星团形成机制）与用户兴趣高度一致。

TL;DR: JWST观测揭示了一个z=6.2的强引力透镜星系MACS0308-zD1（"宇宙之矛"）中的极端致密星团，这些星团半径约5pc，质量10^6-10^7太阳质量，表面密度超过10^4太阳质量/平方pc，年龄仅5-9百万年，但已形成引力束缚系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究早期宇宙（z>6）中星系的恒星形成过程，特别是通过JWST的高分辨率观测来探索高红移星系中的极端致密星团形成机制，这些星团比本地星团更致密、质量更大。

Method: 使用JWST的NIRCam成像和NIRSpec IFU光谱仪进行观测，覆盖了从紫外到光学波段的静止框架。利用引力透镜效应放大和解析星系结构，对星团进行空间分辨分析，测量其有效半径、恒星质量、表面密度和年龄等参数。

Result: 发现了三个极端致密的年轻星团（Reff~5pc，M*~10^6-10^7太阳质量，Σ*>10^4太阳质量/平方pc），年龄仅5-9百万年但已形成引力束缚系统。最亮星团的核心区域显示出被抑制的电离光子产生效率，可能表明存在反馈驱动的LyC逃逸通道。

Conclusion: 早期宇宙中存在比本地星团更致密、质量更大的极端致密星团，这些星团在很年轻时就能形成引力束缚系统。中心区域的电离光子产生效率抑制可能暗示着反馈机制促进了LyC光子的逃逸，这对理解早期宇宙的再电离过程具有重要意义。

Abstract: We present spatially resolved analysis of stellar populations in the brightest $z>6$ galaxy known to date (AB mag 23), the strongly lensed MACS0308$-$zD1 (dubbed the ``Cosmic Spear'') at $z_{\rm spec}=6.2$. New JWST NIRCam imaging and high-resolution NIRSpec IFU spectroscopy span the rest-frame ultraviolet to optical. The NIRCam imaging reveals bright star-forming clumps and a tail consisting of three distinct, extremely compact star clusters that are multiply-imaged by gravitational lensing. The star clusters have effective radii of $R_{\rm{eff}} \sim 5$ pc, stellar masses of $M_{*} \sim 10^{6}-10^{7}\,M_{\odot}$, and high stellar mass surface densities of $Σ_{*} > 10^{4}\,M_{\odot}~\rm{pc}^{-2}$. While their stellar populations are very young ($\sim 5-9$ Myr), their dynamical ages exceed unity, consistent with the clusters being gravitationally bound systems. Placing the star clusters in the size vs.~stellar mass density plane, we find they occupy a region similar to other high-redshift star clusters within galaxies observed recently with JWST, being significantly more massive and denser than local star clusters. Spatially resolved analysis of the brightest clump reveals a compact, intensely star-forming core. The ionizing photon production efficiency ($ξ_{\rm{ion}}$) is slightly suppressed in this central region, potentially indicating a locally elevated Lyman continuum escape fraction facilitated by feedback-driven channels.

Abstract Translation:
我们展示了已知最亮的z>6星系（AB星等23），即强引力透镜星系MACS0308-zD1（称为“宇宙之矛”，光谱红移z=6.2）中恒星族群的 spatially resolved 分析。新的JWST NIRCam成像和高分辨率NIRSpec IFU光谱覆盖了从紫外到光学的静止系波段。NIRCam成像揭示了明亮的恒星形成团块和一个由三个截然不同、极其致密的星团组成的尾状结构，这些星团因引力透镜效应而成像。这些星团的有效半径约为5秒差距，恒星质量约为10^6至10^7太阳质量，恒星质量面密度超过10^4太阳质量每平方秒差距。尽管它们的恒星族群非常年轻（约5-9百万年），但它们的动力学年龄超过1，这与星团是引力束缚系统一致。将这些星团置于大小与恒星质量面密度的平面中，我们发现它们占据了与最近JWST观测到的其他高红移星系中星团相似的区域，比本地星团显著更大质量和更致密。对最亮团块的 spatially resolved 分析揭示了一个致密、强烈恒星形成的核心。该中心区域的电离光子产生效率略有抑制，可能表明由反馈驱动的通道促进了局部莱曼连续谱逃逸分数。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，早期宇宙中存在比本地星团更致密、质量更大的极端致密星团，这些星团在很年轻时就能形成引力束缚系统。中心区域的电离光子产生效率抑制可能暗示着反馈机制促进了LyC光子的逃逸，这对理解早期宇宙的再电离过程具有重要意义。

#### Figure 1

图1：宇宙之矛（红移z=6.2）的NIRCam彩色图像（红色：F277W+F356W，绿色：F150W+F200W，蓝色：F090W+F115W），背景为红移z=0.356的星系团MACS J0308+2645。强透镜星系（右侧两图所示）分解为两个主要成分：一对大而明亮的恒星形成团块（1和2），以及一个包含三个不同星团（3、4和5）的弧，这些星团被多重成像为七个源（3a、3b、3c、4a、4b、5a和5b）。左上角插图为透镜模型识别出的对应像，显示团块形态，具有三个不同的子结构（下限）。红线表示红移z=6.2的透镜临界曲线，白线显示恒定放大率等高线。

<small>Figure 1: NIRCam color image (red: F277W+F356W, green: F150W+F200W, and blue: F090W+F115W) of the Cosmic Spear, at z = 6.2 z=6.2 , in the background of galaxy cluster MACS J0308+2645 at z = 0.356 z=0.356 . The strongly-lensed galaxy (shown in the two right panels) is resolved into two main components: a pair of large, bright star-forming clumps (1 and 2), and an arc containing three distinct star clusters (3, 4, and 5) which are multiply imaged into seven sources (3a, 3b, 3c, 4a, 4b, 5a, and 5b). The top-left corner inset shows a counter-image identified from the lens model. It reveals a clumpy morphology, with three distinct substructures (lower limit). The red line represents a lensing critical curve at z = 6.2 z=6.2 , while the white lines show contours of constant magnifications.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/galfit_result_venusimg_new_1.png)

图2：使用GALFIT对十一个NIRCam滤光片进行形态建模的结果。在建模中，星系被分解为十个成分：弧下宿主星系的弥散光（即尾状结构）、两个明亮团块，以及与星团多重像相关的七个致密源。在残差图像中，红色、白色和蓝色分别表示正值、零值和负值。约化卡方值显示在残差图的右下角。

<small>Figure 2: Results of morphological modeling using GALFIT applied to eleven NIRCam filters. In the modeling, the galaxy is decomposed into ten components: the diffuse light of the host galaxy underlying the arc (i.e., tail), two bright clumps, and seven compact sources associated with the multiple images of the star clusters. In the residual images, red, white, and blue colors are for positive, zero, and negative values, respectively. The reduced chi-square ( χ ν 2 \chi_{\nu}^{2} ) values are shown in the bottom-right corner of the residual maps.</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/plot_datacube_nirspec_nircam.png)

图3：使用piXedfit结合NIRCam成像和NIRSpec IFU数据构建的光谱光度数据立方体。该数据立方体用于团块的 spatially resolved SED拟合。为创建数据立方体，数据集通过PSF匹配在空间和光谱上对齐至NIRSpec G395H/F290LP数据最长波长网格的空间分辨率，重采样至0.1角秒的像素尺度，并调整光谱与测光之间的归一化以确保一致性。左上图显示[OIII] λ5007图，由NIRSpec IFU数据在发射线波长中心窄波段（100埃）上积分光谱得到。其余图显示空间对齐和PSF匹配至NIRSpec IFU分辨率后的NIRCam图像。IFU的视场在左上图中可见，并在其他图中由白色方框标出。

<small>Figure 3: Spectrophotometric data cube constructed by combining NIRCam imaging and NIRSpec IFU data using piXedfit . This data cube is used for spatially resolved SED fitting of the clumps. To create the data cube, the datasets were spatially and spectrally aligned through PSF matching to the spatial resolution of the longest-wavelength grid of the NIRSpec G395H/F290LP data, resampling to a pixel scale of 0 ​ . ′ ′ ​ 1 0\farcs 1 , and aligning normalization between the spectra and the photometry for consistency. The top-left panel displays the [OIII] λ ​ 5007 \lambda\,5007 map, derived from the NIRSpec IFU data by integrating the spectra accross a narrow ( 100 ​ Å 100\,\AA ) wavelength grids centered at the emission line wavelength. The remaining panels show the NIRCam images following spatial alignment and PSF matching to the NIRSpec IFU resolution. The IFU’s FoV is apparent in the top-left panel and is outlined by the white box in the rest of the panels.</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/plot_sed_bagpipes_clump1_cont1.png)

图4：使用bagpipes对团块、星团（使用堆叠测光）和对应像进行SED拟合的结果。星团（3、4和5）的SED来自其多重像测光的堆叠。在每个图中，观测测光以绿色圆圈显示。最佳拟合模型以蓝色方块（测光）和黑色线（光谱）表示。

<small>Figure 4: Results of the SED fitting for the clumps, star clusters (using stacked photometry), and the counter-image, performed with bagpipes . The SED of the star clusters (3, 4, and 5) are obtained from stacking the photometry of their multiple images. In each panel, the observed photometry is shown as green circles. The best-fit model is represented by the blue squares (photometry) and the black line (spectrum).</small>

Georgiev et al., 2009 ) . For the clumps in the Cosmic Grapes, we only show ones that are gravitationally bound and have an effective radius smaller than 70 70 pc.</small>

### [60] [VENUS: an ultra-faint galaxy hosting the metal-poor type II supernova at $z=5.13$ Witnessing the initial metal enrichment with extremely frequent core-collapse supernovae?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14355)
*Yoshihisa Asada,Seiji Fujimoto,Joseph F. V. Allingham,David A. Coulter,Conor Larison,Matthew R. Siebert,Gabriel Brammer,Dan Coe,Pratika Dayal,Qinyue Fei,Lukas J. Furtak,Vasily Kokorev,Keiichi Maeda,Richard Pan,Johan Richard,Fengwu Sun,Abdurro'uf,Jacqueline Antwi-Danso,Franz E. Bauer,Marusa Bradac,Larry D. Bradley,Volker Bromm,John Chisholm,Christopher J. Conselice,Christa DeCoursey,Anderas L. Faisst,Brenda Frye,Mauro Gonzalez-Otero,Yuichi Harikane,Tiger Y. Y. Hsiao,Kohei Inayoshi,Yolanda Jimenez-Teja,Anton M. Koekemoer,Kotaro Kohno,Paulo A. A. Lopes,Ray A. Lucas,Georgios E. Magdis,Vladan Markov,Nicholas Martis,Jorryt Matthee,Minami Nakane,Rohan P. Naidu,Gael Noirot,Masami Ouchi,Armin Rest,Massimo Ricotti,Louis-Gregory Strolger,Raffaella Schneider,Francesco Valentino,Eros Vanzella,Hayley Williams,Rogier A. Windhorst,Adi Zitrin*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文利用引力透镜效应研究高红移（z=5.13）超新星宿主星系，涉及强引力透镜、高红移星系物理、早期化学增丰等主题，与用户兴趣画像高度吻合。论文作者中包含多位用户核心作者（如Seiji Fujimoto、Kohei Inayoshi、Anton M. Koekemoer、Georgios E. Magdis），且关键词匹配“lensed”、“lensing”、“jwst”。虽然论文主要聚焦超新星而非直接研究星系动力学或分子气体，但其对高红移贫金属环境的研究与用户对高红移星系物理的兴趣高度相关。

TL;DR: 本文首次表征了红移z=5.13的IIP型超新星Eos及其引力透镜主星系，发现该星系是一个极端贫金属（<1%太阳丰度）的紫外超暗Lyman-α发射体，SN Eos的发现表明高红移贫金属环境中超新星发生率可能显著更高，并可能解释JWST巡天中频繁发现的"无宿主"超新星现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对高红移（z=5.13）超新星Eos的宿主星系进行首次表征，以理解早期宇宙中超新星爆发环境及其对星系化学增丰的贡献。

Method: 利用引力透镜效应（总放大率μ~53）对SN Eos及其宿主星系进行高分辨率空间解析，定位核塌缩超新星位置并表征其局域环境；通过光谱观测分析宿主星系的紫外光度、Lyman-α发射线等值宽度、[O III]与Hα谱线强度等特征。

Result: 宿主星系为紫外超暗（M_UV=-14.4±0.3 mag）的Lyman-α发射体，具有高等值宽度但[O III]谱线极弱（[O III]5007/Hβ<0.7），表明气体相金属丰度极低（<1%太阳丰度）。

Conclusion: SN Eos标志着极端贫金属环境中金属贫乏恒星的形成与爆发，推动了宿主星系的早期化学增丰；高红移贫金属环境中超新星发生率可能更高，暗示恒星初始质量函数或大质量恒星爆炸性可能依赖金属丰度，或致密星团中存在 runaway 恒星碰撞；此类超亮星系可作为JWST巡天中"无宿主"超新星的代表性起源。

Abstract: We present the first characterization of the host galaxy of a recently discovered type IIP SN at $z=5.13$ (SN Eos). SN Eos and its host galaxy are gravitationally lensed and multiply imaged. The total magnification $μ\sim53$ enables spatially resolving the system, allowing us to localize the core-collapse supernova (CCSN) position and to characterize its local environment within an early galaxy. Our observation reveals that the host is an ultra-faint ($M_{\rm UV}=-14.4\pm0.3$ mag) Lyman-$α$ emitter with a very high equivalent width. The host galaxy also shows very weak [O iii]4959,5007 lines despite an H$α$ line detection ([O iii]5007/H$β<0.7$ with case B recombination). Assuming that the weak [O iii] is due to low gas-phase metallicity given the low-metallicity of SN Eos itself, SN Eos plausibly marks the formation and explosion of a metal-poor star in an extremely metal-poor environment ($<1\ \%\ Z_\odot$), facilitating the initial stages of the chemical enrichment of the host. Finding the CCSN in such an ultra-faint galaxy at $z=5.13$ also indicates that the SN rate could be considerably higher in high-$z$, metal-poor environments, potentially implying e.g., a $Z$-dependent IMF, $Z$-dependent massive star explodability, or runaway stellar collisions in dense star clusters. Without lensing, only SN Eos would be detectable and the host would be below the detection limit in any NIRCam surveys ever performed. The Eos host galaxy can thus be representative of the origin of {\it hostless} supernovae frequently found in JWST blank field surveys.

Abstract Translation:
我们首次描述了最近在红移z=5.13处发现的IIP型超新星（SN Eos）的宿主星系。SN Eos及其宿主星系受到引力透镜效应并产生多重成像。总放大率μ~53使我们能够对该系统进行空间分辨，从而定位核坍缩超新星（CCSN）的位置，并表征其在早期星系内的局部环境。我们的观测揭示，该宿主是一个极暗弱（M_UV=-14.4±0.3 mag）的莱曼α发射体，具有非常高的等值宽度。尽管探测到了Hα线，但宿主星系的[O III]4959,5007线非常弱（在B型复合条件下[O III]5007/Hβ<0.7）。假设弱的[O III]是由于低气体相金属丰度（与SN Eos本身的低金属丰度一致），那么SN Eos很可能标志着在极端贫金属环境（<1% Z_⊙）中一颗贫金属恒星的形成与爆发，从而推动了宿主星系化学增丰的初始阶段。在红移z=5.13的极暗弱星系中发现CCSN也表明，在高红移、贫金属环境中，超新星发生率可能相当高，这可能暗示例如依赖于金属丰度的初始质量函数、依赖于金属丰度的大质量恒星可爆炸性，或致密星团中的逃逸恒星碰撞。如果没有引力透镜效应，只有SN Eos本身可被探测到，而宿主星系将低于任何已进行的NIRCam巡天的探测极限。因此，Eos宿主星系可能代表了JWST空白场巡天中频繁发现的“无宿主”超新星的典型起源。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，SN Eos标志着极端贫金属环境中贫金属恒星的形成与爆发，推动了宿主星系的早期化学增丰；高红移贫金属环境中超新星发生率可能更高，暗示恒星初始质量函数或大质量恒星爆炸性可能依赖金属丰度，或致密星团中存在逃逸恒星碰撞；此类极暗弱星系可作为JWST巡天中“无宿主”超新星的代表性起源。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.14355v1/x1.png)

图1：SN Eos宿主星系的JWST/NIRCam图像。左图：NIRCam RGB图像（蓝色：F115W+F150W，绿色：F200W+F277W，红色：F356W+F444W）。黄色曲线显示了在\(z=5.13\)处的临界线，来自最新的透镜模型（Allingham等人，2026）。SN Eos表现为明亮且红色的双像源。该源总共被五重成像，靠近临界线的两个最高放大率像（像1和像2）被放大\(\mu\sim 27\)倍。NIRSpec后续观测通过DD-9493项目使用S200A1固定狭缝进行，其狭缝位置由白色矩形标出。剪裁图像宽度为\(4.\!^{\prime\prime}0\)。中图：静止系紫外波段（F090W+F115W+F150W）的NIRCam叠加图像。宿主星系在SN Eos的同一位置被微弱探测到。红色圆圈半径为\(r=0.\!^{\prime\prime}07\)。右图：经过点源减除的强静止光学发射线滤光片NIRCam叠加图像。经过点源减除后，可以看到一个透镜弧结构对称地成像在临界线两侧。蓝色等高线显示了VLT/MUSE拍摄的Ly \(\alpha\)线的零阶矩图。Ly \(\alpha\)线发射在空间上偏离了紫外团块和SN Eos的位置，并与透镜弧结构相关联。

<small>Figure 1: JWST /NIRCam images of the SN Eos host galaxy. Left : the NIRCam RGB image (blue: F115W+F150W, green: F200W+F277W, red: F356W+F444W). The critical curve at \(z=5.13\) is shown in yellow, obtained from the latest lens model (Allingham et al. , 2026 ) . SN Eos stands out as the bright and red, doubly-imaged source. The source is quintuply imaged in total, and the highest two magnification images (image 1 and image 2) near the critical line are magnified by \(\mu\sim 27\) . The NIRSpec follow-up observation was taken with the S200A1 fixed-slit via the program DD-9493, and their slit positions are denoted by the white rectangles. The cutout image is \(4.\!^{\prime\prime}0\) wide. Middle : NIRCam stacked image of the rest-frame UV (F090W+F115W+F150W). The host galaxy is marginally detected at the same position of SN Eos . Red circles have a \(r=0.\!^{\prime\prime}07\) radius. Right : NIRCam stacked image of strong rest-optical emission line filters with point-source subtraction. With point-source subtraction, a lensed arc structure can be seen symmetrically imaged across the critical line. The blue contour presents the moment-zero map of the Ly \(\alpha\) line taken with VLT/MUSE. The Ly \(\alpha\) line emission is spatially offset from the position of the UV clump and SN Eos , and associated with the lensed arc structure.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.14355v1/x2.png)

图2：SN Eos及其宿主星系的JWST/NIRSpec PRISM光谱。(A) SN Eos+宿主的完整一维光谱。显示了像1（蓝色）、像2（红色）和复合光谱（黑色）的光谱。所有光谱均已校正引力透镜效应。橙色曲线显示了NIRSpec PRISM分辨率下红移\(z\sim 5\)处暗弱星系的典型星系光谱（Roberts-Borsani等人，2024），已缩放以匹配SN Eos宿主星系的紫外流量水平。(B) 宿主的静止系紫外光谱。尽管SN Eos在静止光学波段（\(\lambda_{rest}\gtrsim 3700\) Å；灰色阴影）比宿主星系更亮，但宿主星系在静止紫外波段被清晰探测到，且在NIRCam观测历元（红色实心圆）和NIRSpec观测历元之间没有时间变化。(C) 复合光谱（黑色；像1+像2）在（静止系）5000 Å附近的NIRSpec光谱建模。该光谱很好地被IIP型超新星成分（具有宽P-cygni H \(\beta\)线和Fe ii 5169吸收的黑体连续谱；蓝色曲线）建模，仅留下宿主[O III]4959,5007线的最小残差（红色实心阶梯）。[O III]线明显弱于按比例缩放的典型星系光谱（橙色曲线）的预测。(D) H \(\alpha\)线轮廓建模。与[O III]不同，H \(\alpha\)线轮廓可以很好地用宿主星系（即窄）H \(\alpha\)贡献加上来自SN Eos的宽P-cyg H \(\alpha\)线来建模。H \(\alpha\)流量大致与按比例缩放的参考光谱（橙色）的预测一致。

<small>Figure 2: JWST /NIRSpec PRISM spectrum of SN Eos + its host galaxy. (A) the full 1D spectrum of SN Eos + host. The spectrum in image 1 (blue), image 2 (red), and the composite spectrum (black) are shown. All spectra are corrected for the gravitational lensing effect. The orange curve shows the typical galaxy spectrum of faint galaxies at \(z\sim 5\) in the NIRSpec PRISM resolution (Roberts-Borsani et al. , 2024 ) , scaled to match the UV flux level of the SN Eos host galaxy. (B) the rest-UV spectrum of the host. Although SN Eos outshines the host galaxy in rest-frame optical ( \(\lambda_{rest}\gtrsim 3700\) Å; gray shaded), the host galaxy is clearly detected in rest UV, with no time variability between the epoch of the NIRCam observation (red filled circle) and the NIRSpec observation. (C) NIRSpec spectral modeling around (rest-frame) 5000 Å of the combined spectrum (black; image 1 + image 2). The spectrum is well modeled with the type IIP SN component (black body continuum with a broad P-cygni H \(\beta\) and the Fe ii 5169 absorption; blue curve), leaving only minimal residual for the host [O iii ]4959,5007 line (red filled step). The [O iii ] line is considerably weaker than the prediction by the scaled typical galaxy spectrum (orange curve). (D) H \(\alpha\) line profile modeling. Unlike [O iii ], the H \(\alpha\) line profile is well modeled with the host galaxy (i.e., narrow) H \(\alpha\) contribution, on top of the broad P-cyg H \(\alpha\) line from the SN Eos . The H \(\alpha\) flux is roughly consistent with the prediction by the scaled reference spectrum (orange).</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.14355v1/x4.png)

图4：SN Eos宿主的背景。(A) Eos宿主作为贫金属星系候选体。在Eos宿主中发现的极低\(R3\)值表明它是极端贫金属星系候选体（CR3: Cai等人2025，AMORE6: Morishita等人2025，LAP1-B: Vanzella等人2023；Nakajima等人2025，LAP2: Vanzella等人2025）的成员。它们的\(R3\)值显著低于透镜场中通常发现的其他暗弱端星系（UNCOVER: Chemerynska等人2024，GLIMPSE-D: Asada等人2026，黑色虚线显示了Korber等人2026给出的经验关系），并且假设\(R3\)-金属丰度转换关系（\(\lesssim 1\ \%Z_{\odot}\)；紫色虚线由Nakajima等人2022的转换给出），它们可能是极端贫金属星系。(B) 迄今发现的红移\(z>1\)处CCSN宿主星系的\(M_{UV}\)-红移\(z\)图。超亮超新星也包含在内。Eos宿主（红色实心星）是光谱确认的高红移CCSN宿主星系（黑色空心星；Cooke等人，2009，2012；Schulze等人，2018）中红移最高且最暗弱的星系宿主。通过NIRCam巡天发现的光度候选CCSN的宿主也一并绘出（细圆圈：DeCoursey等人，2025a，b；Coulter等人，2026a）。黑色虚线是对应于观测星等28星等（无透镜效应）的\(M_{UV}\)的指导线。

<small>Figure 4: Context of the SN Eos host. (A) Eos host as a metal-poor galaxy candidate. The very low \(R3\) value found in the Eos host implies that it is a member of extremely metal-poor galaxy candidates (CR3: Cai et al. 2025 , AMORE6: Morishita et al. 2025 , LAP1-B: Vanzella et al. 2023 ; Nakajima et al. 2025 , LAP2: Vanzella et al. 2025 ). They have considerably lower \(R3\) values than other faint-end galaxies generally found in lensing fields (UNCOVER: Chemerynska et al. 2024 , GLIMPSE-D: Asada et al. 2026 , the black dashed line presents an empirical relation given by Korber et al. 2026 ), and they are potentially extremely metal-poor galaxies assuming an \(R3\) -metallicity conversion ( \(\lesssim 1\ \%Z_{\odot}\) ; purple dashed line given by Nakajima et al. 2022 conversion). (B) \(M_{UV}\) - \(z\) diagram of CCSN-host galaxies at \(z>1\) found so far. Super Luminous SNe are also included. The Eos host (the red filled star) is the faintest galaxy host at the highest redshift among spectroscopically confirmed high- \(z\) CCSN-host galaxies (black open stars; Cooke et al. , 2009 , 2012 ; Schulze et al. , 2018 ) . Hosts of photometric candidates of CCSNe found with NIRCam surveys are also plotted (thin circles DeCoursey et al. , 2025a , b ; Coulter et al. , 2026a ) . The black dashed curve is a guideline of \(M_{UV}\) corresponding to the observed magnitude of 28 mag (without lensing).</small>

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.14355v1/x5.png)

图5：在高红移发现CCSN时，决定宿主\(M_{UV}\)概率分布的四个关键因素。这四个因素的卷积给出了\(P_{host}(M_{UV})\)的形状（图6右图），因此对单位恒星形成率下的CCSN率采用不同的假设（本图中的红色曲线；另见图6左图）会影响\(P_{host}(M_{UV})\)的整体形状。

<small>Figure 5: Four key factors that determine the host \(M_{UV}\) probability distribution when a CCSN is found at high- \(z\) . The convolution of these four gives the shape of \(P_{host}(M_{UV})\) (Figure 6 right), and thus adopting a different assumption on the CCSN rate per unit SFR (red curve in this plot; see also Figure 6 left) affects the overall shape of \(P_{host}(M_{UV})\) .</small>

#### Figure 6
![Figure 6](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.14355v1/x6.png)

图6：在极暗弱星系中发现CCSN的含义。左图：单位恒星形成率下的CCSN率随金属丰度的变化，以太阳金属丰度归一化。Pessi等人（2023）发现，在本地宇宙中，单位恒星形成率下的CCSN率在低金属丰度环境中变得更高，直至\(\sim 10\)% \(Z_{\odot}\)。我们探讨了三种情况来推断更低金属丰度下的超新星率：无金属丰度依赖性（黑色）、Pessi等人（2023）导出的二阶多项式的常数外推（黄色）以及对数线性外推（蓝色）。右图：在红移\(z\sim 5\)处发现CCSN时，宿主星系\(M_{UV}\)的概率分布。概率函数通过卷积Bouwens等人（2022）的紫外光度函数、恒星形成率以及红移\(z\sim 5.0\)处M1931星团场中依赖于\(M_{UV}\)的有效体积（另见图5）计算得到。顶部子面板显示了对应于CCSN率金属丰度依赖性的三种假设的三个概率分布。底部子面板显示了累积概率。

<small>Figure 6: Implication of finding of the CCSN in an ultra-faint galaxy. Left : CCSN rate per unit SFR as a function of the metallicity, normalized at the solar metallicity. Pessi et al. ( 2023 ) found that the CCSN rate per unit SFR becomes higher in low-metallicity environments down to \(\sim 10\) % \(Z_{\odot}\) in the local universe. We explore three cases to infer the SN rate at even lower-metallicity: no metallicity-dependency (black), constant extrapolation of the 2nd order polynomial derived in Pessi et al. ( 2023 ) (yellow), and log-linear extrapolation (blue). Right : the probability distribution of the host-galaxy \(M_{UV}\) when a CCSN is found at \(z\sim 5\) . The probability function is computed by convolving the UV LF by Bouwens et al. ( 2022 ) , star-formation rate, and the \(M_{UV}\) -dependent effective volume in the M1931 cluster field at \(z\sim 5.0\) (see also Figure 5 ). The top sub-panel shows the three probability distributions corresponding to the three assumptions of the CCSN rate’s metallicity-dependency. The bottom sub-panel displays the cumulative probability.</small>

#### Figure 7
![Figure 7](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.14355v1/x7.png)

图7：NIRCam F277W、F300M、F356W、F410M和F444W图像中的点源减除。

<small>Figure 7: Point-source subtractions in NIRCam F277W, F300M, F356W, F410M, and F444W images.</small>

### [61] [How can we finally see the first light? Status and perspective in the search for Population III stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00167)
*Alessandra Venditti,Daniel Schaerer,Erik Zackrisson,Yoshihisa Asada,Harley Katz,Stefania Salvadori,Eros Vanzella,Julian B. Muñoz,Anatole Storck,Andrew J. Bunker,Alessandro Trinca,Dirk Scholte,Fabio Pacucci,Pablo G. Pérez-González,Seiji Fujimoto,Corinne Charbonnel,Roberto Maiolino,Andrea Ferrara,Mauro Giavalisco,Raffaella Schneider,Josephine Baggen,Hakim Atek,Volker Bromm,Karina Caputi,Laure Ciesla,Pratika Dayal,Chiaki Kobayashi,Marco Castellano,Paola Santini*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文综述了寻找第一代恒星（Pop III）的多种观测策略，其中明确包含引力透镜巡天（lensing surveys）和JWST光谱，与用户Zotero画像中的核心关键词'jwst'、'lensing'、'initial mass function'高度匹配。作者列表中包含用户核心作者Seiji Fujimoto和Roberto Maiolino，进一步增强了相关性。虽然论文主题并非直接聚焦于强引力透镜，但引力透镜作为关键观测手段被重点讨论，且论文涉及高红移天体物理，符合用户对高红移研究的偏好。

TL;DR: 本文综述了第一代恒星（Pop III）形成的理论预期、观测策略及未来展望，指出结合JWST光谱、时域搜索、引力透镜、恒星考古和吸收线研究等多手段正在缩小参数空间，迎来Pop III搜寻的“黄金时代”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找第一代恒星是理解早期宇宙恒星形成关键环节的核心科学问题，但目前其初始质量函数、形成位点、反馈机制以及向富金属恒星过渡的时标与拓扑结构仍高度不确定。

Method: 综述了理论模型对Pop III恒星形成的预期，并系统梳理了多种观测策略：近场宇宙学、直接搜寻极贫金属星形成复合体/硬电离谱线特征（高/中红移）、以及追踪至宇宙黎明的Pop III活动信号。

Result: JWST光谱、时域巡天、引力透镜巡天、恒星考古、吸收线研究及改进的模拟正在产生越来越多的观测候选体，收窄了第一代恒星的允许参数空间。

Conclusion: 多手段协同观测与理论模拟的结合正推动Pop III搜寻进入“黄金时代”，有望揭示宇宙第一批恒星的奥秘。

Abstract: Finding the first (Population III or Pop III) stars is one of the fundamental quests of astronomy, aiming to deliver the missing link in how stars form at early cosmic times. Yet their initial mass function, formation sites and feedback remain highly uncertain, as well as the timing and topology of the transition to metal-enriched star formation. The observability of their peculiar spectral features is also debated, due to their short lifetime and faintness. This review summarizes current theoretical expectations for Pop III star formation, and the main observational strategies that have been adopted to constrain their properties across cosmic time, including near-field cosmology studies, direct searches for extremely metal-poor star-forming complexes and/or hard-ionizing spectral signatures at high and intermediate redshifts, and prospects for identifying Pop III activity up to Cosmic Dawn. The combination of JWST spectroscopy, time-domain searches, lensing surveys, stellar archaeology, absorption-line studies, as well as improved simulations, is yielding a growing number of observational candidates and narrowing the allowed parameter space for the first stars, setting the stage for a ``golden era'' of Pop III searches.

Abstract Translation:
寻找第一代（第三族或Pop III）恒星是天文学的基本任务之一，旨在揭示早期宇宙恒星形成过程中缺失的环节。然而，它们的初始质量函数、形成位置和反馈机制，以及向富金属恒星形成过渡的时间和拓扑结构，仍然高度不确定。由于它们寿命短且光度暗淡，其特殊光谱特征的可观测性也存在争议。本综述总结了当前对Pop III恒星形成的理论预期，以及为限制其在整个宇宙时间内的性质而采用的主要观测策略，包括近场宇宙学研究、对高红移和中等红移处极端贫金属恒星形成复合体和/或强电离光谱特征的直接搜索，以及识别直至宇宙黎明时期Pop III活动的可能性。结合JWST光谱学、时域搜索、引力透镜巡天、恒星考古学、吸收线研究以及改进的模拟，正在产生越来越多的观测候选体，并缩小了第一代恒星允许的参数空间，为Pop III搜寻的“黄金时代”奠定了基础。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有总结：多手段协同观测与理论模拟的结合正推动Pop III搜寻进入“黄金时代”，有望揭示宇宙第一批恒星的奥秘。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.00167v1/x1.png)

图1：来自Klessen and Glover (2023)的模拟对Pop III IMF的预测汇编（[1] Wollenberg et al. 2020, [2] Prole et al. 2022, [3] Jaura et al. 2022, [4] Stacy and Bromm 2013, [5] Hirano et al. 2015, [6] Hirano et al. 2014，彩色实线）。包含中心原恒星反馈的模型（例如[3], [5], [6]）平均预测更大的恒星质量。然而，结果也敏感地依赖于所达到的空间分辨率/时间跨度以及数值实现的细节：较低分辨率（例如[4], [5], [6]）和二维模拟（例如[5], [6]）表现出较少的碎裂——可能是由于对内部吸积盘的建模不够详细——而高分辨率三维模拟（例如[1], [2], [3]）仅覆盖了整个吸积历史的一小部分，留下了关于剩余气体储库和现有原恒星最终命运的问题。关于模拟及其比较的更多细节，请参见Klessen and Glover (2023)。尽管质量范围变化很大，但所有这些预测的IMF近似对数平坦，即与典型的Pop II/I恒星（Chabrier 2003，黑色虚线）的标准“底部重型”Chabrier IMF相比，更加“顶部重型”。

<small>Figure 1: Compilation of predictions on the Pop III IMF from simulations ( [1] Wollenberg et al. 2020 , [2] Prole et al. 2022 , [3] Jaura et al. 2022 , [4] Stacy and Bromm 2013 , [5] Hirano et al. 2015 , [6] Hirano et al. 2014 , colored, solid lines ), from Klessen and Glover ( 2023 ) . Models that include stellar feedback from the central proto-star (e.g. [3] , [5] , [6] ) predict larger stellar masses on average. However results also sensitively depend on the spatial resolution/time span achieved, and on details of the numerical implementation: lower-resolution (e.g. [4] , [5] , [6] ) and 2D simulations (e.g. [5] , [6] ) exhibit less fragmentation – possibly due to a less detailed modelling of the inner accretion disk –, while high-resolution, 3D simulations (e.g. [1] , [2] , [3] ) only cover a small fraction of the full accretion history, leaving the question open on the final fate of the remaining gas reservoir and of existing proto-stars. See Klessen and Glover ( 2023 ) for more details on the simulations and their comparison. Despite the large variation in mass range, however, all these predicted IMFs are approximately logarithmically flat, i.e. much more “top-heavy” compared to a standard “bottom-heavy” Chabrier IMF, typical of Pop II/I stars ( Chabrier 2003 , black, dashed line ).</small>

![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.00167v1/figures/CEMPs_PopIII_signature.png)

图2：当考虑来自后续Pop II恒星世代（从黄色到紫色）的递增污染水平时，由Pop III超新星增丰事件（爆炸能量从左到右增加）产生的碳增强（[C/Fe]）与金属丰度（[Fe/H]）的关系，改编自Vanni et al. (2023a)。

<small>Figure 2: Carbon enhancement ([C/Fe]) vs metallicity ([Fe/H]) resulting from Pop III SN enrichment episodes with an increasing explosion energy (from left to right ), when considering an incremental level of contamination from subsequent generations of Pop II stars (from yellow to purple ), adapted from Vanni et al. ( 2023a ) .</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.00167v1/x2.png)

图3：基于(i)在SAGA星表（Suda et al., 2008, 2017）中未检测到单一增丰的PISN后裔（红色等高线），以及(ii)假设J1010+2358恒星（在15000颗极贫金属LAMOST恒星中发现）的PISN起源解释（蓝色/绿色等高线），可以排除具有给定峰值质量和斜率的Pop III IMF的置信水平，该结果源自与宇宙学星系形成模型NEFERTITI预测的统计比较（改编自Koutsouridou et al. 2024b）。蓝色等高线表明，即使在银河系晕中探测到单个PISN后裔，也能对较低特征质量和/或较陡斜率范围内的Pop III IMF施加强约束。

<small>Figure 3: Confidence levels at which a Pop III IMF with given peak mass and slope can be excluded based on (i) the non-detection of mono-enriched PISNe descendants in the SAGA catalog (Suda et al. , 2008 , 2017 ) at \({[Fe/H]} red contours ), and (ii) the assumption of a PISN origin interpretation for the J1010+2358 star, discovered among 15000 very-metal-poor LAMOST stars ( blue/green contours ), derived from a statistical comparison with predictions of the cosmological galaxy formation model NEFERTITI (adapted from Koutsouridou et al. 2024b ). The blue contours demonstrate how detecting even a single PISN descendant in the Galactic halo will enable strong constraints on the Pop III IMF in the regime corresponding to lower characteristic masses and/or steeper slopes.</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.00167v1/x3.png)

图4：来自LAMOST巡天（Zhao et al., 2012）的J1010+2358恒星表面的化学丰度模式，最初由Xing et al. (2023)测量（上/下面板中的黄色方块），以及后来由Skúladóttir et al. (2024)进行的高分辨率观测（红色星号）（改编自Xing et al. 2023和Skúladóttir et al. 2024）。与上面板中\(260~{M_{\odot}}\) PISN模型的一致性未得到新测量的确认。

( 2024 ) ( red stars ) (adapted from Xing et al. 2023 and Skúladóttir et al. 2024 ). The agreement with the top-panel \(260~{M_{\odot}}\) PISN model was not confirmed by the new measures.</small>

![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.00167v1/x4.png)

图5：11个\(z\approx 1.3-7.7\)的恒星形成星系（星形）和两个\(z\approx 4.5\)的候选AGN宿主（圆圈）的Log(O/Ar)与\(12+{Log(Ar/H)}\)的关系，按红移着色。绿色和蓝色线分别显示了低红移（\(z < 0.1\)）星暴星系（Bhattacharya et al., 2025b）的平均值序列，改编自Bhattacharya et al. <small>Figure 5: Log(O/Ar) vs \(12+{Log(Ar/H)}\) for 11 star-forming galaxies at \(z\approx 1.3-7.7\) ( stars ) and two candidate AGN hosts at \(z\approx 4.5\) ( circles ), colored by their redshift. The green and blue lines respectively show the sequence of mean values of low-redshift ( \(z (Bhattacharya et al. , 2025b ) , adopted from Bhattacharya et al. ( 2025a ) . The MW solar neighborhood Galactic chemical evolution (GCE) model from Kobayashi et al. ( 2020 ) is also shown as a reference ( black line ). Four of these objects at \(z\sim 3.5-7.7\) (marked by orange/red edgecolors ) have Log(O/Ar) values below the MW GCE model, and even below the sequence traced by lower-mass, low- \(z\) starbursts, possibly indicative of alternative enrichment scenarios, including a rapid PISN enrichment channel (particularly for the ERO 10612 at \(z=7.66\) , red edgecolor , with a low – albeit uncertain – estimated star-formation timescale of \(4.37^{+4.13}_{-2.13}\) Myr).</small>

![Figure 6](https://arxiv.org/html/2607.00167v1/figures/mass-metallicity+PopIII_candidates.png)

图6：来自Bolamperti et al. (2026)的\(z>3\)处质量-金属丰度关系，包括低质量、恒星形成复合体，其未探测到的金属线表明金属丰度\(\lesssim 8\times 10^{-3}~{Z_{\odot}}\)（LAP2, Vanzella et al. 2026, AMORE6, Morishita et al. 2025; Messa et al. 2026, Hebe Maiolino et al. 2026; Übler et al. 2026和MPG-CR3, Cai et al. 2025，来自表1）。

### [62] [MSA-3D: Rotation Curves and Dark Matter Fractions at z~0.5-1.7 with JWST/NIRSpec](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27853)
*Juan M. Espejo Salcedo,Danail Obreschkow,Karl Glazebrook,Tucker Jones,Ivana Barišić,Natascha M. Förster Schreiber,Takafumi Tsukui,Xin Wang,Mengting Ju,Qianqiao Zhou,Amit Nestor-Schachar,Ryan L. Sanders,Stavros Pastras,Namrata Roy,Alaina Henry,Kyle Westfall,Themiya Nanayakkara,Matthew Malkan,Fahmi M. Al Farisy,Isaac Kanowski*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文利用JWST/NIRSpec对z~0.5-1.7的恒星形成星系进行旋转曲线和暗物质分数测量，直接涉及强引力透镜用户的核心兴趣：高红移星系动力学、暗物质分布、JWST观测。论文作者中包含用户核心作者Natascha M. Förster Schreiber和Stavros Pastras，且方法（正向动力学建模）与用户常用方法高度一致。论文主题与用户Zotero库中的高权重关键词（JWST、暗物质、旋转曲线、恒星形成星系）高度匹配，且属于用户明确优先的高红移星系动力学研究。

TL;DR: 基于JWST/NIRSpec的MSA-3D巡天数据，对30个红移0.5-1.7的恒星形成星系进行旋转曲线和暗物质分布分析，发现23个星系中暗物质分数中位数为0.63，存在旋转曲线上升、平坦、下降三种形态，且恒星Tully-Fisher关系接近局域关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用JWST高分辨率数据，研究高红移（z~1）恒星形成星系的动力学状态和暗物质分布，填补较低恒星质量星系的高红移观测空白，探讨空间分辨率对Tully-Fisher关系测量的影响。

Method: 结合JWST/NIRSpec空间分辨电离气体运动学和JWST/NIRCam成像数据，通过正向动力学建模约束重子和暗物质贡献；使用恒星质量图和SFR导出气体剖面进行一致性检验；进行简化的视宁度退化测试。

Result: 23个星系中，暗物质分数f_DM(Re)范围0.1-0.9，中位数0.63，弥散约0.2 dex；19个延伸至2Re的星系中识别出6个上升、6个平坦、7个下降旋转曲线；恒星Tully-Fisher关系接近局域关系，视宁度退化会使归一化偏移约0.2 dex。

Conclusion: MSA-3D巡天提供了向低质量端扩展的高红移星系动力学样本，证实z~1附近恒星形成盘星系具有广泛的动力学状态和内部质量分布多样性。

Abstract: We present rotation curves and inner mass distributions for 30 star-forming galaxies at $0.5<z<1.7$, observed with JWST/NIRSpec as part of the MSA-3D Cycle 1 survey. Combining spatially resolved ionised-gas kinematics with JWST/NIRCam imaging, we constrain baryonic and dark matter contributions through forward dynamical modelling for galaxies extending down to stellar masses of $\sim10^{9}M_\odot$. For the 23 galaxies in our primary statistical sample, we find predominantly rotationally supported disks with intrinsic dispersions $σ_0\sim31$-65 km s$^{-1}$ and a wide range of dark matter fractions, $f_{DM}(R_e)\sim0.1$-0.9, with a median of 0.63 and substantial galaxy-to-galaxy scatter of $\sim0.2$ dex. These results are supported by a complementary consistency check using stellar mass maps and SFR-derived gas profiles. Among the 19 galaxies reaching $\gtrsim2R_e$, we identify six rising, six flat, and seven falling rotation curves. These classes define an observed ordering from rotationally dominated, dark-matter-rich disks ($V_{rot}/σ_0\approx4$, $f_{DM}\gtrsim0.7$) to more dispersion-supported systems with centrally concentrated baryonic mass distributions ($V_{rot}/σ_0\approx2$, $f_{DM}\lesssim0.55$). The stellar Tully-Fisher relation lies close to the local relation evolved under the adopted self-similar $Λ$CDM scaling. A simplified seeing-degradation test shifts the inferred normalisation by ~0.2 dex at fixed $V_c$, suggesting that spatial resolution contributes to, but does not fully explain, differences among high-redshift Tully-Fisher measurements. Overall, MSA-3D provides a high-resolution extension of previous surveys toward lower stellar masses, spanning $9.0 < \log(M_\star/M_\odot) < 11.2$, and reinforces that star-forming disks near $z\sim1$ span a broad range of dynamical states and inner mass distributions.

Abstract Translation:
我们展示了30个恒星形成星系在$0.5<z<1.7$范围内的旋转曲线和内部质量分布，这些星系作为MSA-3D Cycle 1巡天的一部分，由JWST/NIRSpec观测得到。结合空间分辨的电离气体运动学与JWST/NIRCam成像，我们通过正向动力学建模约束了重子和暗物质贡献，星系恒星质量低至$\sim10^{9}M_\odot$。对于主要统计样本中的23个星系，我们发现它们主要是旋转支持的盘，固有速度弥散$σ_0\sim31$-65 km s$^{-1}$，暗物质分数$f_{DM}(R_e)\sim0.1$-0.9范围广泛，中位数为0.63，星系间弥散约$\sim0.2$ dex。这些结果得到了使用恒星质量图和SFR导出的气体分布进行的补充一致性检验的支持。在达到$\gtrsim2R_e$的19个星系中，我们识别出6个上升型、6个平坦型和7个下降型旋转曲线。这些类别定义了一个从旋转主导、暗物质丰富的盘（$V_{rot}/σ_0\approx4$，$f_{DM}\gtrsim0.7$）到更弥散支持、重子质量分布集中在中心的系统（$V_{rot}/σ_0\approx2$，$f_{DM}\lesssim0.55$）的观测排序。恒星Tully-Fisher关系接近在采用的自相似$Λ$CDM标度下演化的局域关系。一个简化的视宁度退化测试在固定$V_c$下将推断的归一化偏移了约0.2 dex，表明空间分辨率对高红移Tully-Fisher测量差异有贡献，但不能完全解释。总体而言，MSA-3D将先前巡天向更低恒星质量扩展，覆盖$9.0 < \log(M_\star/M_\odot) < 11.2$，并强化了$z\sim1$附近的恒星形成盘星系具有广泛的动力学状态和内部质量分布。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，MSA-3D巡天提供了向低质量端扩展的高红移星系动力学样本，证实z~1附近恒星形成盘星系具有广泛的动力学状态和内部质量分布多样性。

### [63] [Cm-wavelength Studies of Molecular Gas and Star Formation at High Redshift with the SKA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26640)
*Ran Wang,Jeff Wagg,Mark T. Sargent,Manuel Aravena,Mamta Pandey-Pommier,Elisabete da Cunha,Eric Murphy,Dominik Riechers,Jacqueline Hodge*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文聚焦于利用SKA研究高红移星系中的冷分子气体和恒星形成，与用户画像中的高红移星系、分子气体、致密气体等核心主题高度吻合。作者Manuel Aravena是用户的核心作者之一。论文强调SKA对低阶分子谱线的观测能力，直接关联用户对高红移星系动力学和多相气体的研究兴趣。虽然未直接涉及强引力透镜，但主题和方法与用户的主要兴趣领域一致。

TL;DR: 本文强调了SKA在高频段（>15 GHz）观测高红移星系低阶分子谱线的重要性，特别是研究早期宇宙年轻星系中的冷分子气体含量和活跃恒星形成区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着JWST发现越来越多的高红移年轻星系，需要利用SKA的高频观测能力来研究这些早期星系中的冷分子气体，弥补当前观测手段在低阶分子谱线方面的不足。

Method: 通过SKA在高频段（>15 GHz）对红移后的CO、HCN、HCO+等低阶分子跃迁线进行观测，结合现有ALMA和JWST的观测数据，综合分析星系中的冷气体分布与恒星形成活动。

Result: SKA能够探测早期宇宙年轻星系中的冷分子气体含量，并利用CO及多种致密气体示踪物研究活跃恒星形成区域。

Conclusion: SKA超过15 GHz的频率覆盖能力对于研究高红移星系的冷分子气体和恒星形成过程至关重要，是理解早期宇宙星系演化的关键工具。

Abstract: The Square Kilometre Array will be a revolutionary instrument for the study of gas in the distant Universe. At frequencies below ~50 GHz, observations of redshifted emission from low-J transitions of CO, HCN, HCO+, and HNC, etc. provide insight into the kinematics and mass budget of the cold, dense star-forming gas in galaxies. Over the past decade, sensitive imaging using ALMA has detected and resolved the redshifted high-J molecular CO line emission and far-infrared fine structure lines in samples of galaxies over a wide redshift range, shedding light on active star-formation processes at the early epoch of galaxy evolution. In recent years, increasing numbers of young galaxies at high redshift are discovered by JWST, which significantly improved our knowledge of different galaxy populations across cosmic time. In this updated chapter of the SKA science book, we would like to highlight the importance of studies of the low-J molecular lines in high-z galaxies using SKA toward high frequencies, discussing the request of frequency coverage beyond 15 GHz and emphasizing its crucial role in exploring the cold molecular gas content in the young galaxy populations in the early universe and investigating the regions of active-star formation using molecular CO and various dense gas tracers.

Abstract Translation:
平方公里阵列（SKA）将成为研究遥远宇宙中气体的革命性仪器。在低于约50 GHz的频率下，观测来自CO、HCN、HCO+和HNC等分子的低J跃迁的红移发射，可以深入了解星系中冷、致密恒星形成气体的运动学和物质预算。在过去十年中，利用ALMA进行的灵敏成像已经探测并解析了广泛红移范围内星系样本中的红移高J分子CO谱线发射和远红外精细结构谱线，揭示了星系演化早期活跃的恒星形成过程。近年来，JWST发现了越来越多的高红移年轻星系，这显著提高了我们对不同星系种群在整个宇宙时间尺度上的认识。在这份更新的SKA科学书籍章节中，我们希望强调利用SKA在高频方向研究高红移星系中低J分子谱线的重要性，讨论频率覆盖范围超过15 GHz的需求，并强调其在探索早期宇宙年轻星系种群中的冷分子气体含量以及利用分子CO和各种致密气体示踪物研究活跃恒星形成区域方面的关键作用。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要的总结：SKA超过15 GHz的频率覆盖能力对于研究高红移星系的冷分子气体和恒星形成过程至关重要，是理解早期宇宙星系演化的关键工具。

The blue solid, dashed, and dash-dotted lines represent CO J =1-0 transition from galaxies with SFRs of 500 \(M_{\odot}\,yr^{-1}\) , 100 \(M_{\odot}\,yr^{-1}\) , and 20 \(M_{\odot}\,yr^{-1}\) , respectively. The blue vertical bars mark the redshifts of z=2 to 7. The orange and yellow lines shows the peak flux densities of HCN J =1-0 from a galaxy with SFR=500 \(M_{\odot}\,yr^{-1}\) and HCO + J =1-0 with SFR=1000 \(M_{\odot}\,yr^{-1}\) , respectively. The orange and yellow vertical bars marks the redshifts of z=1 to 5. We corrected for CMB effect adopting a kinetic temperature of \(T_{kin}=40K\) (da Cunha et al. , 2013 ) . The black dashed lines show the 3 \(\sigma\) detection limits with on-source integration time of 10, 50, and 500 hours. These are estimated from the rms line sensitivity in SKA Memo 20-01.</small>

### [64] [Little Red Dots on FIRE: Exploring the formation and observational signatures of ultra-compact early galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23683)
*Niranjan Chandra Roy,Daniel Anglés-Alcázar,Rachel K. Cochrane,Alexander J. Richings,Jonathan Mercedes-Feliz,Christopher C. Hayward,Claude-André Faucher-Giguère,Erini Lambrides,Robert Feldmann,Boon Kiat Oh,Andrew Marszewski,Guochao Sun,Kelcey Davis,Jed McKinney,Caitlin M. Casey,Tanio Díaz-Santos,Madisyn Brooks,Grace Farrell*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文研究高红移（z≈4-8）超致密早期星系的形成与观测特征，直接涉及用户核心兴趣中的高红移星系动力学、尘埃、致密气体以及宇宙正午前后的星系演化。论文使用FIRE宇宙学模拟和3D尘埃辐射传输，方法上与用户关注的模拟和观测手段高度吻合。作者列表中包含Caitlin M. Casey、Jed McKinney、Erini Lambrides、Christopher C. Hayward等用户核心作者，且论文主题与用户Zotero库中的“dust”、“dense gas”、“massive main-sequence galaxy”、“cosmic noon”等高频关键词紧密相关。虽然论文未直接聚焦于强引力透镜，但其对高红移致密星系的详细研究（包括尘埃、气体、动力学）与用户的主要研究领域高度互补，且用户明确要求优先考虑高红移星系动力学、多相气体等方向。因此给予五星评分。

TL;DR: 本文利用FIRE宇宙学模拟和3D尘埃辐射传输，发现超致密早期星系（不含AGN）能解释小红点（LRD）的部分观测特征（如强巴尔默跳、UV光谱斜率、尘埃质量等），但无法重现极端的红连续谱、更宽的发射线以及宽巴尔默/窄禁线特征，因此提出恒星+AGN混合模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小红点（LRD）是未知起源的致密源，具有宽巴尔默线、巴尔默跳、异常UV辐射和上升的红连续谱。本文旨在检验超致密早期星系能否在没有AGN的情况下重现LRD的观测特征，以厘清其物理本质。

Method: 采用FIRE宇宙学模拟、3D尘埃辐射传输和合成发射线数据立方体，分析z≈4–8、当前群晕前身中的瞬态超致密星系，并与JWST观测的LRD性质进行对比。

Result: 超致密星系可解释部分LRD特征：强巴尔默跳（~2）、蓝UVβ斜率（~-1.25）、尘埃质量、ALMA未探测、巴尔默线宽达~1500 km/s。但无法解释红连续谱、更极端的巴尔默跳（>2.5）和线宽（>2000 km/s）及宽巴尔默/窄禁线AGN特征。超致密条件同时促进中心黑洞吸积，支持混合模型。

Conclusion: 超致密早期星系（不含AGN）可贡献部分LRD种群，但极端LRD特征需要AGN参与。混合恒星+AGN模型能统一解释LRD的多波段观测特征，超致密星系在z≈4–8的数密度约为2×10⁻⁵ cMpc⁻³。

Abstract: Little Red Dots (LRDs) are compact sources with broad Balmer lines, Balmer breaks, anomalous UV emission, rising red continuum, and uncertain origin. We use FIRE cosmological simulations, 3D dust radiative transfer, and synthetic emission-line data cubes to test whether ultra-compact early galaxies can reproduce LRD-like observables without invoking AGN. In progenitors of present-day group halos ($M_{\rm halo} > 10^{13.5} M_{\odot}$), we identify transient phases at $z \approx 4-8$ lasting $\sim 150-400$ Myr in which strong dissipative inflows build massive ($M_{\star} \sim 10^{8.5}-10^{10.5} M_{\odot}$), UV-bright ($-23 \lesssim M_{\rm UV} \lesssim -20$), ultra-compact ($R_{\rm eff} < 300$ pc) stellar cores with extreme circular velocity ($V_{\rm circ} > 500$ km s$^{-1}$) and consistent with several LRD properties: strong Balmer breaks ($F_ν(4200{\rm Å})/F_ν(3500{\rm Å}) \sim 2$); blue UV beta slopes ($β_{\rm UV} \approx -1.25$); dust masses; ALMA non-detections; and Balmer-line widths up to $\sim 1500$ km s$^{-1}$ broadened by galaxy-scale dynamics. However, stellar emission and host-galaxy kinematics alone do not reproduce the red rest-optical continuum, more extreme Balmer breaks ($\gtrsim 2.5$) and line widths ($\gtrsim 2000$ km s$^{-1}$), or the broad-Balmer/narrow-forbidden-line signature of broad-line AGN. The same ultra-compact conditions efficiently fuel central BHs, suggesting a hybrid stellar+AGN scenario in which compact stars explain the UV continuum, Balmer break, and intermediate line widths while AGN supply the red optical continuum and more extreme line properties. With halo masses $M_{\rm halo} \sim 10^{11-12.5} M_\odot$ and comoving abundance $\sim 2 \times 10^{-5} {\rm cMpc}^{-3}$ (for $\sim 20\%$ duty-cycle at $z \approx 4-8$), ultra-compact galaxies can contribute to the massive, bright LRD population.

Abstract Translation:
小红点（LRDs）是紧凑型源，具有宽巴尔默线、巴尔默跃变、异常紫外发射、上升的红色连续谱以及不确定的起源。我们利用FIRE宇宙学模拟、三维尘埃辐射传输和合成发射线数据立方体，测试超致密早期星系是否能在不涉及活动星系核（AGN）的情况下再现类似LRD的可观测特征。在现今群级暗晕（$M_{\rm halo} > 10^{13.5} M_{\odot}$）的前身中，我们识别出在$z \approx 4-8$期间持续约$\sim 150-400$ Myr的瞬态阶段，其中强烈的耗散内流构建了质量巨大（$M_{\star} \sim 10^{8.5}-10^{10.5} M_{\odot}$）、紫外明亮（$-23 \lesssim M_{\rm UV} \lesssim -20$）、超致密（$R_{\rm eff} < 300$ pc）的恒星核，具有极高的环状速度（$V_{\rm circ} > 500$ km s$^{-1}$），并与LRD的若干性质一致：强巴尔默跃变（$F_ν(4200{\rm Å})/F_ν(3500{\rm Å}) \sim 2$）；蓝色紫外β斜率（$β_{\rm UV} \approx -1.25$）；尘埃质量；ALMA未探测；以及由星系尺度动力学展宽的巴尔默线宽度高达$\sim 1500$ km s$^{-1}$。然而，仅凭恒星辐射和宿主星系运动学无法再现红色静止光学连续谱、更极端的巴尔默跃变（$\gtrsim 2.5$）和线宽（$\gtrsim 2000$ km s$^{-1}$），或宽巴尔默/窄禁线标志的宽线AGN特征。相同的超致密条件有效为中央黑洞提供燃料，暗示一种混合恒星+AGN情景：其中致密恒星解释了紫外连续谱、巴尔默跃变和中等线宽，而AGN则提供红色光学连续谱和更极端的线性质。暗晕质量$M_{\rm halo} \sim 10^{11-12.5} M_\odot$且共动数密度$\sim 2 \times 10^{-5} {\rm cMpc}^{-3}$（在$z \approx 4-8$期间占空比约$\sim 20\%$）的超致密星系，可对质量巨大、明亮的LRD种群做出贡献。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要：超致密早期星系（不含AGN）可贡献部分LRD种群，但极端LRD特征需要AGN参与。混合恒星+AGN模型能统一解释LRD的多波段观测特征，超致密星系在z≈4–8的数密度约为2×10⁻⁵ cMpc⁻³。
